# Berean Standard Bible

## License Information

**Berean Standard Bible** is based on and adapted from: _Berean Standard Bible_, [Berean Standard Bible](https://berean.bible), None, which is licensed under a [Public Domain CC0](https://creativecommons.org/public-domain/cc0/).

This markdown version is provided under the same license.



--------------------------------

## Psalms 1:1 (id: 119001001)

1Blessed is the man who does not walk in the counsel of the wicked, or set foot on the path of sinners, or sit in the seat of mockers.


## Psalms 1:2 (id: 119001002)

2But his delight is in the Law of the LORD, and on His law he meditates day and night.


## Psalms 1:3 (id: 119001003)

3He is like a tree planted by streams of water, yielding its fruit in season, whose leaf does not wither, and who prospers in all he does.


## Psalms 1:4 (id: 119001004)

4Not so the wicked! For they are like chaff driven off by the wind.


## Psalms 1:5 (id: 119001005)

5Therefore the wicked will not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the assembly of the righteous.


## Psalms 1:6 (id: 119001006)

6For the LORD guards the path of the righteous, but the way of the wicked will perish.


## Psalms 2:1 (id: 119002001)

1Why do the nations rage and the peoples plot in vain?


## Psalms 2:2 (id: 119002002)

2The kings of the earth take their stand and the rulers gather together, against the LORD and against His Anointed One:


## Psalms 2:3 (id: 119002003)

3“Let us break Their chains and cast away Their cords.”


## Psalms 2:4 (id: 119002004)

4The One enthroned in heaven laughs; the Lord taunts them.


## Psalms 2:5 (id: 119002005)

5Then He rebukes them in His anger, and terrifies them in His fury:


## Psalms 2:6 (id: 119002006)

6“I have installed My King on Zion, upon My holy mountain.”


## Psalms 2:7 (id: 119002007)

7I will proclaim the decree spoken to Me by the LORD: “You are My Son; today I have become Your Father.


## Psalms 2:8 (id: 119002008)

8Ask Me, and I will make the nations Your inheritance, the ends of the earth Your possession.


## Psalms 2:9 (id: 119002009)

9You will break them with an iron scepter; You will shatter them like pottery.”


## Psalms 2:10 (id: 119002010)

10Therefore be wise, O kings; be admonished, O judges of the earth.


## Psalms 2:11 (id: 119002011)

11Serve the LORD with fear, and rejoice with trembling.


## Psalms 2:12 (id: 119002012)

12Kiss the Son, lest He be angry and you perish in your rebellion, when His wrath ignites in an instant. Blessed are all who take refuge in Him.


## Psalms 3:0 (id: 119003000)

0A Psalm of David, when he fled from his son Absalom.


## Psalms 3:1 (id: 119003001)

1O LORD, how my foes have increased! How many rise up against me!


## Psalms 3:2 (id: 119003002)

2Many say of me, “God will not deliver him.” Selah


## Psalms 3:3 (id: 119003003)

3But You, O LORD, are a shield around me, my glory, and the One who lifts my head.


## Psalms 3:4 (id: 119003004)

4To the LORD I cry aloud, and He answers me from His holy mountain. Selah


## Psalms 3:5 (id: 119003005)

5I lie down and sleep; I wake again, for the LORD sustains me.


## Psalms 3:6 (id: 119003006)

6I will not fear the myriads set against me on every side.


## Psalms 3:7 (id: 119003007)

7Arise, O LORD! Save me, O my God! Strike all my enemies on the jaw; break the teeth of the wicked.


## Psalms 3:8 (id: 119003008)

8Salvation belongs to the LORD; may Your blessing be on Your people. Selah


## Psalms 4:0 (id: 119004000)

0For the choirmaster. With stringed instruments. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 4:1 (id: 119004001)

1Answer me when I call, O God of my righteousness! You have relieved my distress; show me grace and hear my prayer.


## Psalms 4:2 (id: 119004002)

2How long, O men, will my honor be maligned? How long will you love vanity and seek after lies? Selah


## Psalms 4:3 (id: 119004003)

3Know that the LORD has set apart the godly for Himself; the LORD hears when I call to Him.


## Psalms 4:4 (id: 119004004)

4Be angry, yet do not sin; on your bed, search your heart and be still. Selah


## Psalms 4:5 (id: 119004005)

5Offer the sacrifices of the righteous and trust in the LORD.


## Psalms 4:6 (id: 119004006)

6Many ask, “Who can show us the good?” Shine the light of Your face upon us, O LORD.


## Psalms 4:7 (id: 119004007)

7You have filled my heart with more joy than when grain and new wine abound.


## Psalms 4:8 (id: 119004008)

8I will lie down and sleep in peace, for You alone, O LORD, make me dwell in safety.


## Psalms 5:0 (id: 119005000)

0For the choirmaster, to be accompanied by flutes. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 5:1 (id: 119005001)

1Give ear to my words, O LORD; consider my groaning.


## Psalms 5:2 (id: 119005002)

2Attend to the sound of my cry, my King and my God, for to You I pray.


## Psalms 5:3 (id: 119005003)

3In the morning, O LORD, You hear my voice; at daybreak I lay my plea before You and wait in expectation.


## Psalms 5:4 (id: 119005004)

4For You are not a God who delights in wickedness; no evil can dwell with You.


## Psalms 5:5 (id: 119005005)

5The boastful cannot stand in Your presence; You hate all workers of iniquity.


## Psalms 5:6 (id: 119005006)

6You destroy those who tell lies; the LORD abhors the man of bloodshed and deceit.


## Psalms 5:7 (id: 119005007)

7But I will enter Your house by the abundance of Your loving devotion; in reverence I will bow down toward Your holy temple.


## Psalms 5:8 (id: 119005008)

8Lead me, O LORD, in Your righteousness because of my enemies; make straight Your way before me.


## Psalms 5:9 (id: 119005009)

9For not a word they speak can be trusted; destruction lies within them. Their throats are open graves; their tongues practice deceit.


## Psalms 5:10 (id: 119005010)

10Declare them guilty, O God; let them fall by their own devices. Drive them out for their many transgressions, for they have rebelled against You.


## Psalms 5:11 (id: 119005011)

11But let all who take refuge in You rejoice; let them ever shout for joy. May You shelter them, that those who love Your name may rejoice in You.


## Psalms 5:12 (id: 119005012)

12For surely You, O LORD, bless the righteous; You surround them with the shield of Your favor.


## Psalms 6:0 (id: 119006000)

0For the choirmaster. With stringed instruments, according to Sheminith. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 6:1 (id: 119006001)

1O LORD, do not rebuke me in Your anger or discipline me in Your wrath.


## Psalms 6:2 (id: 119006002)

2Be merciful to me, O LORD, for I am frail; heal me, O LORD, for my bones are in agony.


## Psalms 6:3 (id: 119006003)

3My soul is deeply distressed. How long, O LORD, how long?


## Psalms 6:4 (id: 119006004)

4Turn, O LORD, and deliver my soul; save me because of Your loving devotion.


## Psalms 6:5 (id: 119006005)

5For there is no mention of You in death; who can praise You from Sheol?


## Psalms 6:6 (id: 119006006)

6I am weary from groaning; all night I flood my bed with weeping and drench my couch with tears.


## Psalms 6:7 (id: 119006007)

7My eyes fail from grief; they grow dim because of all my foes.


## Psalms 6:8 (id: 119006008)

8Depart from me, all you workers of iniquity, for the LORD has heard my weeping.


## Psalms 6:9 (id: 119006009)

9The LORD has heard my cry for mercy; the LORD accepts my prayer.


## Psalms 6:10 (id: 119006010)

10All my enemies will be ashamed and dismayed; they will turn back in sudden disgrace.


## Psalms 7:0 (id: 119007000)

0A Shiggaion of David, which he sang to the LORD concerning the words of Cush, a Benjamite.


## Psalms 7:1 (id: 119007001)

1O LORD my God, I take refuge in You; save me and deliver me from all my pursuers,


## Psalms 7:2 (id: 119007002)

2or they will shred my soul like a lion and tear me to pieces with no one to rescue me.


## Psalms 7:3 (id: 119007003)

3O LORD my God, if I have done this, if injustice is on my hands,


## Psalms 7:4 (id: 119007004)

4if I have rewarded my ally with evil, if I have plundered my foe without cause,


## Psalms 7:5 (id: 119007005)

5then may my enemy pursue me and overtake me; may he trample me to the ground and leave my honor in the dust. Selah


## Psalms 7:6 (id: 119007006)

6Arise, O LORD, in Your anger; rise up against the fury of my enemies. Awake, my God, and ordain judgment.


## Psalms 7:7 (id: 119007007)

7Let the assembled peoples gather around You; take Your seat over them on high.


## Psalms 7:8 (id: 119007008)

8The LORD judges the peoples; vindicate me, O LORD, according to my righteousness and integrity.


## Psalms 7:9 (id: 119007009)

9Put an end to the evil of the wicked, but establish the righteous, O righteous God who searches hearts and minds.


## Psalms 7:10 (id: 119007010)

10My shield is with God, who saves the upright in heart.


## Psalms 7:11 (id: 119007011)

11God is a righteous judge and a God who feels indignation each day.


## Psalms 7:12 (id: 119007012)

12If one does not repent, God will sharpen His sword; He has bent and strung His bow.


## Psalms 7:13 (id: 119007013)

13He has prepared His deadly weapons; He ordains His arrows with fire.


## Psalms 7:14 (id: 119007014)

14Behold, the wicked man travails with evil; he conceives trouble and births falsehood.


## Psalms 7:15 (id: 119007015)

15He has dug a hole and hollowed it out; he has fallen into a pit of his own making.


## Psalms 7:16 (id: 119007016)

16His trouble recoils on himself, and his violence falls on his own head.


## Psalms 7:17 (id: 119007017)

17I will thank the LORD for His righteousness and sing praise to the name of the LORD Most High.


## Psalms 8:0 (id: 119008000)

0For the choirmaster. According to Gittith. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 8:1 (id: 119008001)

1O LORD, our Lord, how majestic is Your name in all the earth! You have set Your glory above the heavens.


## Psalms 8:2 (id: 119008002)

2From the mouths of children and infants You have ordained praise on account of Your adversaries, to silence the enemy and avenger.


## Psalms 8:3 (id: 119008003)

3When I behold Your heavens, the work of Your fingers, the moon and the stars, which You have set in place—


## Psalms 8:4 (id: 119008004)

4what is man that You are mindful of him, or the son of man that You care for him?


## Psalms 8:5 (id: 119008005)

5You made him a little lower than the angels; You crowned him with glory and honor.


## Psalms 8:6 (id: 119008006)

6You made him ruler of the works of Your hands; You have placed everything under his feet:


## Psalms 8:7 (id: 119008007)

7all sheep and oxen, and even the beasts of the field,


## Psalms 8:8 (id: 119008008)

8the birds of the air and the fish of the sea, all that swim the paths of the seas.


## Psalms 8:9 (id: 119008009)

9O LORD, our Lord, how majestic is Your name in all the earth!


## Psalms 9:0 (id: 119009000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “The Death of the Son.” A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 9:1 (id: 119009001)

1I will give thanks to the LORD with all my heart; I will recount all Your wonders.


## Psalms 9:2 (id: 119009002)

2I will be glad and rejoice in You; I will sing praise to Your name, O Most High.


## Psalms 9:3 (id: 119009003)

3When my enemies retreat, they stumble and perish before You.


## Psalms 9:4 (id: 119009004)

4For You have upheld my just cause; You sit on Your throne judging righteously.


## Psalms 9:5 (id: 119009005)

5You have rebuked the nations; You have destroyed the wicked; You have erased their name forever and ever.


## Psalms 9:6 (id: 119009006)

6The enemy has come to eternal ruin, and You have uprooted their cities; the very memory of them has vanished.


## Psalms 9:7 (id: 119009007)

7But the LORD abides forever; He has established His throne for judgment.


## Psalms 9:8 (id: 119009008)

8He judges the world with justice; He governs the people with equity.


## Psalms 9:9 (id: 119009009)

9The LORD is a refuge for the oppressed, a stronghold in times of trouble.


## Psalms 9:10 (id: 119009010)

10Those who know Your name trust in You, for You, O LORD, have not forsaken those who seek You.


## Psalms 9:11 (id: 119009011)

11Sing praises to the LORD, who dwells in Zion; proclaim His deeds among the nations.


## Psalms 9:12 (id: 119009012)

12For the Avenger of bloodshed remembers; He does not ignore the cry of the afflicted.


## Psalms 9:13 (id: 119009013)

13Be merciful to me, O LORD; see how my enemies afflict me! Lift me up from the gates of death,


## Psalms 9:14 (id: 119009014)

14that I may declare all Your praises—that within the gates of Daughter Zion I may rejoice in Your salvation.


## Psalms 9:15 (id: 119009015)

15The nations have fallen into a pit of their making; their feet are caught in the net they have hidden.


## Psalms 9:16 (id: 119009016)

16The LORD is known by the justice He brings; the wicked are ensnared by the work of their hands. Higgaion Selah


## Psalms 9:17 (id: 119009017)

17The wicked will return to Sheol—all the nations who forget God.


## Psalms 9:18 (id: 119009018)

18For the needy will not always be forgotten; nor the hope of the oppressed forever dashed.


## Psalms 9:19 (id: 119009019)

19Rise up, O LORD, do not let man prevail; let the nations be judged in Your presence.


## Psalms 9:20 (id: 119009020)

20Lay terror upon them, O LORD; let the nations know they are but men. Selah


## Psalms 10:1 (id: 119010001)

1Why, O LORD, do You stand far off? Why do You hide in times of trouble?


## Psalms 10:2 (id: 119010002)

2In pride the wicked pursue the needy; let them be caught in the schemes they devise.


## Psalms 10:3 (id: 119010003)

3For the wicked man boasts in the cravings of his heart; he blesses the greedy and reviles the LORD.


## Psalms 10:4 (id: 119010004)

4In his pride the wicked man does not seek Him; in all his schemes there is no God.


## Psalms 10:5 (id: 119010005)

5He is secure in his ways at all times; Your lofty judgments are far from him; he sneers at all his foes.


## Psalms 10:6 (id: 119010006)

6He says to himself, “I will not be moved; from age to age I am free of distress.”


## Psalms 10:7 (id: 119010007)

7His mouth is full of cursing, deceit, and violence; trouble and malice are under his tongue.


## Psalms 10:8 (id: 119010008)

8He lies in wait near the villages; in ambush he slays the innocent; his eyes watch in stealth for the helpless.


## Psalms 10:9 (id: 119010009)

9He lies in wait like a lion in a thicket; he lurks to seize the oppressed; he catches the lowly in his net.


## Psalms 10:10 (id: 119010010)

10They are crushed and beaten down; the helpless fall prey to his strength.


## Psalms 10:11 (id: 119010011)

11He says to himself, “God has forgotten; He hides His face and never sees.”


## Psalms 10:12 (id: 119010012)

12Arise, O LORD! Lift up Your hand, O God! Do not forget the helpless.


## Psalms 10:13 (id: 119010013)

13Why has the wicked man renounced God? He says to himself, “You will never call me to account.”


## Psalms 10:14 (id: 119010014)

14But You have regarded trouble and grief; You see to repay it by Your hand. The victim entrusts himself to You; You are the helper of the fatherless.


## Psalms 10:15 (id: 119010015)

15Break the arm of the wicked and evildoer; call him to account for his wickedness until none is left to be found.


## Psalms 10:16 (id: 119010016)

16The LORD is King forever and ever; the nations perish from His land.


## Psalms 10:17 (id: 119010017)

17You have heard, O LORD, the desire of the humble; You will strengthen their hearts. You will incline Your ear,


## Psalms 10:18 (id: 119010018)

18to vindicate the fatherless and oppressed, that the men of the earth may strike terror no more.


## Psalms 11:0 (id: 119011000)

0For the choirmaster. Of David.


## Psalms 11:1 (id: 119011001)

1In the LORD I take refuge. How then can you say to me: “Flee like a bird to your mountain!


## Psalms 11:2 (id: 119011002)

2For behold, the wicked bend their bows. They set their arrow on the string to shoot from the shadows at the upright in heart.


## Psalms 11:3 (id: 119011003)

3If the foundations are destroyed, what can the righteous do?”


## Psalms 11:4 (id: 119011004)

4The LORD is in His holy temple; the LORD is on His heavenly throne. His eyes are watching closely; they examine the sons of men.


## Psalms 11:5 (id: 119011005)

5The LORD tests the righteous and the wicked; His soul hates the lover of violence.


## Psalms 11:6 (id: 119011006)

6On the wicked He will rain down fiery coals and sulfur; a scorching wind will be their portion.


## Psalms 11:7 (id: 119011007)

7For the LORD is righteous; He loves justice. The upright will see His face.


## Psalms 12:0 (id: 119012000)

0For the choirmaster. According to Sheminith. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 12:1 (id: 119012001)

1Help, O LORD, for the godly are no more; the faithful have vanished from among men.


## Psalms 12:2 (id: 119012002)

2They lie to one another; they speak with flattering lips and a double heart.


## Psalms 12:3 (id: 119012003)

3May the LORD cut off all flattering lips and every boastful tongue.


## Psalms 12:4 (id: 119012004)

4They say, “With our tongues we will prevail. We own our lips—who can be our master?”


## Psalms 12:5 (id: 119012005)

5“For the cause of the oppressed and for the groaning of the needy, I will now arise,” says the LORD. “I will bring safety to him who yearns.”


## Psalms 12:6 (id: 119012006)

6The words of the LORD are flawless, like silver refined in a furnace, like gold purified sevenfold.


## Psalms 12:7 (id: 119012007)

7You, O LORD, will keep us; You will forever guard us from this generation.


## Psalms 12:8 (id: 119012008)

8The wicked wander freely, and vileness is exalted among men.


## Psalms 13:0 (id: 119013000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 13:1 (id: 119013001)

1How long, O LORD? Will You forget me forever? How long will You hide Your face from me?


## Psalms 13:2 (id: 119013002)

2How long must I wrestle in my soul, with sorrow in my heart each day? How long will my enemy dominate me?


## Psalms 13:3 (id: 119013003)

3Consider me and respond, O LORD my God. Give light to my eyes, lest I sleep in death,


## Psalms 13:4 (id: 119013004)

4lest my enemy say, “I have overcome him,” and my foes rejoice when I fall.


## Psalms 13:5 (id: 119013005)

5But I have trusted in Your loving devotion; my heart will rejoice in Your salvation.


## Psalms 13:6 (id: 119013006)

6I will sing to the LORD, for He has been good to me.


## Psalms 14:0 (id: 119014000)

0For the choirmaster. Of David.


## Psalms 14:1 (id: 119014001)

1The fool says in his heart, “There is no God.” They are corrupt; their acts are vile. There is no one who does good.


## Psalms 14:2 (id: 119014002)

2The LORD looks down from heaven upon the sons of men to see if any understand, if any seek God.


## Psalms 14:3 (id: 119014003)

3All have turned away, they have together become corrupt; there is no one who does good, not even one.


## Psalms 14:4 (id: 119014004)

4Will the workers of iniquity never learn? They devour my people like bread; they refuse to call upon the LORD.


## Psalms 14:5 (id: 119014005)

5There they are, overwhelmed with dread, for God is in the company of the righteous.


## Psalms 14:6 (id: 119014006)

6You sinners frustrate the plans of the oppressed, yet the LORD is their shelter.


## Psalms 14:7 (id: 119014007)

7Oh, that the salvation of Israel would come from Zion! When the LORD restores His captive people, let Jacob rejoice, let Israel be glad!


## Psalms 15:0 (id: 119015000)

0A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 15:1 (id: 119015001)

1O LORD, who may abide in Your tent? Who may dwell on Your holy mountain?


## Psalms 15:2 (id: 119015002)

2He who walks with integrity and practices righteousness, who speaks the truth from his heart,


## Psalms 15:3 (id: 119015003)

3who has no slander on his tongue, who does no harm to his neighbor, who casts no scorn on his friend,


## Psalms 15:4 (id: 119015004)

4who despises the vile but honors those who fear the LORD, who does not revise a costly oath,


## Psalms 15:5 (id: 119015005)

5who lends his money without interest and refuses a bribe against the innocent. He who does these things will never be shaken.


## Psalms 16:0 (id: 119016000)

0A Miktam of David.


## Psalms 16:1 (id: 119016001)

1Preserve me, O God, for in You I take refuge.


## Psalms 16:2 (id: 119016002)

2I said to the LORD, “You are my Lord; apart from You I have no good thing.”


## Psalms 16:3 (id: 119016003)

3As for the saints in the land, they are the excellence in whom all my delight resides.


## Psalms 16:4 (id: 119016004)

4Sorrows will multiply to those who chase other gods. I will not pour out their libations of blood, or speak their names with my lips.


## Psalms 16:5 (id: 119016005)

5The LORD is my chosen portion and my cup; You have made my lot secure.


## Psalms 16:6 (id: 119016006)

6The lines of my boundary have fallen in pleasant places; surely my inheritance is delightful.


## Psalms 16:7 (id: 119016007)

7I will bless the LORD who counsels me; even at night my conscience instructs me.


## Psalms 16:8 (id: 119016008)

8I have set the LORD always before me. Because He is at my right hand, I will not be shaken.


## Psalms 16:9 (id: 119016009)

9Therefore my heart is glad and my tongue rejoices; my body also will dwell securely.


## Psalms 16:10 (id: 119016010)

10For You will not abandon my soul to Sheol, nor will You let Your Holy One see decay.


## Psalms 16:11 (id: 119016011)

11You have made known to me the path of life; You will fill me with joy in Your presence, with eternal pleasures at Your right hand.


## Psalms 17:0 (id: 119017000)

0A prayer of David.


## Psalms 17:1 (id: 119017001)

1Hear, O LORD, my righteous plea; listen to my cry. Give ear to my prayer—it comes from lips free of deceit.


## Psalms 17:2 (id: 119017002)

2May my vindication come from Your presence; may Your eyes see what is right.


## Psalms 17:3 (id: 119017003)

3You have tried my heart; You have visited me in the night. You have tested me and found no evil; I have resolved not to sin with my mouth.


## Psalms 17:4 (id: 119017004)

4As for the deeds of men—by the word of Your lips I have avoided the ways of the violent.


## Psalms 17:5 (id: 119017005)

5My steps have held to Your paths; my feet have not slipped.


## Psalms 17:6 (id: 119017006)

6I call on You, O God, for You will answer me. Incline Your ear to me; hear my words.


## Psalms 17:7 (id: 119017007)

7Show the wonders of Your loving devotion, You who save by Your right hand those who seek refuge from their foes.


## Psalms 17:8 (id: 119017008)

8Keep me as the apple of Your eye; hide me in the shadow of Your wings


## Psalms 17:9 (id: 119017009)

9from the wicked who assail me, from my mortal enemies who surround me.


## Psalms 17:10 (id: 119017010)

10They have closed their callous hearts; their mouths speak with arrogance.


## Psalms 17:11 (id: 119017011)

11They have tracked us down, and now surround us; their eyes are set to cast us to the ground,


## Psalms 17:12 (id: 119017012)

12like a lion greedy for prey, like a young lion lurking in ambush.


## Psalms 17:13 (id: 119017013)

13Arise, O LORD, confront them! Bring them to their knees; deliver me from the wicked by Your sword,


## Psalms 17:14 (id: 119017014)

14from such men, O LORD, by Your hand—from men of the world whose portion is in this life. May You fill the bellies of Your treasured ones and satisfy their sons, so they leave their abundance to their children.


## Psalms 17:15 (id: 119017015)

15As for me, I will behold Your face in righteousness; when I awake, I will be satisfied in Your presence.


## Psalms 18:0 (id: 119018000)

0For the choirmaster. Of David the servant of the LORD, who sang this song to the LORD on the day the LORD had delivered him from the hand of all his enemies and from the hand of Saul. He said:


## Psalms 18:1 (id: 119018001)

1I love You, O LORD, my strength.


## Psalms 18:2 (id: 119018002)

2The LORD is my rock, my fortress, and my deliverer. My God is my rock, in whom I take refuge, my shield, and the horn of my salvation, my stronghold.


## Psalms 18:3 (id: 119018003)

3I will call upon the LORD, who is worthy to be praised; so shall I be saved from my enemies.


## Psalms 18:4 (id: 119018004)

4The cords of death encompassed me; the torrents of chaos overwhelmed me.


## Psalms 18:5 (id: 119018005)

5The cords of Sheol entangled me; the snares of death confronted me.


## Psalms 18:6 (id: 119018006)

6In my distress I called upon the LORD; I cried to my God for help. From His temple He heard my voice, and my cry for His help reached His ears.


## Psalms 18:7 (id: 119018007)

7Then the earth shook and quaked, and the foundations of the mountains trembled; they were shaken because He burned with anger.


## Psalms 18:8 (id: 119018008)

8Smoke rose from His nostrils, and consuming fire came from His mouth; glowing coals blazed forth.


## Psalms 18:9 (id: 119018009)

9He parted the heavens and came down with dark clouds beneath His feet.


## Psalms 18:10 (id: 119018010)

10He mounted a cherub and flew; He soared on the wings of the wind.


## Psalms 18:11 (id: 119018011)

11He made darkness His hiding place, and storm clouds a canopy around Him.


## Psalms 18:12 (id: 119018012)

12From the brightness of His presence His clouds advanced—hailstones and coals of fire.


## Psalms 18:13 (id: 119018013)

13The LORD thundered from heaven; the voice of the Most High resounded—hailstones and coals of fire.


## Psalms 18:14 (id: 119018014)

14He shot His arrows and scattered the foes; He hurled lightning and routed them.


## Psalms 18:15 (id: 119018015)

15The channels of the sea appeared, and the foundations of the world were exposed, at Your rebuke, O LORD, at the blast of the breath of Your nostrils.


## Psalms 18:16 (id: 119018016)

16He reached down from on high and took hold of me; He drew me out of deep waters.


## Psalms 18:17 (id: 119018017)

17He rescued me from my powerful enemy, from foes too mighty for me.


## Psalms 18:18 (id: 119018018)

18They confronted me in my day of calamity, but the LORD was my support.


## Psalms 18:19 (id: 119018019)

19He brought me out into the open; He rescued me because He delighted in me.


## Psalms 18:20 (id: 119018020)

20The LORD has rewarded me according to my righteousness; He has repaid me according to the cleanness of my hands.


## Psalms 18:21 (id: 119018021)

21For I have kept the ways of the LORD and have not wickedly departed from my God.


## Psalms 18:22 (id: 119018022)

22For all His ordinances are before me; I have not disregarded His statutes.


## Psalms 18:23 (id: 119018023)

23And I have been blameless before Him and kept myself from iniquity.


## Psalms 18:24 (id: 119018024)

24So the LORD has repaid me according to my righteousness, according to the cleanness of my hands in His sight.


## Psalms 18:25 (id: 119018025)

25To the faithful You show Yourself faithful, to the blameless You show Yourself blameless;


## Psalms 18:26 (id: 119018026)

26to the pure You show Yourself pure, but to the crooked You show Yourself shrewd.


## Psalms 18:27 (id: 119018027)

27For You save an afflicted people, but You humble those with haughty eyes.


## Psalms 18:28 (id: 119018028)

28For You, O LORD, light my lamp; my God lights up my darkness.


## Psalms 18:29 (id: 119018029)

29For in You I can charge an army, and with my God I can scale a wall.


## Psalms 18:30 (id: 119018030)

30As for God, His way is perfect; the word of the LORD is flawless. He is a shield to all who take refuge in Him.


## Psalms 18:31 (id: 119018031)

31For who is God besides the LORD? And who is the Rock except our God?


## Psalms 18:32 (id: 119018032)

32It is God who arms me with strength and makes my way clear.


## Psalms 18:33 (id: 119018033)

33He makes my feet like those of a deer and stations me upon the heights.


## Psalms 18:34 (id: 119018034)

34He trains my hands for battle; my arms can bend a bow of bronze.


## Psalms 18:35 (id: 119018035)

35You have given me Your shield of salvation; Your right hand upholds me, and Your gentleness exalts me.


## Psalms 18:36 (id: 119018036)

36You broaden the path beneath me so that my ankles do not give way.


## Psalms 18:37 (id: 119018037)

37I pursued my enemies and overtook them; I did not turn back until they were consumed.


## Psalms 18:38 (id: 119018038)

38I crushed them so they could not rise; they have fallen under my feet.


## Psalms 18:39 (id: 119018039)

39You have armed me with strength for battle; You have subdued my foes beneath me.


## Psalms 18:40 (id: 119018040)

40You have made my enemies retreat before me; I destroyed those who hated me.


## Psalms 18:41 (id: 119018041)

41They cried for help, but there was no one to save them—to the LORD, but He did not answer.


## Psalms 18:42 (id: 119018042)

42I ground them as dust in the face of the wind; I trampled them like mud in the streets.


## Psalms 18:43 (id: 119018043)

43You have delivered me from the strife of the people; You have made me the head of nations; a people I had not known shall serve me.


## Psalms 18:44 (id: 119018044)

44When they hear me, they obey me; foreigners cower before me.


## Psalms 18:45 (id: 119018045)

45Foreigners lose heart and come trembling from their strongholds.


## Psalms 18:46 (id: 119018046)

46The LORD lives, and blessed be my Rock! And may the God of my salvation be exalted—


## Psalms 18:47 (id: 119018047)

47the God who avenges me and subdues nations beneath me,


## Psalms 18:48 (id: 119018048)

48who delivers me from my enemies. You exalt me above my foes; You rescue me from violent men.


## Psalms 18:49 (id: 119018049)

49Therefore I will praise You, O LORD, among the nations; I will sing praises to Your name.


## Psalms 18:50 (id: 119018050)

50Great salvation He brings to His king. He shows loving devotion to His anointed, to David and his descendants forever.


## Psalms 19:0 (id: 119019000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 19:1 (id: 119019001)

1The heavens declare the glory of God; the skies proclaim the work of His hands.


## Psalms 19:2 (id: 119019002)

2Day after day they pour forth speech; night after night they reveal knowledge.


## Psalms 19:3 (id: 119019003)

3Without speech or language, without a sound to be heard,


## Psalms 19:4 (id: 119019004)

4their voice has gone out into all the earth, their words to the ends of the world. In the heavens He has pitched a tent for the sun.


## Psalms 19:5 (id: 119019005)

5Like a bridegroom emerging from his chamber, like a champion rejoicing to run his course,


## Psalms 19:6 (id: 119019006)

6it rises at one end of the heavens and runs its circuit to the other; nothing is deprived of its warmth.


## Psalms 19:7 (id: 119019007)

7The Law of the LORD is perfect, reviving the soul; the testimony of the LORD is trustworthy, making wise the simple.


## Psalms 19:8 (id: 119019008)

8The precepts of the LORD are right, bringing joy to the heart; the commandments of the LORD are radiant, giving light to the eyes.


## Psalms 19:9 (id: 119019009)

9The fear of the LORD is pure, enduring forever; the judgments of the LORD are true, being altogether righteous.


## Psalms 19:10 (id: 119019010)

10They are more precious than gold, than much pure gold; they are sweeter than honey, than honey from the comb.


## Psalms 19:11 (id: 119019011)

11By them indeed Your servant is warned; in keeping them is great reward.


## Psalms 19:12 (id: 119019012)

12Who can discern his own errors? Cleanse me from my hidden faults.


## Psalms 19:13 (id: 119019013)

13Keep Your servant also from willful sins; may they not rule over me. Then I will be blameless and cleansed of great transgression.


## Psalms 19:14 (id: 119019014)

14May the words of my mouth and the meditation of my heart be pleasing in Your sight, O LORD, my Rock and my Redeemer.


## Psalms 20:0 (id: 119020000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 20:1 (id: 119020001)

1May the LORD answer you in the day of trouble; may the name of the God of Jacob protect you.


## Psalms 20:2 (id: 119020002)

2May He send you help from the sanctuary and sustain you from Zion.


## Psalms 20:3 (id: 119020003)

3May He remember all your gifts and look favorably on your burnt offerings. Selah


## Psalms 20:4 (id: 119020004)

4May He give you the desires of your heart and make all your plans succeed.


## Psalms 20:5 (id: 119020005)

5May we shout for joy at your victory and raise a banner in the name of our God. May the LORD grant all your petitions.


## Psalms 20:6 (id: 119020006)

6Now I know that the LORD saves His anointed; He answers him from His holy heaven with the saving power of His right hand.


## Psalms 20:7 (id: 119020007)

7Some trust in chariots and others in horses, but we trust in the name of the LORD our God.


## Psalms 20:8 (id: 119020008)

8They collapse and fall, but we rise up and stand firm.


## Psalms 20:9 (id: 119020009)

9O LORD, save the king. Answer us on the day we call.


## Psalms 21:0 (id: 119021000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 21:1 (id: 119021001)

1O LORD, the king rejoices in Your strength. How greatly he exults in Your salvation!


## Psalms 21:2 (id: 119021002)

2You have granted his heart’s desire and have not withheld the request of his lips. Selah


## Psalms 21:3 (id: 119021003)

3For You welcomed him with rich blessings; You placed on his head a crown of pure gold.


## Psalms 21:4 (id: 119021004)

4He asked You for life, and You granted it—length of days, forever and ever.


## Psalms 21:5 (id: 119021005)

5Great is his glory in Your salvation; You bestow on him splendor and majesty.


## Psalms 21:6 (id: 119021006)

6For You grant him blessings forever; You cheer him with joy in Your presence.


## Psalms 21:7 (id: 119021007)

7For the king trusts in the LORD; through the loving devotion of the Most High, he will not be shaken.


## Psalms 21:8 (id: 119021008)

8Your hand will apprehend all Your enemies; Your right hand will seize those who hate You.


## Psalms 21:9 (id: 119021009)

9You will place them in a fiery furnace at the time of Your appearing. In His wrath the LORD will engulf them, and the fire will consume them.


## Psalms 21:10 (id: 119021010)

10You will wipe their descendants from the earth, and their offspring from the sons of men.


## Psalms 21:11 (id: 119021011)

11Though they intend You harm, the schemes they devise will not prevail.


## Psalms 21:12 (id: 119021012)

12For You will put them to flight when Your bow is trained upon them.


## Psalms 21:13 (id: 119021013)

13Be exalted, O LORD, in Your strength; we will sing and praise Your power.


## Psalms 22:0 (id: 119022000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “The Doe of the Dawn.” A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 22:1 (id: 119022001)

1My God, my God, why have You forsaken me? Why are You so far from saving me, so far from my words of groaning?


## Psalms 22:2 (id: 119022002)

2I cry out by day, O my God, but You do not answer, and by night, but I have no rest.


## Psalms 22:3 (id: 119022003)

3Yet You are holy, enthroned on the praises of Israel.


## Psalms 22:4 (id: 119022004)

4In You our fathers trusted; they trusted and You delivered them.


## Psalms 22:5 (id: 119022005)

5They cried out to You and were set free; they trusted in You and were not disappointed.


## Psalms 22:6 (id: 119022006)

6But I am a worm and not a man, scorned by men and despised by the people.


## Psalms 22:7 (id: 119022007)

7All who see me mock me; they sneer and shake their heads:


## Psalms 22:8 (id: 119022008)

8“He trusts in the LORD, let the LORD deliver him; let the LORD rescue him, since He delights in him.”


## Psalms 22:9 (id: 119022009)

9Yet You brought me forth from the womb; You made me secure at my mother’s breast.


## Psalms 22:10 (id: 119022010)

10From birth I was cast upon You; from my mother’s womb You have been my God.


## Psalms 22:11 (id: 119022011)

11Be not far from me, for trouble is near and there is no one to help.


## Psalms 22:12 (id: 119022012)

12Many bulls surround me; strong bulls of Bashan encircle me.


## Psalms 22:13 (id: 119022013)

13They open their jaws against me like lions that roar and maul.


## Psalms 22:14 (id: 119022014)

14I am poured out like water, and all my bones are disjointed. My heart is like wax; it melts away within me.


## Psalms 22:15 (id: 119022015)

15My strength is dried up like a potsherd, and my tongue sticks to the roof of my mouth. You lay me in the dust of death.


## Psalms 22:16 (id: 119022016)

16For dogs surround me; a band of evil men encircles me; they have pierced my hands and feet.


## Psalms 22:17 (id: 119022017)

17I can count all my bones; they stare and gloat over me.


## Psalms 22:18 (id: 119022018)

18They divide my garments among them and cast lots for my clothing.


## Psalms 22:19 (id: 119022019)

19But You, O LORD, be not far off; O my Strength, come quickly to help me.


## Psalms 22:20 (id: 119022020)

20Deliver my soul from the sword, my precious life from the power of wild dogs.


## Psalms 22:21 (id: 119022021)

21Save me from the mouth of the lion; at the horns of the wild oxen You have answered me!


## Psalms 22:22 (id: 119022022)

22I will proclaim Your name to my brothers; I will praise You in the assembly.


## Psalms 22:23 (id: 119022023)

23You who fear the LORD, praise Him! All descendants of Jacob, honor Him! All offspring of Israel, revere Him!


## Psalms 22:24 (id: 119022024)

24For He has not despised or detested the torment of the afflicted. He has not hidden His face from him, but has attended to his cry for help.


## Psalms 22:25 (id: 119022025)

25My praise for You resounds in the great assembly; I will fulfill my vows before those who fear You.


## Psalms 22:26 (id: 119022026)

26The poor will eat and be satisfied; those who seek the LORD will praise Him. May your hearts live forever!


## Psalms 22:27 (id: 119022027)

27All the ends of the earth will remember and turn to the LORD. All the families of the nations will bow down before Him.


## Psalms 22:28 (id: 119022028)

28For dominion belongs to the LORD and He rules over the nations.


## Psalms 22:29 (id: 119022029)

29All the rich of the earth will feast and worship; all who go down to the dust will kneel before Him—even those unable to preserve their lives.


## Psalms 22:30 (id: 119022030)

30Posterity will serve Him; they will declare the Lord to a new generation.


## Psalms 22:31 (id: 119022031)

31They will come and proclaim His righteousness to a people yet unborn—all that He has done.

0A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 23:1 (id: 119023001)

1The LORD is my shepherd; I shall not want.


## Psalms 23:2 (id: 119023002)

2He makes me lie down in green pastures; He leads me beside quiet waters.


## Psalms 23:3 (id: 119023003)

3He restores my soul; He guides me in the paths of righteousness for the sake of His name.


## Psalms 23:4 (id: 119023004)

4Even though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil, for You are with me; Your rod and Your staff, they comfort me.


## Psalms 23:5 (id: 119023005)

5You prepare a table before me in the presence of my enemies. You anoint my head with oil; my cup overflows.


## Psalms 23:6 (id: 119023006)

6Surely goodness and mercy will follow me all the days of my life, and I will dwell in the house of the LORD forever.

## Psalms 24:1 (id: 119024001)

## Psalms 24:2 (id: 119024002)

## Psalms 24:5 (id: 119024005)

## Psalms 25:0 (id: 119025000)

0Of David.


## Psalms 25:1 (id: 119025001)

1To You, O LORD, I lift up my soul;


## Psalms 25:2 (id: 119025002)

2in You, my God, I trust. Do not let me be put to shame; do not let my enemies exult over me.


## Psalms 25:3 (id: 119025003)

3Surely none who wait for You will be put to shame; but those who engage in treachery without cause will be disgraced.


## Psalms 25:4 (id: 119025004)

4Show me Your ways, O LORD; teach me Your paths.


## Psalms 25:5 (id: 119025005)

5Guide me in Your truth and teach me, for You are the God of my salvation; all day long I wait for You.


## Psalms 25:6 (id: 119025006)

6Remember, O LORD, Your compassion and loving devotion, for they are from age to age.


## Psalms 25:7 (id: 119025007)

7Remember not the sins of my youth, nor my rebellious acts; remember me according to Your loving devotion, because of Your goodness, O LORD.


## Psalms 25:8 (id: 119025008)

8Good and upright is the LORD; therefore He shows sinners the way.


## Psalms 25:9 (id: 119025009)

9He guides the humble in what is right and teaches them His way.


## Psalms 25:10 (id: 119025010)

10All the LORD’s ways are loving and faithful to those who keep His covenant and His decrees.


## Psalms 25:11 (id: 119025011)

11For the sake of Your name, O LORD, forgive my iniquity, for it is great.


## Psalms 25:12 (id: 119025012)

12Who is the man who fears the LORD? He will instruct him in the path chosen for him.


## Psalms 25:13 (id: 119025013)

13His soul will dwell in prosperity, and his descendants will inherit the land.


## Psalms 25:14 (id: 119025014)

14The LORD confides in those who fear Him, and reveals His covenant to them.


## Psalms 25:15 (id: 119025015)

15My eyes are always on the LORD, for He will free my feet from the mesh.


## Psalms 25:16 (id: 119025016)

16Turn to me and be gracious, for I am lonely and afflicted.


## Psalms 25:17 (id: 119025017)

17The troubles of my heart increase; free me from my distress.


## Psalms 25:18 (id: 119025018)

18Consider my affliction and trouble, and take away all my sins.


## Psalms 25:19 (id: 119025019)

19Consider my enemies, for they are many, and they hate me with vicious hatred.


## Psalms 25:20 (id: 119025020)

20Guard my soul and deliver me; let me not be put to shame, for I take refuge in You.


## Psalms 25:21 (id: 119025021)

21May integrity and uprightness preserve me, because I wait for You.


## Psalms 25:22 (id: 119025022)

22Redeem Israel, O God, from all its distress.


## Psalms 26:0 (id: 119026000)

0Of David.


## Psalms 26:1 (id: 119026001)

1Vindicate me, O LORD! For I have walked with integrity; I have trusted in the LORD without wavering.


## Psalms 26:2 (id: 119026002)

2Test me, O LORD, and try me; examine my heart and mind.


## Psalms 26:3 (id: 119026003)

3For Your loving devotion is before my eyes, and I have walked in Your truth.


## Psalms 26:4 (id: 119026004)

4I do not sit with deceitful men, nor keep company with hypocrites.


## Psalms 26:5 (id: 119026005)

5I hate the mob of evildoers, and refuse to sit with the wicked.


## Psalms 26:6 (id: 119026006)

6I wash my hands in innocence that I may go about Your altar, O LORD,


## Psalms 26:7 (id: 119026007)

7to raise my voice in thanksgiving and declare all Your wonderful works.


## Psalms 26:8 (id: 119026008)

8O LORD, I love the house where You dwell, the place where Your glory resides.


## Psalms 26:9 (id: 119026009)

9Do not take my soul away with sinners, or my life with men of bloodshed,


## Psalms 26:10 (id: 119026010)

10in whose hands are wicked schemes, whose right hands are full of bribes.


## Psalms 26:11 (id: 119026011)

11But I will walk with integrity; redeem me and be merciful to me.


## Psalms 26:12 (id: 119026012)

12My feet stand on level ground; in the congregations I will bless the LORD.


## Psalms 27:0 (id: 119027000)

0Of David.


## Psalms 27:1 (id: 119027001)

1The LORD is my light and my salvation—whom shall I fear? The LORD is the stronghold of my life—whom shall I dread?


## Psalms 27:2 (id: 119027002)

2When the wicked came upon me to devour my flesh, my enemies and foes stumbled and fell.


## Psalms 27:3 (id: 119027003)

3Though an army encamps around me, my heart will not fear; though a war breaks out against me, I will keep my trust.


## Psalms 27:4 (id: 119027004)

4One thing I have asked of the LORD; this is what I desire: to dwell in the house of the LORD all the days of my life, to gaze on the beauty of the LORD and seek Him in His temple.


## Psalms 27:5 (id: 119027005)

5For in the day of trouble He will hide me in His shelter; He will conceal me under the cover of His tent; He will set me high upon a rock.


## Psalms 27:6 (id: 119027006)

6Then my head will be held high above my enemies around me. At His tabernacle I will offer sacrifices with shouts of joy; I will sing and make music to the LORD.


## Psalms 27:7 (id: 119027007)

7Hear, O LORD, my voice when I call; be merciful and answer me.


## Psalms 27:8 (id: 119027008)

8My heart said, “Seek His face.” Your face, O LORD, I will seek.


## Psalms 27:9 (id: 119027009)

9Hide not Your face from me, nor turn away Your servant in anger. You have been my helper; do not leave me or forsake me, O God of my salvation.


## Psalms 27:10 (id: 119027010)

10Though my father and mother forsake me, the LORD will receive me.


## Psalms 27:11 (id: 119027011)

11Teach me Your way, O LORD, and lead me on a level path, because of my oppressors.


## Psalms 27:12 (id: 119027012)

12Do not hand me over to the will of my foes, for false witnesses rise up against me, breathing out violence.


## Psalms 27:13 (id: 119027013)

13Still I am certain to see the goodness of the LORD in the land of the living.


## Psalms 27:14 (id: 119027014)

14Wait patiently for the LORD; be strong and courageous. Wait patiently for the LORD!


## Psalms 28:0 (id: 119028000)

0Of David.


## Psalms 28:1 (id: 119028001)

1To You, O LORD, I call; be not deaf to me, O my Rock. For if You remain silent, I will be like those descending to the Pit.


## Psalms 28:2 (id: 119028002)

2Hear my cry for mercy when I call to You for help, when I lift up my hands toward Your holy sanctuary.


## Psalms 28:3 (id: 119028003)

3Do not drag me away with the wicked, and with the workers of iniquity, who speak peace to their neighbors while malice is in their hearts.


## Psalms 28:4 (id: 119028004)

4Repay them according to their deeds and for their works of evil. Repay them for what their hands have done; bring back on them what they deserve.


## Psalms 28:5 (id: 119028005)

5Since they show no regard for the works of the LORD or what His hands have done, He will tear them down and never rebuild them.


## Psalms 28:6 (id: 119028006)

6Blessed be the LORD, for He has heard my cry for mercy.


## Psalms 28:7 (id: 119028007)

7The LORD is my strength and my shield; my heart trusts in Him, and I am helped. Therefore my heart rejoices, and I give thanks to Him with my song.


## Psalms 28:8 (id: 119028008)

8The LORD is the strength of His people, a stronghold of salvation for His anointed.


## Psalms 28:9 (id: 119028009)

9Save Your people and bless Your inheritance; shepherd them and carry them forever.
