0A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 29:1 (id: 119029001)

1Ascribe to the LORD, O heavenly beings, ascribe to the LORD glory and strength.


## Psalms 29:2 (id: 119029002)

2Ascribe to the LORD the glory due His name; worship the LORD in the splendor of His holiness.


## Psalms 29:3 (id: 119029003)

3The voice of the LORD is over the waters; the God of glory thunders; the LORD is heard over many waters.


## Psalms 29:4 (id: 119029004)

4The voice of the LORD is powerful; the voice of the LORD is majestic.


## Psalms 29:5 (id: 119029005)

5The voice of the LORD breaks the cedars; the LORD shatters the cedars of Lebanon.


## Psalms 29:6 (id: 119029006)

6He makes Lebanon skip like a calf, and Sirion like a young wild ox.


## Psalms 29:7 (id: 119029007)

7The voice of the LORD strikes with flames of fire.


## Psalms 29:8 (id: 119029008)

8The voice of the LORD shakes the wilderness; the LORD shakes the Wilderness of Kadesh.


## Psalms 29:9 (id: 119029009)

9The voice of the LORD twists the oaks and strips the forests bare. And in His temple all cry, “Glory!”


## Psalms 29:10 (id: 119029010)

10The LORD sits enthroned over the flood; the LORD is enthroned as King forever.


## Psalms 29:11 (id: 119029011)

11The LORD gives His people strength; the LORD blesses His people with peace.


## Psalms 30:0 (id: 119030000)

0A Psalm. A song for the dedication of the temple. Of David.


## Psalms 30:1 (id: 119030001)

1I will exalt You, O LORD, for You have lifted me up and have not allowed my foes to rejoice over me.


## Psalms 30:2 (id: 119030002)

2O LORD my God, I cried to You for help, and You healed me.


## Psalms 30:3 (id: 119030003)

3O LORD, You pulled me up from Sheol; You spared me from descending into the Pit.


## Psalms 30:4 (id: 119030004)

4Sing to the LORD, O you His saints, and praise His holy name.


## Psalms 30:5 (id: 119030005)

5For His anger is fleeting, but His favor lasts a lifetime. Weeping may stay the night, but joy comes in the morning.


## Psalms 30:6 (id: 119030006)

6In prosperity I said, “I will never be shaken.”


## Psalms 30:7 (id: 119030007)

7O LORD, You favored me; You made my mountain stand strong. When You hid Your face, I was dismayed.


## Psalms 30:8 (id: 119030008)

8To You, O LORD, I called, and I begged my Lord for mercy:


## Psalms 30:9 (id: 119030009)

9“What gain is there in my bloodshed, in my descent to the Pit? Will the dust praise You? Will it proclaim Your faithfulness?


## Psalms 30:10 (id: 119030010)

10Hear me, O LORD, and have mercy; O LORD, be my helper.”


## Psalms 30:11 (id: 119030011)

11You turned my mourning into dancing; You peeled off my sackcloth and clothed me with joy,


## Psalms 30:12 (id: 119030012)

12that my heart may sing Your praises and not be silent. O LORD my God, I will give thanks forever.


## Psalms 31:0 (id: 119031000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 31:1 (id: 119031001)

1In You, O LORD, I have taken refuge; let me never be put to shame; save me by Your righteousness.


## Psalms 31:2 (id: 119031002)

2Incline Your ear to me; come quickly to my rescue. Be my rock of refuge, the stronghold of my deliverance.


## Psalms 31:3 (id: 119031003)

3For You are my rock and my fortress; lead me and guide me for the sake of Your name.


## Psalms 31:4 (id: 119031004)

4You free me from the net laid out for me, for You are my refuge.


## Psalms 31:5 (id: 119031005)

5Into Your hands I commit my spirit; You have redeemed me, O LORD, God of truth.


## Psalms 31:6 (id: 119031006)

6I hate those who cling to worthless idols, but in the LORD I trust.


## Psalms 31:7 (id: 119031007)

7I will be glad and rejoice in Your loving devotion, for You have seen my affliction; You have known the anguish of my soul.


## Psalms 31:8 (id: 119031008)

8You have not delivered me to the enemy; You have set my feet in the open.


## Psalms 31:9 (id: 119031009)

9Be merciful to me, O LORD, for I am in distress; my eyes fail from sorrow, my soul and body as well.


## Psalms 31:10 (id: 119031010)

10For my life is consumed with grief and my years with groaning; my iniquity has drained my strength, and my bones are wasting away.


## Psalms 31:11 (id: 119031011)

11Among all my enemies I am a disgrace, and among my neighbors even more. I am dreaded by my friends—they flee when they see me on the street.


## Psalms 31:12 (id: 119031012)

12I am forgotten like a dead man, out of mind. I am like a broken vessel.


## Psalms 31:13 (id: 119031013)

13For I hear the slander of many; there is terror on every side. They conspire against me and plot to take my life.


## Psalms 31:14 (id: 119031014)

14But I trust in You, O LORD; I say, “You are my God.”


## Psalms 31:15 (id: 119031015)

15My times are in Your hands; deliver me from my enemies and from those who pursue me.


## Psalms 31:16 (id: 119031016)

16Make Your face shine on Your servant; save me by Your loving devotion.


## Psalms 31:17 (id: 119031017)

17O LORD, let me not be ashamed, for I have called on You. Let the wicked be put to shame; let them lie silent in Sheol.


## Psalms 31:18 (id: 119031018)

18May lying lips be silenced—lips that speak with arrogance against the righteous, full of pride and contempt.


## Psalms 31:19 (id: 119031019)

19How great is Your goodness which You have laid up for those who fear You, which You have bestowed before the sons of men on those who take refuge in You!


## Psalms 31:20 (id: 119031020)

20You hide them in the secret place of Your presence from the schemes of men. You conceal them in Your shelter from accusing tongues.


## Psalms 31:21 (id: 119031021)

21Blessed be the LORD, for He has shown me His loving devotion in a city under siege.


## Psalms 31:22 (id: 119031022)

22In my alarm I said, “I am cut off from Your sight!” But You heard my plea for mercy when I called to You for help.


## Psalms 31:23 (id: 119031023)

23Love the LORD, all His saints. The LORD preserves the faithful, but fully repays the arrogant.


## Psalms 31:24 (id: 119031024)

24Be strong and courageous, all you who hope in the LORD.


## Psalms 32:0 (id: 119032000)

0Of David. A Maskil.


## Psalms 32:1 (id: 119032001)

1Blessed is he whose transgressions are forgiven, whose sins are covered.


## Psalms 32:2 (id: 119032002)

2Blessed is the man whose iniquity the LORD does not count against him, in whose spirit there is no deceit.


## Psalms 32:3 (id: 119032003)

3When I kept silent, my bones became brittle from my groaning all day long.


## Psalms 32:4 (id: 119032004)

4For day and night Your hand was heavy upon me; my strength was drained as in the summer heat. Selah


## Psalms 32:5 (id: 119032005)

5Then I acknowledged my sin to You and did not hide my iniquity. I said, “I will confess my transgressions to the LORD,” and You forgave the guilt of my sin. Selah


## Psalms 32:6 (id: 119032006)

6Therefore let all the godly pray to You while You may be found. Surely when great waters rise, they will not come near.


## Psalms 32:7 (id: 119032007)

7You are my hiding place. You protect me from trouble; You surround me with songs of deliverance. Selah


## Psalms 32:8 (id: 119032008)

8I will instruct you and teach you the way you should go; I will give you counsel and watch over you.


## Psalms 32:9 (id: 119032009)

9Do not be like the horse or mule, which have no understanding; they must be controlled with bit and bridle to make them come to you.


## Psalms 32:10 (id: 119032010)

10Many are the sorrows of the wicked, but loving devotion surrounds him who trusts in the LORD.


## Psalms 32:11 (id: 119032011)

11Be glad in the LORD and rejoice, O righteous ones; shout for joy, all you upright in heart.


## Psalms 33:1 (id: 119033001)

1Rejoice in the LORD, O righteous ones; it is fitting for the upright to praise Him.


## Psalms 33:2 (id: 119033002)

2Praise the LORD with the harp; make music to Him with ten strings.


## Psalms 33:3 (id: 119033003)

3Sing to Him a new song; play skillfully with a shout of joy.


## Psalms 33:4 (id: 119033004)

4For the word of the LORD is upright, and all His work is trustworthy.


## Psalms 33:5 (id: 119033005)

5The LORD loves righteousness and justice; the earth is full of His loving devotion.


## Psalms 33:6 (id: 119033006)

6By the word of the LORD the heavens were made, and all the stars by the breath of His mouth.


## Psalms 33:7 (id: 119033007)

7He piles up the waters of the sea; He puts the depths into storehouses.


## Psalms 33:8 (id: 119033008)

8Let all the earth fear the LORD; let all the people of the world revere Him.


## Psalms 33:9 (id: 119033009)

9For He spoke, and it came to be; He commanded, and it stood firm.


## Psalms 33:10 (id: 119033010)

10The LORD frustrates the plans of the nations; He thwarts the devices of the peoples.


## Psalms 33:11 (id: 119033011)

11The counsel of the LORD stands forever, the purposes of His heart to all generations.


## Psalms 33:12 (id: 119033012)

12Blessed is the nation whose God is the LORD, the people He has chosen as His inheritance!


## Psalms 33:13 (id: 119033013)

13The LORD looks down from heaven; He sees all the sons of men.


## Psalms 33:14 (id: 119033014)

14From His dwelling place He gazes on all who inhabit the earth.


## Psalms 33:15 (id: 119033015)

15He shapes the hearts of each; He considers all their works.


## Psalms 33:16 (id: 119033016)

16No king is saved by his vast army; no warrior is delivered by his great strength.


## Psalms 33:17 (id: 119033017)

17A horse is a vain hope for salvation; even its great strength cannot save.


## Psalms 33:18 (id: 119033018)

18Surely the eyes of the LORD are on those who fear Him, on those whose hope is in His loving devotion


## Psalms 33:19 (id: 119033019)

19to deliver them from death and keep them alive in famine.


## Psalms 33:20 (id: 119033020)

20Our soul waits for the LORD; He is our help and our shield.


## Psalms 33:21 (id: 119033021)

21For our hearts rejoice in Him, since we trust in His holy name.


## Psalms 33:22 (id: 119033022)

22May Your loving devotion rest on us, O LORD, as we put our hope in You.


## Psalms 34:0 (id: 119034000)

0Of David, when he pretended to be insane before Abimelech, so that the king drove him away.


## Psalms 34:1 (id: 119034001)

1I will bless the LORD at all times; His praise will always be on my lips.


## Psalms 34:2 (id: 119034002)

2My soul boasts in the LORD; let the oppressed hear and rejoice.


## Psalms 34:3 (id: 119034003)

3Magnify the LORD with me; let us exalt His name together.


## Psalms 34:4 (id: 119034004)

4I sought the LORD, and He answered me; He delivered me from all my fears.


## Psalms 34:5 (id: 119034005)

5Those who look to Him are radiant with joy; their faces shall never be ashamed.


## Psalms 34:6 (id: 119034006)

6This poor man called out, and the LORD heard him; He saved him from all his troubles.


## Psalms 34:7 (id: 119034007)

7The angel of the LORD encamps around those who fear Him, and he delivers them.


## Psalms 34:8 (id: 119034008)

8Taste and see that the LORD is good; blessed is the man who takes refuge in Him!


## Psalms 34:9 (id: 119034009)

9Fear the LORD, you His saints, for those who fear Him lack nothing.


## Psalms 34:10 (id: 119034010)

10Young lions go lacking and hungry, but those who seek the LORD lack no good thing.


## Psalms 34:11 (id: 119034011)

11Come, children, listen to me; I will teach you the fear of the LORD.


## Psalms 34:12 (id: 119034012)

12Who is the man who delights in life, who desires to see good days?


## Psalms 34:13 (id: 119034013)

13Keep your tongue from evil and your lips from deceitful speech.


## Psalms 34:14 (id: 119034014)

14Turn away from evil and do good; seek peace and pursue it.


## Psalms 34:15 (id: 119034015)

15The eyes of the LORD are on the righteous, and His ears are inclined to their cry.


## Psalms 34:16 (id: 119034016)

16But the face of the LORD is against those who do evil, to wipe out all memory of them from the earth.


## Psalms 34:17 (id: 119034017)

17The righteous cry out, and the LORD hears; He delivers them from all their troubles.


## Psalms 34:18 (id: 119034018)

18The LORD is near to the brokenhearted; He saves the contrite in spirit.


## Psalms 34:19 (id: 119034019)

19Many are the afflictions of the righteous, but the LORD delivers him from them all.


## Psalms 34:20 (id: 119034020)

20He protects all his bones; not one of them will be broken.


## Psalms 34:21 (id: 119034021)

21Evil will slay the wicked, and the haters of the righteous will be condemned.


## Psalms 34:22 (id: 119034022)

22The LORD redeems His servants, and none who take refuge in Him will be condemned.


## Psalms 35:0 (id: 119035000)

0Of David.


## Psalms 35:1 (id: 119035001)

1Contend with my opponents, O LORD; fight against those who fight against me.


## Psalms 35:2 (id: 119035002)

2Take up Your shield and buckler; arise and come to my aid.


## Psalms 35:3 (id: 119035003)

3Draw the spear and javelin against my pursuers; say to my soul: “I am your salvation.”


## Psalms 35:4 (id: 119035004)

4May those who seek my life be disgraced and put to shame; may those who plan to harm me be driven back and confounded.


## Psalms 35:5 (id: 119035005)

5May they be like chaff in the wind, as the angel of the LORD drives them away.


## Psalms 35:6 (id: 119035006)

6May their path be dark and slick, as the angel of the LORD pursues.


## Psalms 35:7 (id: 119035007)

7For without cause they laid their net for me; without reason they dug a pit for my soul.


## Psalms 35:8 (id: 119035008)

8May ruin befall them by surprise; may the net they hid ensnare them; may they fall into the hazard they created.


## Psalms 35:9 (id: 119035009)

9Then my soul will rejoice in the LORD and exult in His salvation.


## Psalms 35:10 (id: 119035010)

10All my bones will exclaim, “Who is like You, O LORD, who delivers the afflicted from the aggressor, the poor and needy from the robber?”


## Psalms 35:11 (id: 119035011)

11Hostile witnesses come forward; they make charges I know nothing about.


## Psalms 35:12 (id: 119035012)

12They repay me evil for good, to the bereavement of my soul.


## Psalms 35:13 (id: 119035013)

13Yet when they were ill, I put on sackcloth; I humbled myself with fasting, but my prayers returned unanswered.


## Psalms 35:14 (id: 119035014)

14I paced about as for my friend or brother; I was bowed down with grief, like one mourning for his mother.


## Psalms 35:15 (id: 119035015)

15But when I stumbled, they assembled in glee; they gathered together against me. Assailants I did not know slandered me without ceasing.


## Psalms 35:16 (id: 119035016)

16Like godless jesters at a feast, they gnashed their teeth at me.


## Psalms 35:17 (id: 119035017)

17How long, O Lord, will You look on? Rescue my soul from their ravages, my precious life from these lions.


## Psalms 35:18 (id: 119035018)

18Then I will give You thanks in the great assembly; I will praise You among many people.


## Psalms 35:19 (id: 119035019)

19Let not my enemies gloat over me without cause, nor those who hate me without reason wink in malice.


## Psalms 35:20 (id: 119035020)

20For they do not speak peace, but they devise deceitful schemes against those who live quietly in the land.


## Psalms 35:21 (id: 119035021)

21They gape at me and say, “Aha, aha! Our eyes have seen!”


## Psalms 35:22 (id: 119035022)

22O LORD, You have seen it; be not silent. O Lord, be not far from me.


## Psalms 35:23 (id: 119035023)

23Awake and rise to my defense, to my cause, my God and my Lord!


## Psalms 35:24 (id: 119035024)

24Vindicate me by Your righteousness, O LORD my God, and do not let them gloat over me.


## Psalms 35:25 (id: 119035025)

25Let them not say in their hearts, “Aha, just what we wanted!” Let them not say, “We have swallowed him up!”


## Psalms 35:26 (id: 119035026)

26May those who gloat in my distress be ashamed and confounded; may those who exalt themselves over me be clothed in shame and reproach.


## Psalms 35:27 (id: 119035027)

27May those who favor my vindication shout for joy and gladness; may they always say, “Exalted be the LORD who delights in His servant’s well\-being.”


## Psalms 35:28 (id: 119035028)

28Then my tongue will proclaim Your righteousness and Your praises all day long.


## Psalms 36:0 (id: 119036000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David, the servant of the LORD.


## Psalms 36:1 (id: 119036001)

1An oracle is in my heart regarding the transgression of the wicked man: There is no fear of God before his eyes.


## Psalms 36:2 (id: 119036002)

2For his eyes are too full of conceit to detect or hate his own sin.


## Psalms 36:3 (id: 119036003)

3The words of his mouth are wicked and deceitful; he has ceased to be wise and well\-doing.


## Psalms 36:4 (id: 119036004)

4Even on his bed he plots wickedness; he sets himself on a path that is not good; he fails to reject evil.


## Psalms 36:5 (id: 119036005)

5Your loving devotion, O LORD, reaches to the heavens, Your faithfulness to the clouds.


## Psalms 36:6 (id: 119036006)

6Your righteousness is like the highest mountains; Your judgments are like the deepest sea. O LORD, You preserve man and beast.


## Psalms 36:7 (id: 119036007)

7How precious is Your loving devotion, O God, that the children of men take refuge in the shadow of Your wings!


## Psalms 36:8 (id: 119036008)

8They feast on the abundance of Your house, and You give them drink from Your river of delights.


## Psalms 36:9 (id: 119036009)

9For with You is the fountain of life; in Your light we see light.


## Psalms 36:10 (id: 119036010)

10Extend Your loving devotion to those who know You, and Your righteousness to the upright in heart.


## Psalms 36:11 (id: 119036011)

11Let not the foot of the proud come against me, nor the hand of the wicked drive me away.


## Psalms 36:12 (id: 119036012)

12There the evildoers lie fallen, thrown down and unable to rise.


## Psalms 37:0 (id: 119037000)

0Of David.


## Psalms 37:1 (id: 119037001)

1Do not fret over those who do evil; do not envy those who do wrong.


## Psalms 37:2 (id: 119037002)

2For they wither quickly like grass and wilt like tender plants.


## Psalms 37:3 (id: 119037003)

3Trust in the LORD and do good; dwell in the land and cultivate faithfulness.


## Psalms 37:4 (id: 119037004)

4Delight yourself in the LORD, and He will give you the desires of your heart.


## Psalms 37:5 (id: 119037005)

5Commit your way to the LORD; trust in Him, and He will do it.


## Psalms 37:6 (id: 119037006)

6He will bring forth your righteousness like the dawn, your justice like the noonday sun.


## Psalms 37:7 (id: 119037007)

7Be still before the LORD and wait patiently for Him; do not fret when men prosper in their ways, when they carry out wicked schemes.


## Psalms 37:8 (id: 119037008)

8Refrain from anger and abandon wrath; do not fret—it can only bring harm.


## Psalms 37:9 (id: 119037009)

9For the evildoers will be cut off, but those who hope in the LORD will inherit the land.


## Psalms 37:10 (id: 119037010)

10Yet a little while, and the wicked will be no more; though you look for them, they will not be found.


## Psalms 37:11 (id: 119037011)

11But the meek will inherit the land and delight in abundant prosperity.


## Psalms 37:12 (id: 119037012)

12The wicked scheme against the righteous and gnash their teeth at them,


## Psalms 37:13 (id: 119037013)

13but the Lord laughs, seeing that their day is coming.


## Psalms 37:14 (id: 119037014)

14The wicked have drawn the sword and bent the bow to bring down the poor and needy, to slay those whose ways are upright.


## Psalms 37:15 (id: 119037015)

15But their swords will pierce their own hearts, and their bows will be broken.


## Psalms 37:16 (id: 119037016)

16Better is the little of the righteous than the abundance of many who are wicked.


## Psalms 37:17 (id: 119037017)

17For the arms of the wicked will be broken, but the LORD upholds the righteous.


## Psalms 37:18 (id: 119037018)

18The LORD knows the days of the blameless, and their inheritance will last forever.


## Psalms 37:19 (id: 119037019)

19In the time of evil they will not be ashamed, and in the days of famine they will be satisfied.


## Psalms 37:20 (id: 119037020)

20But the wicked and enemies of the LORD will perish like the glory of the fields. They will vanish; like smoke they will fade away.


## Psalms 37:21 (id: 119037021)

21The wicked borrow and do not repay, but the righteous are gracious and giving.


## Psalms 37:22 (id: 119037022)

22Surely those He blesses will inherit the land, but the cursed will be destroyed.


## Psalms 37:23 (id: 119037023)

23The steps of a man are ordered by the LORD who takes delight in his journey.


## Psalms 37:24 (id: 119037024)

24Though he falls, he will not be overwhelmed, for the LORD is holding his hand.


## Psalms 37:25 (id: 119037025)

25I once was young and now am old, yet never have I seen the righteous abandoned or their children begging for bread.


## Psalms 37:26 (id: 119037026)

26They are ever generous and quick to lend, and their children are a blessing.


## Psalms 37:27 (id: 119037027)

27Turn away from evil and do good, so that you will abide forever.


## Psalms 37:28 (id: 119037028)

28For the LORD loves justice and will not forsake His saints. They are preserved forever, but the offspring of the wicked will be cut off.


## Psalms 37:29 (id: 119037029)

29The righteous will inherit the land and dwell in it forever.


## Psalms 37:30 (id: 119037030)

30The mouth of the righteous man utters wisdom, and his tongue speaks justice.


## Psalms 37:31 (id: 119037031)

31The law of his God is in his heart; his steps do not falter.


## Psalms 37:32 (id: 119037032)

32Though the wicked lie in wait for the righteous, and seek to slay them,


## Psalms 37:33 (id: 119037033)

33the LORD will not leave them in their power or let them be condemned under judgment.


## Psalms 37:34 (id: 119037034)

34Wait for the LORD and keep His way, and He will raise you up to inherit the land. When the wicked are cut off, you will see it.


## Psalms 37:35 (id: 119037035)

35I have seen a wicked, ruthless man flourishing like a well\-rooted native tree,


## Psalms 37:36 (id: 119037036)

36yet he passed away and was no more; though I searched, he could not be found.


## Psalms 37:37 (id: 119037037)

37Consider the blameless and observe the upright, for posterity awaits the man of peace.


## Psalms 37:38 (id: 119037038)

38But the transgressors will all be destroyed; the future of the wicked will be cut off.


## Psalms 37:39 (id: 119037039)

39The salvation of the righteous is from the LORD; He is their stronghold in time of trouble.


## Psalms 37:40 (id: 119037040)

40The LORD helps and delivers them; He rescues and saves them from the wicked, because they take refuge in Him.


## Psalms 38:0 (id: 119038000)

0A Psalm of David, for remembrance.


## Psalms 38:1 (id: 119038001)

1O LORD, do not rebuke me in Your anger or discipline me in Your wrath.


## Psalms 38:2 (id: 119038002)

2For Your arrows have pierced me deeply, and Your hand has pressed down on me.


## Psalms 38:3 (id: 119038003)

3There is no soundness in my body because of Your anger; there is no rest in my bones because of my sin.


## Psalms 38:4 (id: 119038004)

4For my iniquities have overwhelmed me; they are a burden too heavy to bear.


## Psalms 38:5 (id: 119038005)

5My wounds are foul and festering because of my sinful folly.


## Psalms 38:6 (id: 119038006)

6I am bent and brought low; all day long I go about mourning.


## Psalms 38:7 (id: 119038007)

7For my loins are full of burning pain, and no soundness remains in my body.


## Psalms 38:8 (id: 119038008)

8I am numb and badly crushed; I groan in anguish of heart.


## Psalms 38:9 (id: 119038009)

9O Lord, my every desire is before You; my groaning is not hidden from You.


## Psalms 38:10 (id: 119038010)

10My heart pounds, my strength fails, and even the light of my eyes has faded.


## Psalms 38:11 (id: 119038011)

11My beloved and friends shun my disease, and my kinsmen stand at a distance.


## Psalms 38:12 (id: 119038012)

12Those who seek my life lay snares; those who wish me harm speak destruction, plotting deceit all day long.


## Psalms 38:13 (id: 119038013)

13But like a deaf man, I do not hear; and like a mute man, I do not open my mouth.


## Psalms 38:14 (id: 119038014)

14I am like a man who cannot hear, whose mouth offers no reply.


## Psalms 38:15 (id: 119038015)

15I wait for You, O LORD; You will answer, O Lord my God.


## Psalms 38:16 (id: 119038016)

16For I said, “Let them not gloat over me—those who taunt me when my foot slips.”


## Psalms 38:17 (id: 119038017)

17For I am ready to fall, and my pain is ever with me.


## Psalms 38:18 (id: 119038018)

18Yes, I confess my iniquity; I am troubled by my sin.


## Psalms 38:19 (id: 119038019)

19Many are my enemies without cause, and many hate me without reason.


## Psalms 38:20 (id: 119038020)

20Those who repay my good with evil attack me for pursuing the good.


## Psalms 38:21 (id: 119038021)

21Do not forsake me, O LORD; be not far from me, O my God.


## Psalms 38:22 (id: 119038022)

22Come quickly to help me, O Lord my Savior.


## Psalms 39:0 (id: 119039000)

0For the choirmaster. For Jeduthun. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 39:1 (id: 119039001)

1I said, “I will watch my ways so that I will not sin with my tongue; I will guard my mouth with a muzzle as long as the wicked are present.”


## Psalms 39:2 (id: 119039002)

2I was speechless and still; I remained silent, even from speaking good, and my sorrow was stirred.


## Psalms 39:3 (id: 119039003)

3My heart grew hot within me; as I mused, the fire burned. Then I spoke with my tongue:


## Psalms 39:4 (id: 119039004)

4“Show me, O LORD, my end and the measure of my days. Let me know how fleeting my life is.


## Psalms 39:5 (id: 119039005)

5You, indeed, have made my days as handbreadths, and my lifetime as nothing before You. Truly each man at his best exists as but a breath. Selah


## Psalms 39:6 (id: 119039006)

6Surely every man goes about like a phantom; surely he bustles in vain; he heaps up riches not knowing who will haul them away.


## Psalms 39:7 (id: 119039007)

7And now, O Lord, for what do I wait? My hope is in You.


## Psalms 39:8 (id: 119039008)

8Deliver me from all my transgressions; do not make me the reproach of fools.


## Psalms 39:9 (id: 119039009)

9I have become mute; I do not open my mouth because of what You have done.


## Psalms 39:10 (id: 119039010)

10Remove Your scourge from me; I am perishing by the force of Your hand.


## Psalms 39:11 (id: 119039011)

11You discipline and correct a man for his iniquity, consuming like a moth what he holds dear; surely each man is but a vapor. Selah


## Psalms 39:12 (id: 119039012)

12Hear my prayer, O LORD, and give ear to my cry for help; do not be deaf to my weeping. For I am a foreigner dwelling with You, a stranger like all my fathers.


## Psalms 39:13 (id: 119039013)

13Turn Your gaze away from me, that I may again be cheered before I depart and am no more.”


## Psalms 40:0 (id: 119040000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 40:1 (id: 119040001)

1I waited patiently for the LORD; He inclined to me and heard my cry.


## Psalms 40:2 (id: 119040002)

2He lifted me up from the pit of despair, out of the miry clay; He set my feet upon a rock, and made my footsteps firm.


## Psalms 40:3 (id: 119040003)

3He put a new song in my mouth, a hymn of praise to our God. Many will see and fear and put their trust in the LORD.


## Psalms 40:4 (id: 119040004)

4Blessed is the man who has made the LORD his trust, who has not turned to the proud, nor to those who lapse into falsehood.


## Psalms 40:5 (id: 119040005)

5Many, O LORD my God, are the wonders You have done, and the plans You have for us—none can compare to You—if I proclaim and declare them, they are more than I can count.


## Psalms 40:6 (id: 119040006)

6Sacrifice and offering You did not desire, but my ears You have opened. Burnt offerings and sin offerings You did not require.


## Psalms 40:7 (id: 119040007)

7Then I said, “Here I am, I have come—it is written about me in the scroll:


## Psalms 40:8 (id: 119040008)

8I delight to do Your will, O my God; Your law is within my heart.”


## Psalms 40:9 (id: 119040009)

9I proclaim righteousness in the great assembly; behold, I do not seal my lips, as You, O LORD, do know.


## Psalms 40:10 (id: 119040010)

10I have not covered up Your righteousness in my heart; I have declared Your faithfulness and salvation; I have not concealed Your loving devotion and faithfulness from the great assembly.


## Psalms 40:11 (id: 119040011)

11O LORD, do not withhold Your mercy from me; Your loving devotion and faithfulness will always guard me.


## Psalms 40:12 (id: 119040012)

12For evils without number surround me; my sins have overtaken me, so that I cannot see. They are more than the hairs of my head, and my heart has failed within me.


## Psalms 40:13 (id: 119040013)

13Be pleased, O LORD, to deliver me; hurry, O LORD, to help me.


## Psalms 40:14 (id: 119040014)

14May those who seek my life be ashamed and confounded; may those who wish me harm be repelled and humiliated.


## Psalms 40:15 (id: 119040015)

15May those who say to me, “Aha, aha!” be appalled at their own shame.


## Psalms 40:16 (id: 119040016)

16May all who seek You rejoice and be glad in You; may those who love Your salvation always say, “The LORD be magnified!”


## Psalms 40:17 (id: 119040017)

17But I am poor and needy; may the Lord think of me. You are my helper and deliverer; O my God, do not delay.


## Psalms 41:0 (id: 119041000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 41:1 (id: 119041001)

1Blessed is the one who cares for the poor; the LORD will deliver him in the day of trouble.


## Psalms 41:2 (id: 119041002)

2The LORD will protect and preserve him; He will bless him in the land and refuse to give him over to the will of his foes.


## Psalms 41:3 (id: 119041003)

3The LORD will sustain him on his bed of illness and restore him from his bed of sickness.


## Psalms 41:4 (id: 119041004)

4I said, “O LORD, be gracious to me; heal me, for I have sinned against You.”


## Psalms 41:5 (id: 119041005)

5My enemies say with malice: “When will he die and be forgotten?”


## Psalms 41:6 (id: 119041006)

6My visitor speaks falsehood; he gathers slander in his heart; he goes out and spreads it abroad.


## Psalms 41:7 (id: 119041007)

7All who hate me whisper against me; they imagine the worst for me:


## Psalms 41:8 (id: 119041008)

8“A vile disease has been poured into him; he will never get up from where he lies!”


## Psalms 41:9 (id: 119041009)

9Even my close friend whom I trusted, the one who shared my bread, has lifted up his heel against me.


## Psalms 41:10 (id: 119041010)

10But You, O LORD, be gracious to me and raise me up, that I may repay them.


## Psalms 41:11 (id: 119041011)

11By this I know that You delight in me, for my enemy does not triumph over me.


## Psalms 41:12 (id: 119041012)

12In my integrity You uphold me and set me in Your presence forever.


## Psalms 41:13 (id: 119041013)

13Blessed be the LORD, the God of Israel, from everlasting to everlasting. Amen and Amen.


## Psalms 42:0 (id: 119042000)

0For the choirmaster. A Maskil of the sons of Korah.


## Psalms 42:1 (id: 119042001)

1As the deer pants for streams of water, so my soul longs after You, O God.


## Psalms 42:2 (id: 119042002)

2My soul thirsts for God, the living God. When shall I come and appear in God’s presence?


## Psalms 42:3 (id: 119042003)

3My tears have been my food both day and night, while men ask me all day long, “Where is your God?”


## Psalms 42:4 (id: 119042004)

4These things come to mind as I pour out my soul: how I walked with the multitude, leading the festive procession to the house of God with shouts of joy and praise.


## Psalms 42:5 (id: 119042005)

5Why are you downcast, O my soul? Why the unease within me? Put your hope in God, for I will yet praise Him for the salvation of His presence.


## Psalms 42:6 (id: 119042006)

6O my God, my soul despairs within me. Therefore I remember You from the land of Jordan and the peaks of Hermon—even from Mount Mizar.


## Psalms 42:7 (id: 119042007)

7Deep calls to deep in the roar of Your waterfalls; all Your breakers and waves have rolled over me.


## Psalms 42:8 (id: 119042008)

8The LORD decrees His loving devotion by day, and at night His song is with me as a prayer to the God of my life.


## Psalms 42:9 (id: 119042009)

9I say to God my Rock, “Why have You forgotten me? Why must I walk in sorrow because of the enemy’s oppression?”


## Psalms 42:10 (id: 119042010)

10Like the crushing of my bones, my enemies taunt me, while they say to me all day long, “Where is your God?”


## Psalms 42:11 (id: 119042011)

11Why are you downcast, O my soul? Why the unease within me? Put your hope in God, for I will yet praise Him, my Savior and my God.


## Psalms 43:1 (id: 119043001)

1Vindicate me, O God, and plead my case against an ungodly nation; deliver me from deceitful and unjust men.


## Psalms 43:2 (id: 119043002)

2For You are the God of my refuge. Why have You rejected me? Why must I walk in sorrow because of the enemy’s oppression?


## Psalms 43:3 (id: 119043003)

3Send out Your light and Your truth; let them lead me. Let them bring me to Your holy mountain and to the place where You dwell.


## Psalms 43:4 (id: 119043004)

4Then I will go to the altar of God, to God, my greatest joy. I will praise You with the harp, O God, my God.


## Psalms 43:5 (id: 119043005)

5Why are you downcast, O my soul? Why the unease within me? Put your hope in God, for I will yet praise Him, my Savior and my God.


## Psalms 44:0 (id: 119044000)

0For the choirmaster. A Maskil of the sons of Korah.


## Psalms 44:1 (id: 119044001)

1We have heard with our ears, O God; our fathers have told us the work You did in their days, in the days of old.


## Psalms 44:2 (id: 119044002)

2With Your hand You drove out the nations and planted our fathers there; You crushed the peoples and cast them out.


## Psalms 44:3 (id: 119044003)

3For it was not by their sword that they took the land; their arm did not bring them victory. It was by Your right hand, Your arm, and the light of Your face, because You favored them.


## Psalms 44:4 (id: 119044004)

4You are my King, O God, who ordains victories for Jacob.


## Psalms 44:5 (id: 119044005)

5Through You we repel our foes; through Your name we trample our enemies.


## Psalms 44:6 (id: 119044006)

6For I do not trust in my bow, nor does my sword save me.


## Psalms 44:7 (id: 119044007)

7For You save us from our enemies; You put those who hate us to shame.


## Psalms 44:8 (id: 119044008)

8In God we have boasted all day long, and Your name we will praise forever. Selah


## Psalms 44:9 (id: 119044009)

9But You have rejected and humbled us; You no longer go forth with our armies.


## Psalms 44:10 (id: 119044010)

10You have made us retreat from the foe, and those who hate us have plundered us.


## Psalms 44:11 (id: 119044011)

11You have given us up as sheep to be devoured; You have scattered us among the nations.


## Psalms 44:12 (id: 119044012)

12You sell Your people for nothing; no profit do You gain from their sale.


## Psalms 44:13 (id: 119044013)

13You have made us a reproach to our neighbors, a mockery and derision to those around us.


## Psalms 44:14 (id: 119044014)

14You have made us a byword among the nations, a laughingstock among the peoples.


## Psalms 44:15 (id: 119044015)

15All day long my disgrace is before me, and shame has covered my face,


## Psalms 44:16 (id: 119044016)

16at the voice of the scorner and reviler, because of the enemy, bent on revenge.


## Psalms 44:17 (id: 119044017)

17All this has come upon us, though we have not forgotten You or betrayed Your covenant.


## Psalms 44:18 (id: 119044018)

18Our hearts have not turned back; our steps have not strayed from Your path.


## Psalms 44:19 (id: 119044019)

19But You have crushed us in the lair of jackals; You have covered us with deepest darkness.


## Psalms 44:20 (id: 119044020)

20If we had forgotten the name of our God or spread out our hands to a foreign god,


## Psalms 44:21 (id: 119044021)

21would not God have discovered, since He knows the secrets of the heart?


## Psalms 44:22 (id: 119044022)

22Yet for Your sake we face death all day long; we are considered as sheep to be slaughtered.


## Psalms 44:23 (id: 119044023)

23Wake up, O Lord! Why are You sleeping? Arise! Do not reject us forever.


## Psalms 44:24 (id: 119044024)

24Why do You hide Your face and forget our affliction and oppression?


## Psalms 44:25 (id: 119044025)

25For our soul has sunk to the dust; our bodies cling to the earth.


## Psalms 44:26 (id: 119044026)

26Rise up; be our help! Redeem us on account of Your loving devotion.


## Psalms 45:0 (id: 119045000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “The Lilies.” A Maskil of the sons of Korah. A love song.


## Psalms 45:1 (id: 119045001)

1My heart is stirred by a noble theme as I recite my verses to the king; my tongue is the pen of a skillful writer.


## Psalms 45:2 (id: 119045002)

2You are the most handsome of men; grace has anointed your lips; therefore God has blessed you forever.


## Psalms 45:3 (id: 119045003)

3Strap your sword at your side, O mighty warrior; appear in your majesty and splendor.


## Psalms 45:4 (id: 119045004)

4In your splendor ride forth in victory on behalf of truth and humility and justice; may your right hand show your awesome deeds.


## Psalms 45:5 (id: 119045005)

5Your arrows pierce the hearts of the king’s foes; the nations fall beneath your feet.


## Psalms 45:6 (id: 119045006)

6Your throne, O God, endures forever and ever, and justice is the scepter of Your kingdom.


## Psalms 45:7 (id: 119045007)

7You have loved righteousness and hated wickedness; therefore God, your God, has anointed you above your companions with the oil of joy.


## Psalms 45:8 (id: 119045008)

8All your garments are fragrant with myrrh and aloes and cassia; from palaces of ivory the harps make you glad.


## Psalms 45:9 (id: 119045009)

9The daughters of kings are among your honored women; the queen stands at your right hand, adorned with the gold of Ophir.


## Psalms 45:10 (id: 119045010)

10Listen, O daughter! Consider and incline your ear: Forget your people and your father’s house,


## Psalms 45:11 (id: 119045011)

11and the king will desire your beauty; bow to him, for he is your lord.


## Psalms 45:12 (id: 119045012)

12The Daughter of Tyre will come with a gift; men of wealth will seek your favor.


## Psalms 45:13 (id: 119045013)

13All glorious is the princess in her chamber; her gown is embroidered with gold.


## Psalms 45:14 (id: 119045014)

14In colorful garments she is led to the king; her virgin companions are brought before you.


## Psalms 45:15 (id: 119045015)

15They are led in with joy and gladness; they enter the palace of the king.


## Psalms 45:16 (id: 119045016)

16Your sons will succeed your fathers; you will make them princes throughout the land.


## Psalms 45:17 (id: 119045017)

17I will commemorate your name through all generations; therefore the nations will praise you forever and ever.

0For the choirmaster. Of the sons of Korah. According to Alamoth. A song.


## Psalms 46:1 (id: 119046001)

1God is our refuge and strength, an ever\-present help in times of trouble.


## Psalms 46:2 (id: 119046002)

2Therefore we will not fear, though the earth is transformed and the mountains are toppled into the depths of the seas,


## Psalms 46:3 (id: 119046003)

3though their waters roar and foam and the mountains quake in the surge. Selah


## Psalms 46:4 (id: 119046004)

4There is a river whose streams delight the city of God, the holy place where the Most High dwells.


## Psalms 46:5 (id: 119046005)

5God is within her; she will not be moved. God will help her when morning dawns.


## Psalms 46:6 (id: 119046006)

6Nations rage, kingdoms crumble; the earth melts when He lifts His voice.


## Psalms 46:7 (id: 119046007)

7The LORD of Hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our fortress. Selah


## Psalms 46:8 (id: 119046008)

8Come, see the works of the LORD, who brings devastation upon the earth.


## Psalms 46:9 (id: 119046009)

9He makes wars to cease throughout the earth; He breaks the bow and shatters the spear; He burns the shields in the fire.


## Psalms 46:10 (id: 119046010)

10“Be still and know that I am God; I will be exalted among the nations, I will be exalted over the earth.”


## Psalms 46:11 (id: 119046011)

11The LORD of Hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our fortress. Selah


## Psalms 47:0 (id: 119047000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of the sons of Korah.


## Psalms 47:1 (id: 119047001)

1Clap your hands, all you peoples; shout unto God with a voice of triumph.


## Psalms 47:2 (id: 119047002)

2How awesome is the LORD Most High, the great King over all the earth!


## Psalms 47:3 (id: 119047003)

3He subdues nations beneath us, and peoples under our feet.


## Psalms 47:4 (id: 119047004)

4He chooses our inheritance for us, the pride of Jacob, whom He loves. Selah


## Psalms 47:5 (id: 119047005)

5God has ascended amid shouts of joy, the LORD with the sound of the horn.


## Psalms 47:6 (id: 119047006)

6Sing praises to God, sing praises; sing praises to our King, sing praises!


## Psalms 47:7 (id: 119047007)

7For God is King of all the earth; sing to Him a psalm of praise.


## Psalms 47:8 (id: 119047008)

8God reigns over the nations; God is seated on His holy throne.


## Psalms 47:9 (id: 119047009)

9The nobles of the nations have assembled as the people of the God of Abraham; for the shields of the earth belong to God; He is highly exalted.


## Psalms 48:0 (id: 119048000)

0A song. A Psalm of the sons of Korah.


## Psalms 48:1 (id: 119048001)

1Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised in the city of our God, His holy mountain.


## Psalms 48:2 (id: 119048002)

2Beautiful in loftiness, the joy of all the earth, like the peaks of Zaphon is Mount Zion, the city of the great King.


## Psalms 48:3 (id: 119048003)

3God is in her citadels; He has shown Himself to be a fortress.


## Psalms 48:4 (id: 119048004)

4For behold, the kings assembled; they all advanced together.


## Psalms 48:5 (id: 119048005)

5They saw and were astounded; they fled in terror.


## Psalms 48:6 (id: 119048006)

6Trembling seized them there, anguish like a woman in labor.


## Psalms 48:7 (id: 119048007)

7With a wind from the east You wrecked the ships of Tarshish.


## Psalms 48:8 (id: 119048008)

8As we have heard, so we have seen in the city of the LORD of Hosts, in the city of our God: God will establish her forever. Selah


## Psalms 48:9 (id: 119048009)

9Within Your temple, O God, we contemplate Your loving devotion.


## Psalms 48:10 (id: 119048010)

10Your name, O God, like Your praise, reaches to the ends of the earth; Your right hand is full of righteousness.


## Psalms 48:11 (id: 119048011)

11Mount Zion is glad, the daughters of Judah rejoice, on account of Your judgments.


## Psalms 48:12 (id: 119048012)

12March around Zion, encircle her, count her towers,


## Psalms 48:13 (id: 119048013)

13consider her ramparts, tour her citadels, that you may tell the next generation.


## Psalms 48:14 (id: 119048014)

14For this God is our God forever and ever; He will be our guide even till death.


## Psalms 49:0 (id: 119049000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of the sons of Korah.


## Psalms 49:1 (id: 119049001)

1Hear this, all you peoples; listen, all inhabitants of the world,


## Psalms 49:2 (id: 119049002)

2both low and high, rich and poor alike.


## Psalms 49:3 (id: 119049003)

3My mouth will impart wisdom, and the meditation of my heart will bring understanding.


## Psalms 49:4 (id: 119049004)

4I will incline my ear to a proverb; I will express my riddle with the harp:


## Psalms 49:5 (id: 119049005)

5Why should I fear in times of trouble, when wicked usurpers surround me?


## Psalms 49:6 (id: 119049006)

6They trust in their wealth and boast in their great riches.


## Psalms 49:7 (id: 119049007)

7No man can possibly redeem his brother or pay his ransom to God.


## Psalms 49:8 (id: 119049008)

8For the redemption of his soul is costly, and never can payment suffice,


## Psalms 49:9 (id: 119049009)

9that he should live on forever and not see decay.


## Psalms 49:10 (id: 119049010)

10For it is clear that wise men die, and the foolish and the senseless both perish and leave their wealth to others.


## Psalms 49:11 (id: 119049011)

11Their graves are their eternal homes—their dwellings for endless generations—even though their lands were their namesakes.


## Psalms 49:12 (id: 119049012)

12But a man, despite his wealth, cannot endure; he is like the beasts that perish.


## Psalms 49:13 (id: 119049013)

13This is the fate of the foolish and their followers who endorse their sayings. Selah


## Psalms 49:14 (id: 119049014)

14Like sheep they are destined for Sheol. Death will be their shepherd. The upright will rule them in the morning, and their form will decay in Sheol, far from their lofty abode.


## Psalms 49:15 (id: 119049015)

15But God will redeem my life from Sheol, for He will surely take me to Himself. Selah


## Psalms 49:16 (id: 119049016)

16Do not be afraid when a man grows rich, when the splendor of his house increases.


## Psalms 49:17 (id: 119049017)

17For when he dies, he will carry nothing away; his abundance will not follow him down.


## Psalms 49:18 (id: 119049018)

18Though in his lifetime he blesses his soul—and men praise you when you prosper—


## Psalms 49:19 (id: 119049019)

19he will join the generation of his fathers, who will never see the light of day.


## Psalms 49:20 (id: 119049020)

20A man who has riches without understanding is like the beasts that perish.


## Psalms 50:0 (id: 119050000)

0A Psalm of Asaph.


## Psalms 50:1 (id: 119050001)

1The Mighty One, God the LORD, speaks and summons the earth from where the sun rises to where it sets.


## Psalms 50:2 (id: 119050002)

2From Zion, perfect in beauty, God shines forth.


## Psalms 50:3 (id: 119050003)

3Our God approaches and will not be silent! Consuming fire precedes Him, and a tempest rages around Him.


## Psalms 50:4 (id: 119050004)

4He summons the heavens above, and the earth, that He may judge His people:


## Psalms 50:5 (id: 119050005)

5“Gather to Me My saints, who made a covenant with Me by sacrifice.”


## Psalms 50:6 (id: 119050006)

6And the heavens proclaim His righteousness, for God Himself is Judge. Selah


## Psalms 50:7 (id: 119050007)

7“Hear, O My people, and I will speak, O Israel, and I will testify against you: I am God, your God.


## Psalms 50:8 (id: 119050008)

8I do not rebuke you for your sacrifices, and your burnt offerings are ever before Me.


## Psalms 50:9 (id: 119050009)

9I have no need for a bull from your stall or goats from your pens,


## Psalms 50:10 (id: 119050010)

10for every beast of the forest is Mine—the cattle on a thousand hills.


## Psalms 50:11 (id: 119050011)

11I know every bird in the mountains, and the creatures of the field are Mine.


## Psalms 50:12 (id: 119050012)

12If I were hungry, I would not tell you, for the world is Mine, and the fullness thereof.


## Psalms 50:13 (id: 119050013)

13Do I eat the flesh of bulls, or drink the blood of goats?


## Psalms 50:14 (id: 119050014)

14Sacrifice a thank offering to God, and fulfill your vows to the Most High.


## Psalms 50:15 (id: 119050015)

15Call upon Me in the day of trouble; I will deliver you, and you will honor Me.”


## Psalms 50:16 (id: 119050016)

16To the wicked, however, God says, “What right have you to recite My statutes and to bear My covenant on your lips?


## Psalms 50:17 (id: 119050017)

17For you hate My instruction and cast My words behind you.


## Psalms 50:18 (id: 119050018)

18When you see a thief, you befriend him, and throw in your lot with adulterers.


## Psalms 50:19 (id: 119050019)

19You unleash your mouth for evil and harness your tongue to deceit.


## Psalms 50:20 (id: 119050020)

20You sit and malign your brother; you slander your own mother’s son.


## Psalms 50:21 (id: 119050021)

21You have done these things, and I kept silent; you thought I was just like you. But now I rebuke you and accuse you to your face.


## Psalms 50:22 (id: 119050022)

22Now consider this, you who forget God, lest I tear you to pieces, with no one to rescue you:


## Psalms 50:23 (id: 119050023)

23He who sacrifices a thank offering honors Me, and to him who rightly orders his way, I will show the salvation of God.”


## Psalms 51:0 (id: 119051000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David. When Nathan the prophet came to him after his adultery with Bathsheba.


## Psalms 51:1 (id: 119051001)

1Have mercy on me, O God, according to Your loving devotion; according to Your great compassion, blot out my transgressions.


## Psalms 51:2 (id: 119051002)

2Wash me clean of my iniquity and cleanse me from my sin.


## Psalms 51:3 (id: 119051003)

3For I know my transgressions, and my sin is always before me.


## Psalms 51:4 (id: 119051004)

4Against You, You only, have I sinned and done what is evil in Your sight, so that You may be proved right when You speak and blameless when You judge.


## Psalms 51:5 (id: 119051005)

5Surely I was brought forth in iniquity; I was sinful when my mother conceived me.


## Psalms 51:6 (id: 119051006)

6Surely You desire truth in the inmost being; You teach me wisdom in the inmost place.


## Psalms 51:7 (id: 119051007)

7Purify me with hyssop, and I will be clean; wash me, and I will be whiter than snow.


## Psalms 51:8 (id: 119051008)

8Let me hear joy and gladness; let the bones You have crushed rejoice.


## Psalms 51:9 (id: 119051009)

9Hide Your face from my sins and blot out all my iniquities.


## Psalms 51:10 (id: 119051010)

10Create in me a clean heart, O God, and renew a right spirit within me.


## Psalms 51:11 (id: 119051011)

11Cast me not away from Your presence; take not Your Holy Spirit from me.


## Psalms 51:12 (id: 119051012)

12Restore to me the joy of Your salvation, and sustain me with a willing spirit.


## Psalms 51:13 (id: 119051013)

13Then I will teach transgressors Your ways, and sinners will return to You.


## Psalms 51:14 (id: 119051014)

14Deliver me from bloodguilt, O God, the God of my salvation, and my tongue will sing of Your righteousness.


## Psalms 51:15 (id: 119051015)

15O Lord, open my lips, and my mouth will declare Your praise.


## Psalms 51:16 (id: 119051016)

16For You do not delight in sacrifice, or I would bring it; You take no pleasure in burnt offerings.


## Psalms 51:17 (id: 119051017)

17The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit; a broken and a contrite heart, O God, You will not despise.


## Psalms 51:18 (id: 119051018)

18In Your good pleasure, cause Zion to prosper; build up the walls of Jerusalem.


## Psalms 51:19 (id: 119051019)

19Then You will delight in righteous sacrifices, in whole burnt offerings; then bulls will be offered on Your altar.


## Psalms 52:0 (id: 119052000)

0For the choirmaster. A Maskil of David. After Doeg the Edomite went to Saul and told him, “David has gone to the house of Ahimelech.”


## Psalms 52:1 (id: 119052001)

1Why do you boast of evil, O mighty man? The loving devotion of God endures all day long.


## Psalms 52:2 (id: 119052002)

2Your tongue devises destruction like a sharpened razor, O worker of deceit.


## Psalms 52:3 (id: 119052003)

3You love evil more than good, falsehood more than speaking truth. Selah


## Psalms 52:4 (id: 119052004)

4You love every word that devours, O deceitful tongue.


## Psalms 52:5 (id: 119052005)

5Surely God will bring you down to everlasting ruin; He will snatch you up and tear you away from your tent; He will uproot you from the land of the living. Selah


## Psalms 52:6 (id: 119052006)

6The righteous will see and fear; they will mock the evildoer, saying,


## Psalms 52:7 (id: 119052007)

7“Look at the man who did not make God his refuge, but trusted in the abundance of his wealth and strengthened himself by destruction.”


## Psalms 52:8 (id: 119052008)

8But I am like an olive tree flourishing in the house of God; I trust in the loving devotion of God forever and ever.


## Psalms 52:9 (id: 119052009)

9I will praise You forever, because You have done it. I will wait on Your name—for it is good—in the presence of Your saints.


## Psalms 53:0 (id: 119053000)

0For the choirmaster. According to Mahalath. A Maskil of David.


## Psalms 53:1 (id: 119053001)

1The fool says in his heart, “There is no God.” They are corrupt; their ways are vile. There is no one who does good.


## Psalms 53:2 (id: 119053002)

2God looks down from heaven upon the sons of men to see if any understand, if any seek God.


## Psalms 53:3 (id: 119053003)

3All have turned away, they have together become corrupt; there is no one who does good, not even one.


## Psalms 53:4 (id: 119053004)

4Will the workers of iniquity never learn? They devour my people like bread; they refuse to call upon God.


## Psalms 53:5 (id: 119053005)

5There they are, overwhelmed with dread, where there was nothing to fear. For God has scattered the bones of those who besieged you. You put them to shame, for God has despised them.


## Psalms 53:6 (id: 119053006)

6Oh, that the salvation of Israel would come from Zion! When God restores His captive people, let Jacob rejoice, let Israel be glad!


## Psalms 54:0 (id: 119054000)

0For the choirmaster. With stringed instruments. A Maskil of David. When the Ziphites went to Saul and said, “Is David not hiding among us?”


## Psalms 54:1 (id: 119054001)

1Save me, O God, by Your name, and vindicate me by Your might!


## Psalms 54:2 (id: 119054002)

2Hear my prayer, O God; listen to the words of my mouth.


## Psalms 54:3 (id: 119054003)

3For strangers rise up against me, and ruthless men seek my life—men with no regard for God. Selah


## Psalms 54:4 (id: 119054004)

4Surely God is my helper; the Lord is the sustainer of my soul.


## Psalms 54:5 (id: 119054005)

5He will reward my enemies with evil. In Your faithfulness, destroy them.


## Psalms 54:6 (id: 119054006)

6Freely I will sacrifice to You; I will praise Your name, O LORD, for it is good.


## Psalms 54:7 (id: 119054007)

7For He has delivered me from every trouble, and my eyes have looked in triumph on my foes.


## Psalms 55:0 (id: 119055000)

0For the choirmaster. With stringed instruments. A Maskil of David.


## Psalms 55:1 (id: 119055001)

1Listen to my prayer, O God, and do not ignore my plea.


## Psalms 55:2 (id: 119055002)

2Attend to me and answer me. I am restless in my complaint, and distraught


## Psalms 55:3 (id: 119055003)

3at the voice of the enemy, at the pressure of the wicked. For they bring down disaster upon me and resent me in their anger.


## Psalms 55:4 (id: 119055004)

4My heart pounds within me, and the terrors of death assail me.


## Psalms 55:5 (id: 119055005)

5Fear and trembling grip me, and horror has overwhelmed me.


## Psalms 55:6 (id: 119055006)

6I said, “Oh, that I had wings like a dove! I would fly away and find rest.


## Psalms 55:7 (id: 119055007)

7How far away I would flee! In the wilderness I would remain. Selah


## Psalms 55:8 (id: 119055008)

8I would hurry to my shelter, far from this raging tempest.”


## Psalms 55:9 (id: 119055009)

9O Lord, confuse and confound their speech, for I see violence and strife in the city.


## Psalms 55:10 (id: 119055010)

10Day and night they encircle the walls, while malice and trouble lie within.


## Psalms 55:11 (id: 119055011)

11Destruction is within; oppression and deceit never leave the streets.


## Psalms 55:12 (id: 119055012)

12For it is not an enemy who insults me; that I could endure. It is not a foe who rises against me; from him I could hide.


## Psalms 55:13 (id: 119055013)

13But it is you, a man like myself, my companion and close friend.


## Psalms 55:14 (id: 119055014)

14We shared sweet fellowship together; we walked with the crowd into the house of God.


## Psalms 55:15 (id: 119055015)

15Let death seize them by surprise; let them go down to Sheol alive, for evil is with them in their homes.


## Psalms 55:16 (id: 119055016)

16But I call to God, and the LORD saves me.


## Psalms 55:17 (id: 119055017)

17Morning, noon, and night, I cry out in distress, and He hears my voice.


## Psalms 55:18 (id: 119055018)

18He redeems my soul in peace from the battle waged against me, even though many oppose me.


## Psalms 55:19 (id: 119055019)

19God will hear and humiliate them—the One enthroned for the ages—Selah because they do not change and they have no fear of God.


## Psalms 55:20 (id: 119055020)

20My companion attacks his friends; he violates his covenant.


## Psalms 55:21 (id: 119055021)

21His speech is smooth as butter, but war is in his heart. His words are softer than oil, yet they are swords unsheathed.


## Psalms 55:22 (id: 119055022)

22Cast your burden upon the LORD and He will sustain you; He will never let the righteous be shaken.


## Psalms 55:23 (id: 119055023)

23But You, O God, will bring them down to the Pit of destruction; men of bloodshed and deceit will not live out half their days. But I will trust in You.


## Psalms 56:0 (id: 119056000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “A Dove on Distant Oaks.” A Miktam of David, when the Philistines seized him in Gath.


## Psalms 56:1 (id: 119056001)

1Be merciful to me, O God, for men are hounding me; all day they press their attack.


## Psalms 56:2 (id: 119056002)

2My enemies pursue me all day long, for many proudly assail me.


## Psalms 56:3 (id: 119056003)

3When I am afraid, I put my trust in You.


## Psalms 56:4 (id: 119056004)

4In God, whose word I praise—in God I trust. I will not be afraid. What can man do to me?


## Psalms 56:5 (id: 119056005)

5All day long they twist my words; all their thoughts are on my demise.


## Psalms 56:6 (id: 119056006)

6They conspire, they lurk, they watch my steps while they wait to take my life.


## Psalms 56:7 (id: 119056007)

7In spite of such sin, will they escape? In Your anger, O God, cast down the nations.


## Psalms 56:8 (id: 119056008)

8You have taken account of my wanderings. Put my tears in Your bottle—are they not in Your book?


## Psalms 56:9 (id: 119056009)

9Then my enemies will retreat on the day I cry for help. By this I will know that God is on my side.


## Psalms 56:10 (id: 119056010)

10In God, whose word I praise, in the LORD, whose word I praise,


## Psalms 56:11 (id: 119056011)

11in God I trust; I will not be afraid. What can man do to me?


## Psalms 56:12 (id: 119056012)

12Your vows are upon me, O God; I will render thank offerings to You.


## Psalms 56:13 (id: 119056013)

13For You have delivered my soul from death, and my feet from stumbling, that I may walk before God in the light of life.


## Psalms 57:0 (id: 119057000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A Miktam of David, when he fled from Saul into the cave.


## Psalms 57:1 (id: 119057001)

1Have mercy on me, O God, have mercy, for in You my soul takes refuge. In the shadow of Your wings I will take shelter until the danger has passed.


## Psalms 57:2 (id: 119057002)

2I cry out to God Most High, to God who fulfills His purpose for me.


## Psalms 57:3 (id: 119057003)

3He reaches down from heaven and saves me; He rebukes those who trample me. Selah God sends forth His loving devotion and His truth.


## Psalms 57:4 (id: 119057004)

4My soul is among the lions; I lie down with ravenous beasts—with men whose teeth are spears and arrows, whose tongues are sharp swords.


## Psalms 57:5 (id: 119057005)

5Be exalted, O God, above the heavens; may Your glory cover all the earth.


## Psalms 57:6 (id: 119057006)

6They spread a net for my feet; my soul was despondent. They dug a pit before me, but they themselves have fallen into it! Selah


## Psalms 57:7 (id: 119057007)

7My heart is steadfast, O God, my heart is steadfast. I will sing and make music.


## Psalms 57:8 (id: 119057008)

8Awake, my glory! Awake, O harp and lyre! I will awaken the dawn.


## Psalms 57:9 (id: 119057009)

## Psalms 57:10 (id: 119057010)

10For Your loving devotion reaches to the heavens, and Your faithfulness to the clouds.


## Psalms 57:11 (id: 119057011)

11Be exalted, O God, above the heavens; may Your glory cover all the earth.


## Psalms 58:0 (id: 119058000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A Miktam of David.


## Psalms 58:1 (id: 119058001)

1Do you indeed speak justly, O rulers? Do you judge uprightly, O sons of men?


## Psalms 58:2 (id: 119058002)

2No, in your hearts you devise injustice; with your hands you mete out violence on the earth.


## Psalms 58:3 (id: 119058003)

3The wicked are estranged from the womb; the liars go astray from birth.


## Psalms 58:4 (id: 119058004)

4Their venom is like the venom of a snake, like a cobra that shuts its ears,


## Psalms 58:5 (id: 119058005)

5refusing to hear the tune of the charmer who skillfully weaves his spell.


## Psalms 58:6 (id: 119058006)

6O God, shatter their teeth in their mouths; O LORD, tear out the fangs of the lions.


## Psalms 58:7 (id: 119058007)

7May they vanish like water that runs off; when they draw the bow, may their arrows be blunted.


## Psalms 58:8 (id: 119058008)

8Like a slug that dissolves in its slime, like a woman’s stillborn child, may they never see the sun.


## Psalms 58:9 (id: 119058009)

9Before your pots can feel the burning thorns—whether green or dry—He will sweep them away.


## Psalms 58:10 (id: 119058010)

10The righteous will rejoice when they see they are avenged; they will wash their feet in the blood of the wicked.


## Psalms 58:11 (id: 119058011)

11Then men will say, “There is surely a reward for the righteous! There is surely a God who judges the earth!”


## Psalms 59:0 (id: 119059000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A Miktam of David, when Saul sent men to watch David’s house in order to kill him.


## Psalms 59:1 (id: 119059001)

1Deliver me from my enemies, O my God; protect me from those who rise against me.


## Psalms 59:2 (id: 119059002)

2Deliver me from workers of iniquity, and save me from men of bloodshed.


## Psalms 59:3 (id: 119059003)

3See how they lie in wait for me. Fierce men conspire against me for no transgression or sin of my own, O LORD.


## Psalms 59:4 (id: 119059004)

4For no fault of my own, they move swiftly to attack me. Arise to help me, and take notice.


## Psalms 59:5 (id: 119059005)

5O LORD God of Hosts, the God of Israel, rouse Yourself to punish all the nations; show no mercy to the wicked traitors. Selah


## Psalms 59:6 (id: 119059006)

6They return in the evening, snarling like dogs and prowling around the city.


## Psalms 59:7 (id: 119059007)

7See what they spew from their mouths—sharp words from their lips: “For who can hear us?”


## Psalms 59:8 (id: 119059008)

8But You, O LORD, laugh at them; You scoff at all the nations.


## Psalms 59:9 (id: 119059009)

9I will keep watch for You, O my strength, because You, O God, are my fortress.


## Psalms 59:10 (id: 119059010)

10My God of loving devotion will come to meet me; God will let me stare down my foes.


## Psalms 59:11 (id: 119059011)

11Do not kill them, or my people will forget. Scatter them by Your power, and bring them down, O Lord, our shield.


## Psalms 59:12 (id: 119059012)

12By the sins of their mouths and the words of their lips, let them be trapped in their pride, in the curses and lies they utter.


## Psalms 59:13 (id: 119059013)

13Consume them in wrath; consume them till they are no more, so it may be known to the ends of the earth that God rules over Jacob. Selah


## Psalms 59:14 (id: 119059014)

14They return in the evening, snarling like dogs and prowling around the city.


## Psalms 59:15 (id: 119059015)

15They scavenge for food, and growl if they are not satisfied.


## Psalms 59:16 (id: 119059016)

16But I will sing of Your strength and proclaim Your loving devotion in the morning. For You are my fortress, my refuge in times of trouble.


## Psalms 59:17 (id: 119059017)

17To You, O my strength, I sing praises, for You, O God, are my fortress, my God of loving devotion.


## Psalms 60:0 (id: 119060000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “The Lily of the Covenant.” A Miktam of David for instruction. When he fought Aram\-naharaim and Aram\-zobah, and Joab returned and struck down 12,000 Edomites in the Valley of Salt.


## Psalms 60:1 (id: 119060001)

1You have rejected us, O God; You have broken us; You have been angry; restore us!

## Psalms 60:3 (id: 119060003)

3You have shown Your people hardship; we are staggered from the wine You made us drink.


## Psalms 60:4 (id: 119060004)

4You have raised a banner for those who fear You, that they may flee the bow. Selah


## Psalms 60:5 (id: 119060005)

5Respond and save us with Your right hand, that Your beloved may be delivered.

## Psalms 60:7 (id: 119060007)

7Gilead is Mine, and Manasseh is Mine; Ephraim is My helmet, Judah is My scepter.


## Psalms 60:8 (id: 119060008)

8Moab is My washbasin; upon Edom I toss My sandal; over Philistia I shout in triumph.”


## Psalms 60:9 (id: 119060009)

9Who will bring me to the fortified city? Who will lead me to Edom?


## Psalms 60:10 (id: 119060010)

10Have You not rejected us, O God? Will You no longer march out, O God, with our armies?


## Psalms 60:11 (id: 119060011)

11Give us aid against the enemy, for the help of man is worthless.


## Psalms 60:12 (id: 119060012)

12With God we will perform with valor, and He will trample our enemies.

## Psalms 62:0 (id: 119062000)

0For the choirmaster. According to Jeduthun. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 62:1 (id: 119062001)

1In God alone my soul finds rest; my salvation comes from Him.


## Psalms 62:2 (id: 119062002)

2He alone is my rock and my salvation. He is my fortress; I will never be shaken.


## Psalms 62:3 (id: 119062003)

3How long will you threaten a man? Will all of you throw him down like a leaning wall or a tottering fence?


## Psalms 62:4 (id: 119062004)

## Psalms 62:5 (id: 119062005)

## Psalms 62:6 (id: 119062006)

6He alone is my rock and my salvation; He is my fortress; I will not be shaken.


## Psalms 62:7 (id: 119062007)

7My salvation and my honor rest on God, my strong rock; my refuge is in God.


## Psalms 62:8 (id: 119062008)

8Trust in Him at all times, O people; pour out your hearts before Him. God is our refuge. Selah


## Psalms 62:9 (id: 119062009)

## Psalms 62:10 (id: 119062010)

10Place no trust in extortion or false hope in stolen goods. If your riches increase, do not set your heart upon them.

11God has spoken once; I have heard this twice: that power belongs to God,


## Psalms 62:12 (id: 119062012)

12and loving devotion to You, O Lord. For You will repay each man according to his deeds.


## Psalms 63:0 (id: 119063000)

0A Psalm of David, when he was in the Wilderness of Judah.


## Psalms 63:1 (id: 119063001)

1O God, You are my God. Earnestly I seek You; my soul thirsts for You. My body yearns for You in a dry and weary land without water.


## Psalms 63:2 (id: 119063002)

2So I have seen You in the sanctuary and beheld Your power and glory.


## Psalms 63:3 (id: 119063003)

3Because Your loving devotion is better than life, my lips will glorify You.


## Psalms 63:4 (id: 119063004)

4So I will bless You as long as I live; in Your name I will lift my hands.


## Psalms 63:5 (id: 119063005)

5My soul is satisfied as with the richest of foods; with joyful lips my mouth will praise You.


## Psalms 63:6 (id: 119063006)

6When I remember You on my bed, I think of You through the watches of the night.


## Psalms 63:7 (id: 119063007)

7For You are my help; I will sing for joy in the shadow of Your wings.


## Psalms 63:8 (id: 119063008)

8My soul clings to You; Your right hand upholds me.


## Psalms 63:9 (id: 119063009)

9But those who seek my life to destroy it will go into the depths of the earth.


## Psalms 63:10 (id: 119063010)

10They will fall to the power of the sword; they will become a portion for foxes.


## Psalms 63:11 (id: 119063011)

11But the king will rejoice in God; all who swear by Him will exult, for the mouths of liars will be shut.


## Psalms 64:0 (id: 119064000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 64:1 (id: 119064001)

1Hear, O God, my voice of complaint; preserve my life from dread of the enemy.


## Psalms 64:2 (id: 119064002)

2Hide me from the scheming of the wicked, from the mob of workers of iniquity,


## Psalms 64:3 (id: 119064003)

3who sharpen their tongues like swords and aim their bitter words like arrows,


## Psalms 64:4 (id: 119064004)

4ambushing the innocent in seclusion, shooting suddenly, without fear.


## Psalms 64:5 (id: 119064005)

5They hold fast to their evil purpose; they speak of hiding their snares. “Who will see them?” they say.


## Psalms 64:6 (id: 119064006)

6They devise injustice and say, “We have perfected a secret plan.” For the inner man and the heart are mysterious.


## Psalms 64:7 (id: 119064007)

7But God will shoot them with arrows; suddenly they will be wounded.


## Psalms 64:8 (id: 119064008)

8They will be made to stumble, their own tongues turned against them. All who see will shake their heads.


## Psalms 64:9 (id: 119064009)

9Then all mankind will fear and proclaim the work of God; so they will ponder what He has done.


## Psalms 64:10 (id: 119064010)

10Let the righteous rejoice in the LORD and take refuge in Him; let all the upright in heart exult.


## Psalms 65:0 (id: 119065000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David. A song.


## Psalms 65:1 (id: 119065001)

1Praise awaits You, O God, in Zion; to You our vows will be fulfilled.


## Psalms 65:2 (id: 119065002)

2O You who listen to prayer, all people will come to You.


## Psalms 65:3 (id: 119065003)

3When iniquities prevail against me, You atone for our transgressions.


## Psalms 65:4 (id: 119065004)

4Blessed is the one You choose and bring near to dwell in Your courts! We are filled with the goodness of Your house, the holiness of Your temple.


## Psalms 65:5 (id: 119065005)

5With awesome deeds of righteousness You answer us, O God of our salvation, the hope of all the ends of the earth and of the farthest seas.


## Psalms 65:6 (id: 119065006)

6You formed the mountains by Your power, having girded Yourself with might.


## Psalms 65:7 (id: 119065007)

7You stilled the roaring of the seas, the pounding of their waves, and the tumult of the nations.


## Psalms 65:8 (id: 119065008)

8Those who live far away fear Your wonders; You make the dawn and sunset shout for joy.


## Psalms 65:9 (id: 119065009)

9You attend to the earth and water it; with abundance You enrich it. The streams of God are full of water, for You prepare our grain by providing for the earth.


## Psalms 65:10 (id: 119065010)

10You soak its furrows and level its ridges; You soften it with showers and bless its growth.


## Psalms 65:11 (id: 119065011)

11You crown the year with Your bounty, and Your paths overflow with plenty.


## Psalms 65:12 (id: 119065012)

12The pastures of the wilderness overflow; the hills are robed with joy.


## Psalms 65:13 (id: 119065013)

13The pastures are clothed with flocks, and the valleys are decked with grain. They shout in triumph; indeed, they sing.


## Psalms 66:0 (id: 119066000)

0For the choirmaster. A song. A Psalm.


## Psalms 66:1 (id: 119066001)

1Make a joyful noise to God, all the earth!


## Psalms 66:2 (id: 119066002)

2Sing the glory of His name; make His praise glorious.


## Psalms 66:3 (id: 119066003)

3Say to God, “How awesome are Your deeds! So great is Your power that Your enemies cower before You.


## Psalms 66:4 (id: 119066004)

4All the earth bows down to You; they sing praise to You; they sing praise to Your name.” Selah


## Psalms 66:5 (id: 119066005)

5Come and see the works of God; how awesome are His deeds toward mankind.


## Psalms 66:6 (id: 119066006)

6He turned the sea into dry land; they passed through the waters on foot; there we rejoiced in Him.


## Psalms 66:7 (id: 119066007)

7He rules forever by His power; His eyes watch the nations. Do not let the rebellious exalt themselves. Selah


## Psalms 66:8 (id: 119066008)

8Bless our God, O peoples; let the sound of His praise be heard.


## Psalms 66:9 (id: 119066009)

9He preserves our lives and keeps our feet from slipping.


## Psalms 66:10 (id: 119066010)

10For You, O God, have tested us; You have refined us like silver.


## Psalms 66:11 (id: 119066011)

11You led us into the net; You laid burdens on our backs.


## Psalms 66:12 (id: 119066012)

12You let men ride over our heads; we went through fire and water, but You brought us into abundance.


## Psalms 66:13 (id: 119066013)

13I will enter Your house with burnt offerings; I will fulfill my vows to You—


## Psalms 66:14 (id: 119066014)

14the vows that my lips promised and my mouth spoke in my distress.


## Psalms 66:15 (id: 119066015)

15I will offer You fatlings as burnt offerings, with the fragrant smoke of rams; I will offer bulls and goats. Selah


## Psalms 66:16 (id: 119066016)

16Come and listen, all you who fear God, and I will declare what He has done for me.


## Psalms 66:17 (id: 119066017)

17I cried out to Him with my mouth and praised Him with my tongue.


## Psalms 66:18 (id: 119066018)

18If I had cherished iniquity in my heart, the Lord would not have listened.


## Psalms 66:19 (id: 119066019)

19But God has surely heard; He has attended to the sound of my prayer.


## Psalms 66:20 (id: 119066020)

20Blessed be God, who has not rejected my prayer or withheld from me His loving devotion!


## Psalms 67:0 (id: 119067000)

0For the choirmaster. With stringed instruments. A Psalm. A song.


## Psalms 67:1 (id: 119067001)

1May God be gracious to us and bless us, and cause His face to shine upon us, Selah


## Psalms 67:2 (id: 119067002)

2that Your ways may be known on earth, Your salvation among all nations.


## Psalms 67:3 (id: 119067003)

3Let the peoples praise You, O God; let all the peoples praise You.


## Psalms 67:4 (id: 119067004)

4Let the nations be glad and sing for joy, for You judge the peoples justly and lead the nations of the earth. Selah


## Psalms 67:5 (id: 119067005)

5Let the peoples praise You, O God; let all the peoples praise You.


## Psalms 67:6 (id: 119067006)

## Psalms 67:7 (id: 119067007)
