## Psalms 68:0 (id: 119068000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David. A song.


## Psalms 68:1 (id: 119068001)

1God arises. His enemies are scattered, and those who hate Him flee His presence.


## Psalms 68:2 (id: 119068002)

2As smoke is blown away, You will drive them out; as wax melts before the fire, the wicked will perish in the presence of God.


## Psalms 68:3 (id: 119068003)

3But the righteous will be glad and rejoice before God; they will celebrate with joy.


## Psalms 68:4 (id: 119068004)

4Sing to God! Sing praises to His name. Exalt Him who rides on the clouds—His name is the LORD—and rejoice before Him.


## Psalms 68:5 (id: 119068005)

5A father of the fatherless and a defender of widows is God in His holy habitation.


## Psalms 68:6 (id: 119068006)

6God settles the lonely in families; He leads the prisoners out to prosperity, but the rebellious dwell in a sun\-scorched land.


## Psalms 68:7 (id: 119068007)

7O God, when You went out before Your people, when You marched through the wasteland, Selah


## Psalms 68:8 (id: 119068008)

8the earth shook and the heavens poured down rain before God, the One on Sinai, before God, the God of Israel.


## Psalms 68:9 (id: 119068009)

9You sent abundant rain, O God; You refreshed Your weary inheritance.


## Psalms 68:10 (id: 119068010)

10Your flock settled therein; O God, from Your bounty You provided for the poor.


## Psalms 68:11 (id: 119068011)

11The Lord gives the command; a great company of women proclaim it:


## Psalms 68:12 (id: 119068012)

12“Kings and their armies flee in haste; she who waits at home divides the plunder.


## Psalms 68:13 (id: 119068013)

13Though you lie down among the sheepfolds, the wings of the dove are covered with silver, and her feathers with shimmering gold.”


## Psalms 68:14 (id: 119068014)

14When the Almighty scattered the kings in the land, it was like the snow falling on Zalmon.


## Psalms 68:15 (id: 119068015)

15A mountain of God is Mount Bashan; a mountain of many peaks is Mount Bashan.


## Psalms 68:16 (id: 119068016)

16Why do you gaze in envy, O mountains of many peaks? This is the mountain God chose for His dwelling, where the LORD will surely dwell forever.


## Psalms 68:17 (id: 119068017)

17The chariots of God are tens of thousands—thousands of thousands are they; the Lord is in His sanctuary as He was at Sinai.


## Psalms 68:18 (id: 119068018)

18You have ascended on high; You have led captives away. You have received gifts from men, even from the rebellious, that the LORD God may dwell there.


## Psalms 68:19 (id: 119068019)

19Blessed be the Lord, who daily bears our burden, the God of our salvation. Selah


## Psalms 68:20 (id: 119068020)

20Our God is a God of deliverance; the Lord GOD is our rescuer from death.


## Psalms 68:21 (id: 119068021)

21Surely God will crush the heads of His enemies, the hairy crowns of those who persist in guilty ways.


## Psalms 68:22 (id: 119068022)

22The Lord said, “I will retrieve them from Bashan, I will bring them up from the depths of the sea,


## Psalms 68:23 (id: 119068023)

23that your foot may be dipped in the blood of your foes—the tongues of your dogs in the same.”


## Psalms 68:24 (id: 119068024)

24They have seen Your procession, O God—the march of my God and King into the sanctuary.


## Psalms 68:25 (id: 119068025)

25The singers lead the way, the musicians follow after, among the maidens playing tambourines.


## Psalms 68:26 (id: 119068026)

26Bless God in the great congregation; bless the LORD from the fountain of Israel.


## Psalms 68:27 (id: 119068027)

27There is Benjamin, the youngest, ruling them, the princes of Judah in their company, the princes of Zebulun and of Naphtali.


## Psalms 68:28 (id: 119068028)

28Summon Your power, O God; show Your strength, O God, which You have exerted on our behalf.


## Psalms 68:29 (id: 119068029)

29Because of Your temple at Jerusalem kings will bring You gifts.


## Psalms 68:30 (id: 119068030)

30Rebuke the beast in the reeds, the herd of bulls among the calves of the nations, until it submits, bringing bars of silver. Scatter the nations who delight in war.


## Psalms 68:31 (id: 119068031)

31Envoys will arrive from Egypt; Cush will stretch out her hands to God.


## Psalms 68:32 (id: 119068032)

32Sing to God, O kingdoms of the earth; sing praises to the Lord—Selah


## Psalms 68:33 (id: 119068033)

33to Him who rides upon the highest heavens of old; behold, His mighty voice resounds.


## Psalms 68:34 (id: 119068034)

34Ascribe the power to God, whose majesty is over Israel, whose strength is in the skies.


## Psalms 68:35 (id: 119068035)

35O God, You are awesome in Your sanctuary; the God of Israel Himself gives strength and power to His people. Blessed be God!


## Psalms 69:0 (id: 119069000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “Lilies.” Of David.


## Psalms 69:1 (id: 119069001)

1Save me, O God, for the waters are up to my neck.


## Psalms 69:2 (id: 119069002)

2I have sunk into the miry depths, where there is no footing; I have drifted into deep waters, where the flood engulfs me.


## Psalms 69:3 (id: 119069003)

3I am weary from my crying; my throat is parched. My eyes fail, looking for my God.


## Psalms 69:4 (id: 119069004)

4Those who hate me without cause outnumber the hairs of my head; many are those who would destroy me—my enemies for no reason. Though I did not steal, I must repay.


## Psalms 69:5 (id: 119069005)

5You know my folly, O God, and my guilt is not hidden from You.


## Psalms 69:6 (id: 119069006)

6May those who hope in You not be ashamed through me, O Lord GOD of Hosts; may those who seek You not be dishonored through me, O God of Israel.


## Psalms 69:7 (id: 119069007)

7For I have endured scorn for Your sake, and shame has covered my face.


## Psalms 69:8 (id: 119069008)

8I have become a stranger to my brothers and a foreigner to my mother’s sons,


## Psalms 69:9 (id: 119069009)

9because zeal for Your house has consumed me, and the insults of those who insult You have fallen on me.


## Psalms 69:10 (id: 119069010)

10I wept and fasted, but it brought me reproach.


## Psalms 69:11 (id: 119069011)

11I made sackcloth my clothing, and I was sport to them.


## Psalms 69:12 (id: 119069012)

12Those who sit at the gate mock me, and I am the song of drunkards.


## Psalms 69:13 (id: 119069013)

13But my prayer to You, O LORD, is for a time of favor. In Your abundant loving devotion, O God, answer me with Your sure salvation.


## Psalms 69:14 (id: 119069014)

14Rescue me from the mire and do not let me sink; deliver me from my foes and out of the deep waters.


## Psalms 69:15 (id: 119069015)

15Do not let the floods engulf me or the depths swallow me up; let not the Pit close its mouth over me.


## Psalms 69:16 (id: 119069016)

16Answer me, O LORD, for Your loving devotion is good; turn to me in keeping with Your great compassion.


## Psalms 69:17 (id: 119069017)

17Hide not Your face from Your servant, for I am in distress. Answer me quickly!


## Psalms 69:18 (id: 119069018)

18Draw near to my soul and redeem me; ransom me because of my foes.


## Psalms 69:19 (id: 119069019)

19You know my reproach, my shame and disgrace. All my adversaries are before You.


## Psalms 69:20 (id: 119069020)

20Insults have broken my heart, and I am in despair. I looked for sympathy, but there was none, for comforters, but I found no one.


## Psalms 69:21 (id: 119069021)

21They poisoned my food with gall and gave me vinegar to quench my thirst.


## Psalms 69:22 (id: 119069022)

22May their table become a snare; may it be a retribution and a trap.


## Psalms 69:23 (id: 119069023)

23May their eyes be darkened so they cannot see, and their backs be bent forever.


## Psalms 69:24 (id: 119069024)

24Pour out Your wrath upon them, and let Your burning anger overtake them.


## Psalms 69:25 (id: 119069025)

25May their place be deserted; let there be no one to dwell in their tents.


## Psalms 69:26 (id: 119069026)

26For they persecute the one You struck and recount the pain of those You wounded.


## Psalms 69:27 (id: 119069027)

27Add iniquity to their iniquity; let them not share in Your righteousness.


## Psalms 69:28 (id: 119069028)

28May they be blotted out of the Book of Life and not listed with the righteous.


## Psalms 69:29 (id: 119069029)

29But I am in pain and distress; let Your salvation protect me, O God.


## Psalms 69:30 (id: 119069030)

30I will praise God’s name in song and exalt Him with thanksgiving.


## Psalms 69:31 (id: 119069031)

31And this will please the LORD more than an ox, more than a bull with horns and hooves.


## Psalms 69:32 (id: 119069032)

32The humble will see and rejoice. You who seek God, let your hearts be revived!


## Psalms 69:33 (id: 119069033)

33For the LORD listens to the needy and does not despise His captive people.


## Psalms 69:34 (id: 119069034)

34Let heaven and earth praise Him, the seas and everything that moves in them.


## Psalms 69:35 (id: 119069035)

35For God will save Zion and rebuild the cities of Judah, that they may dwell there and possess it.


## Psalms 69:36 (id: 119069036)

36The descendants of His servants will inherit it, and those who love His name will settle in it.


## Psalms 70:0 (id: 119070000)

0For the choirmaster. Of David. To bring remembrance.


## Psalms 70:1 (id: 119070001)

1Make haste, O God, to deliver me! Hurry, O LORD, to help me!


## Psalms 70:2 (id: 119070002)

2May those who seek my life be ashamed and confounded; may those who wish me harm be repelled and humiliated.


## Psalms 70:3 (id: 119070003)

3May those who say, “Aha, aha!” retreat because of their shame.


## Psalms 70:4 (id: 119070004)

4May all who seek You rejoice and be glad in You; may those who love Your salvation always say, “Let God be magnified!”


## Psalms 70:5 (id: 119070005)

5But I am poor and needy; hurry to me, O God. You are my help and my deliverer; O LORD, do not delay.


## Psalms 71:1 (id: 119071001)

1In You, O LORD, I have taken refuge; let me never be put to shame.


## Psalms 71:2 (id: 119071002)

2In Your justice, rescue and deliver me; incline Your ear and save me.


## Psalms 71:3 (id: 119071003)

3Be my rock of refuge, where I can always go. Give the command to save me, for You are my rock and my fortress.


## Psalms 71:4 (id: 119071004)

4Deliver me, O my God, from the hand of the wicked, from the grasp of the unjust and ruthless.


## Psalms 71:5 (id: 119071005)

5For You are my hope, O Lord GOD, my confidence from my youth.


## Psalms 71:6 (id: 119071006)

6I have leaned on You since birth; You pulled me from my mother’s womb. My praise is always for You.


## Psalms 71:7 (id: 119071007)

7I have become a portent to many, but You are my strong refuge.


## Psalms 71:8 (id: 119071008)

8My mouth is filled with Your praise and with Your splendor all day long.


## Psalms 71:9 (id: 119071009)

9Do not discard me in my old age; do not forsake me when my strength fails.


## Psalms 71:10 (id: 119071010)

10For my enemies speak against me, and those who lie in wait for my life conspire,


## Psalms 71:11 (id: 119071011)

11saying, “God has forsaken him; pursue him and seize him, for there is no one to rescue him.”


## Psalms 71:12 (id: 119071012)

12Be not far from me, O God. Hurry, O my God, to help me.


## Psalms 71:13 (id: 119071013)

13May the accusers of my soul be ashamed and consumed; may those who seek my harm be covered with scorn and disgrace.


## Psalms 71:14 (id: 119071014)

14But I will always hope and will praise You more and more.


## Psalms 71:15 (id: 119071015)

15My mouth will declare Your righteousness and Your salvation all day long, though I cannot know their full measure.


## Psalms 71:16 (id: 119071016)

16I will come in the strength of the Lord GOD; I will proclaim Your righteousness—Yours alone.


## Psalms 71:17 (id: 119071017)

17O God, You have taught me from my youth, and to this day I proclaim Your marvelous deeds.


## Psalms 71:18 (id: 119071018)

18Even when I am old and gray, do not forsake me, O God, until I proclaim Your power to the next generation, Your might to all who are to come.


## Psalms 71:19 (id: 119071019)

19Your righteousness reaches to the heavens, O God, You who have done great things. Who, O God, is like You?


## Psalms 71:20 (id: 119071020)

20Though You have shown me many troubles and misfortunes, You will revive me once again. Even from the depths of the earth You will bring me back up.


## Psalms 71:21 (id: 119071021)

21You will increase my honor and comfort me once again.


## Psalms 71:22 (id: 119071022)

22So I will praise You with the harp for Your faithfulness, O my God; I will sing praise to You with the lyre, O Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 71:23 (id: 119071023)

23When I sing praise to You my lips will shout for joy, along with my soul, which You have redeemed.


## Psalms 71:24 (id: 119071024)

24My tongue will indeed proclaim Your righteousness all day long, for those who seek my harm are disgraced and confounded.


## Psalms 72:0 (id: 119072000)

0Of Solomon.


## Psalms 72:1 (id: 119072001)

1Endow the king with Your justice, O God, and the son of the king with Your righteousness.


## Psalms 72:2 (id: 119072002)

2May he judge Your people with righteousness and Your afflicted with justice.


## Psalms 72:3 (id: 119072003)

3May the mountains bring peace to the people, and the hills bring righteousness.


## Psalms 72:4 (id: 119072004)

4May he vindicate the afflicted among the people; may he save the children of the needy and crush the oppressor.


## Psalms 72:5 (id: 119072005)

5May they fear him as long as the sun shines, as long as the moon remains, through all generations.


## Psalms 72:6 (id: 119072006)

6May he be like rain that falls on freshly cut grass, like spring showers that water the earth.


## Psalms 72:7 (id: 119072007)

7May the righteous flourish in his days and prosperity abound until the moon is no more.


## Psalms 72:8 (id: 119072008)

8May he rule from sea to sea, and from the Euphrates to the ends of the earth.


## Psalms 72:9 (id: 119072009)

9May the nomads bow before him, and his enemies lick the dust.


## Psalms 72:10 (id: 119072010)

10May the kings of Tarshish and distant shores bring tribute; may the kings of Sheba and Seba offer gifts.


## Psalms 72:11 (id: 119072011)

11May all kings bow down to him and all nations serve him.


## Psalms 72:12 (id: 119072012)

12For he will deliver the needy who cry out and the afflicted who have no helper.


## Psalms 72:13 (id: 119072013)

13He will take pity on the poor and needy and save the lives of the oppressed.


## Psalms 72:14 (id: 119072014)

14He will redeem them from oppression and violence, for their blood is precious in his sight.


## Psalms 72:15 (id: 119072015)

15Long may he live! May gold from Sheba be given him. May people ever pray for him; may they bless him all day long.


## Psalms 72:16 (id: 119072016)

16May there be an abundance of grain in the land; may it sway atop the hills. May its fruit trees flourish like the forests of Lebanon, the people of its cities like the grass of the field.


## Psalms 72:17 (id: 119072017)

17May his name endure forever; may his name continue as long as the sun shines. In him may all nations be blessed; may they call him blessed.


## Psalms 72:18 (id: 119072018)

18Blessed be the LORD God, the God of Israel, who alone does marvelous deeds.


## Psalms 72:19 (id: 119072019)

19And blessed be His glorious name forever; may all the earth be filled with His glory. Amen and amen.


## Psalms 72:20 (id: 119072020)

20Thus conclude the prayers of David son of Jesse.


## Psalms 73:0 (id: 119073000)

0A Psalm of Asaph.


## Psalms 73:1 (id: 119073001)

1Surely God is good to Israel, to those who are pure in heart.


## Psalms 73:2 (id: 119073002)

2But as for me, my feet had almost stumbled; my steps had nearly slipped.


## Psalms 73:3 (id: 119073003)

3For I envied the arrogant when I saw the prosperity of the wicked.


## Psalms 73:4 (id: 119073004)

4They have no struggle in their death; their bodies are well\-fed.


## Psalms 73:5 (id: 119073005)

5They are free of the burdens others carry; they are not afflicted like other men.


## Psalms 73:6 (id: 119073006)

6Therefore pride is their necklace; a garment of violence covers them.


## Psalms 73:7 (id: 119073007)

7From their prosperity proceeds iniquity; the imaginations of their hearts run wild.


## Psalms 73:8 (id: 119073008)

8They mock and speak with malice; with arrogance they threaten oppression.


## Psalms 73:9 (id: 119073009)

9They set their mouths against the heavens, and their tongues strut across the earth.


## Psalms 73:10 (id: 119073010)

10So their people return to this place and drink up waters in abundance.


## Psalms 73:11 (id: 119073011)

11The wicked say, “How can God know? Does the Most High have knowledge?”


## Psalms 73:12 (id: 119073012)

12Behold, these are the wicked—always carefree as they increase their wealth.


## Psalms 73:13 (id: 119073013)

13Surely in vain I have kept my heart pure; in innocence I have washed my hands.


## Psalms 73:14 (id: 119073014)

14For I am afflicted all day long and punished every morning.


## Psalms 73:15 (id: 119073015)

15If I had said, “I will speak this way,” then I would have betrayed Your children.


## Psalms 73:16 (id: 119073016)

16When I tried to understand all this, it was troublesome in my sight


## Psalms 73:17 (id: 119073017)

17until I entered God’s sanctuary; then I discerned their end.


## Psalms 73:18 (id: 119073018)

18Surely You set them on slick ground; You cast them down into ruin.


## Psalms 73:19 (id: 119073019)

19How suddenly they are laid waste, completely swept away by terrors!


## Psalms 73:20 (id: 119073020)

20Like one waking from a dream, so You, O Lord, awaken and despise their form.


## Psalms 73:21 (id: 119073021)

21When my heart was grieved and I was pierced within,


## Psalms 73:22 (id: 119073022)

22I was senseless and ignorant; I was a brute beast before You.


## Psalms 73:23 (id: 119073023)

23Yet I am always with You; You hold my right hand.


## Psalms 73:24 (id: 119073024)

24You guide me with Your counsel, and later receive me in glory.


## Psalms 73:25 (id: 119073025)

25Whom have I in heaven but You? And on earth I desire no one besides You.


## Psalms 73:26 (id: 119073026)

26My flesh and my heart may fail, but God is the strength of my heart and my portion forever.


## Psalms 73:27 (id: 119073027)

27Those far from You will surely perish; You destroy all who are unfaithful to You.


## Psalms 73:28 (id: 119073028)

28But as for me, it is good to draw near to God. I have made the Lord GOD my refuge, that I may proclaim all Your works.


## Psalms 74:0 (id: 119074000)

0A Maskil of Asaph.


## Psalms 74:1 (id: 119074001)

1Why have You rejected us forever, O God? Why does Your anger smolder against the sheep of Your pasture?


## Psalms 74:2 (id: 119074002)

2Remember Your congregation, which You purchased long ago and redeemed as the tribe of Your inheritance—Mount Zion, where You dwell.


## Psalms 74:3 (id: 119074003)

3Turn Your steps to the everlasting ruins, to everything in the sanctuary the enemy has destroyed.


## Psalms 74:4 (id: 119074004)

4Your foes have roared within Your meeting place; they have unfurled their banners as signs,


## Psalms 74:5 (id: 119074005)

5like men wielding axes in a thicket of trees


## Psalms 74:6 (id: 119074006)

6and smashing all the carvings with hatchets and picks.


## Psalms 74:7 (id: 119074007)

7They have burned Your sanctuary to the ground; they have defiled the dwelling place of Your Name.


## Psalms 74:8 (id: 119074008)

8They said in their hearts, “We will crush them completely.” They burned down every place where God met us in the land.


## Psalms 74:9 (id: 119074009)

9There are no signs for us to see. There is no longer any prophet. And none of us knows how long this will last.


## Psalms 74:10 (id: 119074010)

10How long, O God, will the enemy taunt You? Will the foe revile Your name forever?


## Psalms 74:11 (id: 119074011)

11Why do You withdraw Your strong right hand? Stretch it out to destroy them!


## Psalms 74:12 (id: 119074012)

12Yet God is my King from ancient times, working salvation on the earth.


## Psalms 74:13 (id: 119074013)

13You divided the sea by Your strength; You smashed the heads of the dragons of the sea;


## Psalms 74:14 (id: 119074014)

14You crushed the heads of Leviathan; You fed him to the creatures of the desert.


## Psalms 74:15 (id: 119074015)

15You broke open the fountain and the flood; You dried up the ever\-flowing rivers.


## Psalms 74:16 (id: 119074016)

16The day is Yours, and also the night; You established the moon and the sun.


## Psalms 74:17 (id: 119074017)

17You set all the boundaries of the earth; You made the summer and winter.


## Psalms 74:18 (id: 119074018)

18Remember how the enemy has mocked You, O LORD, how a foolish people has spurned Your name.


## Psalms 74:19 (id: 119074019)

19Do not deliver the soul of Your dove to beasts; do not forget the lives of Your afflicted forever.


## Psalms 74:20 (id: 119074020)

20Consider Your covenant, for haunts of violence fill the dark places of the land.


## Psalms 74:21 (id: 119074021)

21Do not let the oppressed retreat in shame; may the poor and needy praise Your name.


## Psalms 74:22 (id: 119074022)

22Rise up, O God; defend Your cause! Remember how the fool mocks You all day long.


## Psalms 74:23 (id: 119074023)

23Do not disregard the clamor of Your adversaries, the uproar of Your enemies that ascends continually.


## Psalms 75:0 (id: 119075000)

0For the choirmaster: To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A Psalm of Asaph. A song.


## Psalms 75:1 (id: 119075001)

1We give thanks to You, O God; we give thanks, for Your Name is near. The people declare Your wondrous works.


## Psalms 75:2 (id: 119075002)

2“When I choose a time, I will judge fairly.


## Psalms 75:3 (id: 119075003)

3When the earth and all its dwellers quake, it is I who bear up its pillars. Selah


## Psalms 75:4 (id: 119075004)

4I say to the proud, ‘Do not boast,’ and to the wicked, ‘Do not lift up your horn.


## Psalms 75:5 (id: 119075005)

5Do not lift up your horn against heaven or speak with an outstretched neck.’”


## Psalms 75:6 (id: 119075006)

6For exaltation comes neither from east nor west, nor out of the desert,


## Psalms 75:7 (id: 119075007)

7but it is God who judges; He brings down one and exalts another.


## Psalms 75:8 (id: 119075008)

8For a cup is in the hand of the LORD, full of foaming wine mixed with spices. He pours from His cup, and all the wicked of the earth drink it down to the dregs.


## Psalms 75:9 (id: 119075009)

9But I will proclaim Him forever; I will sing praise to the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 75:10 (id: 119075010)

10“All the horns of the wicked I will cut off, but the horns of the righteous will be exalted.”


## Psalms 76:0 (id: 119076000)

0For the choirmaster. With stringed instruments. A Psalm of Asaph. A song.


## Psalms 76:1 (id: 119076001)

1God is known in Judah; His name is great in Israel.


## Psalms 76:2 (id: 119076002)

2His tent is in Salem, His dwelling place in Zion.


## Psalms 76:3 (id: 119076003)

3There He shattered the flaming arrows, the shield and sword and weapons of war. Selah


## Psalms 76:4 (id: 119076004)

4You are resplendent with light, more majestic than mountains filled with game.


## Psalms 76:5 (id: 119076005)

5The valiant lie plundered; they sleep their last sleep. No men of might could lift a hand.


## Psalms 76:6 (id: 119076006)

6At Your rebuke, O God of Jacob, both horse and rider lie stunned.


## Psalms 76:7 (id: 119076007)

7You alone are to be feared. When You are angry, who can stand before You?


## Psalms 76:8 (id: 119076008)

8From heaven You pronounced judgment, and the earth feared and was still


## Psalms 76:9 (id: 119076009)

9when God rose up to judge, to save all the lowly of the earth. Selah


## Psalms 76:10 (id: 119076010)

10Even the wrath of man shall praise You; with the survivors of wrath You will clothe Yourself.


## Psalms 76:11 (id: 119076011)

11Make and fulfill your vows to the LORD your God; let all the neighboring lands bring tribute to Him who is to be feared.


## Psalms 76:12 (id: 119076012)

12He breaks the spirits of princes; He is feared by the kings of the earth.


## Psalms 77:0 (id: 119077000)

0For the choirmaster. According to Jeduthun. A Psalm of Asaph.


## Psalms 77:1 (id: 119077001)

1I cried out to God; I cried aloud to God to hear me.


## Psalms 77:2 (id: 119077002)

2In the day of trouble I sought the Lord; through the night my outstretched hands did not grow weary; my soul refused to be comforted.


## Psalms 77:3 (id: 119077003)

3I remembered You, O God, and I groaned; I mused and my spirit grew faint. Selah


## Psalms 77:4 (id: 119077004)

4You have kept my eyes from closing; I am too troubled to speak.


## Psalms 77:5 (id: 119077005)

5I considered the days of old, the years long in the past.


## Psalms 77:6 (id: 119077006)

6At night I remembered my song; in my heart I mused, and my spirit pondered:


## Psalms 77:7 (id: 119077007)

7“Will the Lord spurn us forever and never show His favor again?


## Psalms 77:8 (id: 119077008)

8Is His loving devotion gone forever? Has His promise failed for all time?


## Psalms 77:9 (id: 119077009)

9Has God forgotten to be gracious? Has His anger shut off His compassion?” Selah


## Psalms 77:10 (id: 119077010)

10So I said, “I am grieved that the right hand of the Most High has changed.”


## Psalms 77:11 (id: 119077011)

11I will remember the works of the LORD; yes, I will remember Your wonders of old.


## Psalms 77:12 (id: 119077012)

12I will reflect on all You have done and ponder Your mighty deeds.


## Psalms 77:13 (id: 119077013)

13Your way, O God, is holy. What god is so great as our God?


## Psalms 77:14 (id: 119077014)

14You are the God who works wonders; You display Your strength among the peoples.


## Psalms 77:15 (id: 119077015)

15With power You redeemed Your people, the sons of Jacob and Joseph. Selah


## Psalms 77:16 (id: 119077016)

16The waters saw You, O God; the waters saw You and swirled; even the depths were shaken.


## Psalms 77:17 (id: 119077017)

17The clouds poured down water; the skies resounded with thunder; Your arrows flashed back and forth.


## Psalms 77:18 (id: 119077018)

18Your thunder resounded in the whirlwind; the lightning lit up the world; the earth trembled and quaked.


## Psalms 77:19 (id: 119077019)

19Your path led through the sea, Your way through the mighty waters, but Your footprints were not to be found.


## Psalms 77:20 (id: 119077020)

20You led Your people like a flock by the hand of Moses and Aaron.


## Psalms 78:0 (id: 119078000)

0A Maskil of Asaph.


## Psalms 78:1 (id: 119078001)

1Give ear, O my people, to my instruction; listen to the words of my mouth.


## Psalms 78:2 (id: 119078002)

2I will open my mouth in parables; I will utter things hidden from the beginning,


## Psalms 78:3 (id: 119078003)

3that we have heard and known and our fathers have relayed to us.


## Psalms 78:4 (id: 119078004)

4We will not hide them from their children but will declare to the next generation the praises of the LORD and His might and the wonders He has performed.


## Psalms 78:5 (id: 119078005)

5For He established a testimony in Jacob and appointed a law in Israel, which He commanded our fathers to teach to their children,


## Psalms 78:6 (id: 119078006)

6that the coming generation would know them—even children yet to be born—to arise and tell their own children


## Psalms 78:7 (id: 119078007)

7that they should put their confidence in God, not forgetting His works, but keeping His commandments.


## Psalms 78:8 (id: 119078008)

8Then they will not be like their fathers, a stubborn and rebellious generation, whose heart was not loyal, whose spirit was not faithful to God.


## Psalms 78:9 (id: 119078009)

9The archers of Ephraim turned back on the day of battle.


## Psalms 78:10 (id: 119078010)

10They failed to keep God’s covenant and refused to live by His law.


## Psalms 78:11 (id: 119078011)

11They forgot what He had done, the wonders He had shown them.


## Psalms 78:12 (id: 119078012)

12He worked wonders before their fathers in the land of Egypt, in the region of Zoan.


## Psalms 78:13 (id: 119078013)

13He split the sea and brought them through; He set the waters upright like a wall.


## Psalms 78:14 (id: 119078014)

14He led them with a cloud by day and with a light of fire all night.


## Psalms 78:15 (id: 119078015)

15He split the rocks in the wilderness and gave them drink as abundant as the seas.


## Psalms 78:16 (id: 119078016)

16He brought streams from the stone and made water flow down like rivers.


## Psalms 78:17 (id: 119078017)

17But they continued to sin against Him, rebelling in the desert against the Most High.


## Psalms 78:18 (id: 119078018)

18They willfully tested God by demanding the food they craved.


## Psalms 78:19 (id: 119078019)

19They spoke against God, saying, “Can God really prepare a table in the wilderness?


## Psalms 78:20 (id: 119078020)

20When He struck the rock, water gushed out and torrents raged. But can He also give bread or supply His people with meat?”


## Psalms 78:21 (id: 119078021)

21Therefore the LORD heard and was filled with wrath; so a fire was kindled against Jacob, and His anger flared against Israel,


## Psalms 78:22 (id: 119078022)

22because they did not believe God or rely on His salvation.


## Psalms 78:23 (id: 119078023)

23Yet He commanded the clouds above and opened the doors of the heavens.


## Psalms 78:24 (id: 119078024)

24He rained down manna for them to eat; He gave them grain from heaven.


## Psalms 78:25 (id: 119078025)

25Man ate the bread of angels; He sent them food in abundance.


## Psalms 78:26 (id: 119078026)

26He stirred the east wind from the heavens and drove the south wind by His might.


## Psalms 78:27 (id: 119078027)

27He rained meat on them like dust, and winged birds like the sand of the sea.


## Psalms 78:28 (id: 119078028)

28He felled them in the midst of their camp, all around their dwellings.


## Psalms 78:29 (id: 119078029)

29So they ate and were well filled, for He gave them what they craved.


## Psalms 78:30 (id: 119078030)

30Yet before they had filled their desire, with the food still in their mouths,


## Psalms 78:31 (id: 119078031)

31God’s anger flared against them, and He put to death their strongest and subdued the young men of Israel.


## Psalms 78:32 (id: 119078032)

32In spite of all this, they kept on sinning; despite His wonderful works, they did not believe.


## Psalms 78:33 (id: 119078033)

33So He ended their days in futility, and their years in sudden terror.


## Psalms 78:34 (id: 119078034)

34When He slew them, they would seek Him; they repented and searched for God.


## Psalms 78:35 (id: 119078035)

35And they remembered that God was their Rock, that God Most High was their Redeemer.


## Psalms 78:36 (id: 119078036)

36But they deceived Him with their mouths, and lied to Him with their tongues.


## Psalms 78:37 (id: 119078037)

37Their hearts were disloyal to Him, and they were unfaithful to His covenant.


## Psalms 78:38 (id: 119078038)

38And yet He was compassionate; He forgave their iniquity and did not destroy them. He often restrained His anger and did not unleash His full wrath.


## Psalms 78:39 (id: 119078039)

39He remembered that they were but flesh, a passing breeze that does not return.


## Psalms 78:40 (id: 119078040)

40How often they disobeyed Him in the wilderness and grieved Him in the desert!


## Psalms 78:41 (id: 119078041)

41Again and again they tested God and provoked the Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 78:42 (id: 119078042)

42They did not remember His power—the day He redeemed them from the adversary,


## Psalms 78:43 (id: 119078043)

43when He performed His signs in Egypt and His wonders in the fields of Zoan.


## Psalms 78:44 (id: 119078044)

44He turned their rivers to blood, and from their streams they could not drink.


## Psalms 78:45 (id: 119078045)

45He sent swarms of flies that devoured them, and frogs that devastated them.


## Psalms 78:46 (id: 119078046)

46He gave their crops to the grasshopper, the fruit of their labor to the locust.


## Psalms 78:47 (id: 119078047)

47He killed their vines with hailstones and their sycamore\-figs with sleet.


## Psalms 78:48 (id: 119078048)

48He abandoned their cattle to the hail and their livestock to bolts of lightning.


## Psalms 78:49 (id: 119078049)

49He unleashed His fury against them, wrath, indignation, and calamity—a band of destroying angels.


## Psalms 78:50 (id: 119078050)

50He cleared a path for His anger; He did not spare them from death but delivered their lives to the plague.


## Psalms 78:51 (id: 119078051)

51He struck all the firstborn of Egypt, the virility in the tents of Ham.


## Psalms 78:52 (id: 119078052)

52He led out His people like sheep and guided them like a flock in the wilderness.


## Psalms 78:53 (id: 119078053)

53He led them safely, so they did not fear, but the sea engulfed their enemies.


## Psalms 78:54 (id: 119078054)

54He brought them to His holy land, to the mountain His right hand had acquired.


## Psalms 78:55 (id: 119078055)

55He drove out nations before them and apportioned their inheritance; He settled the tribes of Israel in their tents.


## Psalms 78:56 (id: 119078056)

56But they tested and disobeyed God Most High, for they did not keep His decrees.


## Psalms 78:57 (id: 119078057)

57They turned back and were faithless like their fathers, twisted like a faulty bow.


## Psalms 78:58 (id: 119078058)

58They enraged Him with their high places and provoked His jealousy with their idols.


## Psalms 78:59 (id: 119078059)

59On hearing it, God was furious and rejected Israel completely.


## Psalms 78:60 (id: 119078060)

60He abandoned the tabernacle of Shiloh, the tent He had pitched among men.


## Psalms 78:61 (id: 119078061)

61He delivered His strength to captivity, and His splendor to the hand of the adversary.


## Psalms 78:62 (id: 119078062)

62He surrendered His people to the sword because He was enraged by His heritage.


## Psalms 78:63 (id: 119078063)

63Fire consumed His young men, and their maidens were left without wedding songs.


## Psalms 78:64 (id: 119078064)

64His priests fell by the sword, but their widows could not lament.


## Psalms 78:65 (id: 119078065)

65Then the Lord awoke as from sleep, like a mighty warrior overcome by wine.


## Psalms 78:66 (id: 119078066)

66He beat back His foes; He put them to everlasting shame.


## Psalms 78:67 (id: 119078067)

67He rejected the tent of Joseph and refused the tribe of Ephraim.


## Psalms 78:68 (id: 119078068)

68But He chose the tribe of Judah, Mount Zion, which He loved.


## Psalms 78:69 (id: 119078069)

69He built His sanctuary like the heights, like the earth He has established forever.


## Psalms 78:70 (id: 119078070)

70He chose David His servant and took him from the sheepfolds;


## Psalms 78:71 (id: 119078071)

71from tending the ewes He brought him to be shepherd of His people Jacob, of Israel His inheritance.


## Psalms 78:72 (id: 119078072)

72So David shepherded them with integrity of heart and guided them with skillful hands.


## Psalms 79:0 (id: 119079000)

0A Psalm of Asaph.


## Psalms 79:1 (id: 119079001)

1The nations, O God, have invaded Your inheritance; they have defiled Your holy temple and reduced Jerusalem to rubble.


## Psalms 79:2 (id: 119079002)

2They have given the corpses of Your servants as food to the birds of the air, the flesh of Your saints to the beasts of the earth.


## Psalms 79:3 (id: 119079003)

3They have poured out their blood like water all around Jerusalem, and there is no one to bury the dead.


## Psalms 79:4 (id: 119079004)

4We have become a reproach to our neighbors, a scorn and derision to those around us.


## Psalms 79:5 (id: 119079005)

5How long, O LORD? Will You be angry forever? Will Your jealousy burn like fire?


## Psalms 79:6 (id: 119079006)

6Pour out Your wrath on the nations that do not acknowledge You, on the kingdoms that refuse to call on Your name,


## Psalms 79:7 (id: 119079007)

7for they have devoured Jacob and devastated his homeland.


## Psalms 79:8 (id: 119079008)

8Do not hold past sins against us; let Your compassion come quickly, for we are brought low.


## Psalms 79:9 (id: 119079009)

9Help us, O God of our salvation, for the glory of Your name; deliver us and atone for our sins, for the sake of Your name.


## Psalms 79:10 (id: 119079010)

10Why should the nations ask, “Where is their God?” Before our eyes, make known among the nations Your vengeance for the bloodshed of Your servants.


## Psalms 79:11 (id: 119079011)

11May the groans of the captives reach You; by the strength of Your arm preserve those condemned to death.


## Psalms 79:12 (id: 119079012)

12Pay back into the laps of our neighbors sevenfold the reproach they hurled at You, O Lord.


## Psalms 79:13 (id: 119079013)

13Then we Your people, the sheep of Your pasture, will thank You forever; from generation to generation we will declare Your praise.


## Psalms 80:0 (id: 119080000)

0For the choirmaster. To the tune of “The Lilies of the Covenant.” A Psalm of Asaph.


## Psalms 80:1 (id: 119080001)

1Hear us, O Shepherd of Israel, who leads Joseph like a flock; You who sit enthroned between the cherubim, shine forth


## Psalms 80:2 (id: 119080002)

2before Ephraim, Benjamin, and Manasseh. Rally Your mighty power and come to save us.


## Psalms 80:3 (id: 119080003)

3Restore us, O God, and cause Your face to shine upon us, that we may be saved.


## Psalms 80:4 (id: 119080004)

4O LORD God of Hosts, how long will Your anger smolder against the prayers of Your people?


## Psalms 80:5 (id: 119080005)

5You fed them with the bread of tears and made them drink the full measure of their tears.


## Psalms 80:6 (id: 119080006)

6You make us contend with our neighbors; our enemies mock us.


## Psalms 80:7 (id: 119080007)

7Restore us, O God of Hosts, and cause Your face to shine upon us, that we may be saved.


## Psalms 80:8 (id: 119080008)

8You uprooted a vine from Egypt; You drove out the nations and transplanted it.


## Psalms 80:9 (id: 119080009)

9You cleared the ground for it, and it took root and filled the land.


## Psalms 80:10 (id: 119080010)

10The mountains were covered by its shade, and the mighty cedars with its branches.


## Psalms 80:11 (id: 119080011)

11It sent out its branches to the Sea, and its shoots toward the River.


## Psalms 80:12 (id: 119080012)

12Why have You broken down its walls, so that all who pass by pick its fruit?


## Psalms 80:13 (id: 119080013)

13The boar from the forest ravages it, and the creatures of the field feed upon it.


## Psalms 80:14 (id: 119080014)

14Return, O God of Hosts, we pray! Look down from heaven and see! Attend to this vine—


## Psalms 80:15 (id: 119080015)

15the root Your right hand has planted, the son You have raised up for Yourself.


## Psalms 80:16 (id: 119080016)

16Your vine has been cut down and burned; they perish at the rebuke of Your countenance.


## Psalms 80:17 (id: 119080017)

17Let Your hand be upon the man at Your right hand, on the son of man You have raised up for Yourself.


## Psalms 80:18 (id: 119080018)

18Then we will not turn away from You; revive us, and we will call on Your name.


## Psalms 80:19 (id: 119080019)

19Restore us, O LORD God of Hosts; cause Your face to shine upon us, that we may be saved.


## Psalms 81:0 (id: 119081000)

0For the choirmaster. According to Gittith. Of Asaph.


## Psalms 81:1 (id: 119081001)

1Sing for joy to God our strength; make a joyful noise to the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 81:2 (id: 119081002)

2Lift up a song, strike the tambourine, play the sweet\-sounding harp and lyre.


## Psalms 81:3 (id: 119081003)

3Sound the ram’s horn at the New Moon, and at the full moon on the day of our Feast.


## Psalms 81:4 (id: 119081004)

4For this is a statute for Israel, an ordinance of the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 81:5 (id: 119081005)

5He ordained it as a testimony for Joseph when he went out over the land of Egypt, where I heard an unfamiliar language:


## Psalms 81:6 (id: 119081006)

6“I relieved his shoulder of the burden; his hands were freed from the basket.


## Psalms 81:7 (id: 119081007)

7You called out in distress, and I rescued you; I answered you from the cloud of thunder; I tested you at the waters of Meribah. Selah


## Psalms 81:8 (id: 119081008)

8Hear, O My people, and I will warn you: O Israel, if only you would listen to Me!


## Psalms 81:9 (id: 119081009)

9There must be no strange god among you, nor shall you bow to a foreign god.


## Psalms 81:10 (id: 119081010)

10I am the LORD your God, who brought you up out of Egypt. Open wide your mouth, and I will fill it.


## Psalms 81:11 (id: 119081011)

11But My people would not listen to Me, and Israel would not obey Me.


## Psalms 81:12 (id: 119081012)

12So I gave them up to their stubborn hearts to follow their own devices.


## Psalms 81:13 (id: 119081013)

13If only My people would listen to Me, if Israel would follow My ways,


## Psalms 81:14 (id: 119081014)

14how soon I would subdue their enemies and turn My hand against their foes!


## Psalms 81:15 (id: 119081015)

15Those who hate the LORD would feign obedience, and their doom would last forever.


## Psalms 81:16 (id: 119081016)

16But I would feed you the finest wheat; with honey from the rock I would satisfy you.”

0A Psalm of Asaph.


## Psalms 82:1 (id: 119082001)

1God presides in the divine assembly; He renders judgment among the gods:


## Psalms 82:2 (id: 119082002)

## Psalms 82:3 (id: 119082003)

3Defend the cause of the weak and fatherless; uphold the rights of the afflicted and oppressed.


## Psalms 82:4 (id: 119082004)

4Rescue the weak and needy; save them from the hand of the wicked.


## Psalms 82:5 (id: 119082005)

5They do not know or understand; they wander in the darkness; all the foundations of the earth are shaken.


## Psalms 82:6 (id: 119082006)

## Psalms 82:7 (id: 119082007)

## Psalms 83:0 (id: 119083000)

0A song. A Psalm of Asaph.


## Psalms 83:1 (id: 119083001)

1O God, be not silent; be not speechless; be not still, O God.


## Psalms 83:2 (id: 119083002)

2See how Your enemies rage, how Your foes have reared their heads.


## Psalms 83:3 (id: 119083003)

3With cunning they scheme against Your people and conspire against those You cherish,


## Psalms 83:4 (id: 119083004)

4saying, “Come, let us erase them as a nation; may the name of Israel be remembered no more.”


## Psalms 83:5 (id: 119083005)

5For with one mind they plot together; they form an alliance against You—


## Psalms 83:6 (id: 119083006)

6the tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites, of Moab and the Hagrites,


## Psalms 83:7 (id: 119083007)

7of Gebal, Ammon, and Amalek, of Philistia with the people of Tyre.


## Psalms 83:8 (id: 119083008)

8Even Assyria has joined them, lending strength to the sons of Lot. Selah


## Psalms 83:9 (id: 119083009)

9Do to them as You did to Midian, as to Sisera and Jabin at the River Kishon,


## Psalms 83:10 (id: 119083010)

10who perished at Endor and became like dung on the ground.


## Psalms 83:11 (id: 119083011)

11Make their nobles like Oreb and Zeeb, and all their princes like Zebah and Zalmunna,


## Psalms 83:12 (id: 119083012)

12who said, “Let us possess for ourselves the pastures of God.”


## Psalms 83:13 (id: 119083013)

13Make them like tumbleweed, O my God, like chaff before the wind.


## Psalms 83:14 (id: 119083014)

14As fire consumes a forest, as a flame sets the mountains ablaze,


## Psalms 83:15 (id: 119083015)

15so pursue them with Your tempest, and terrify them with Your storm.


## Psalms 83:16 (id: 119083016)

16Cover their faces with shame, that they may seek Your name, O LORD.


## Psalms 83:17 (id: 119083017)

17May they be ever ashamed and terrified; may they perish in disgrace.


## Psalms 83:18 (id: 119083018)

18May they know that You alone, whose name is the LORD, are Most High over all the earth.


## Psalms 84:0 (id: 119084000)

0For the choirmaster. According to Gittith. A Psalm of the sons of Korah.


## Psalms 84:1 (id: 119084001)

1How lovely is Your dwelling place, O LORD of Hosts!


## Psalms 84:2 (id: 119084002)

2My soul longs, even faints, for the courts of the LORD; my heart and my flesh cry out for the living God.


## Psalms 84:3 (id: 119084003)

3Even the sparrow has found a home, and the swallow a nest for herself, where she places her young near Your altars, O LORD of Hosts, my King and my God.


## Psalms 84:4 (id: 119084004)

4How blessed are those who dwell in Your house! They are ever praising You. Selah


## Psalms 84:5 (id: 119084005)

5Blessed are those whose strength is in You, whose hearts are set on pilgrimage.


## Psalms 84:6 (id: 119084006)

6As they pass through the Valley of Baca, they make it a place of springs; even the autumn rain covers it with pools.


## Psalms 84:7 (id: 119084007)

7They go from strength to strength, until each appears before God in Zion.


## Psalms 84:8 (id: 119084008)

8O LORD God of Hosts, hear my prayer; give ear, O God of Jacob. Selah


## Psalms 84:9 (id: 119084009)

9Take notice of our shield, O God, and look with favor on the face of Your anointed.


## Psalms 84:10 (id: 119084010)

10For better is one day in Your courts than a thousand elsewhere. I would rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God than dwell in the tents of the wicked.


## Psalms 84:11 (id: 119084011)

11For the LORD God is a sun and a shield; the LORD gives grace and glory; He withholds no good thing from those who walk with integrity.


## Psalms 84:12 (id: 119084012)

12O LORD of Hosts, how blessed is the man who trusts in You!


## Psalms 85:0 (id: 119085000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of the sons of Korah.


## Psalms 85:1 (id: 119085001)

1You showed favor to Your land, O LORD; You restored Jacob from captivity.


## Psalms 85:2 (id: 119085002)

2You forgave the iniquity of Your people; You covered all their sin. Selah


## Psalms 85:3 (id: 119085003)

3You withheld all Your fury; You turned from Your burning anger.


## Psalms 85:4 (id: 119085004)

4Restore us, O God of our salvation, and put away Your displeasure toward us.


## Psalms 85:5 (id: 119085005)

5Will You be angry with us forever? Will You draw out Your anger to all generations?


## Psalms 85:6 (id: 119085006)

6Will You not revive us again, that Your people may rejoice in You?


## Psalms 85:7 (id: 119085007)

7Show us Your loving devotion, O LORD, and grant us Your salvation.


## Psalms 85:8 (id: 119085008)

8I will listen to what God the LORD will say; for He will surely speak peace to His people and His saints; He will not let them return to folly.


## Psalms 85:9 (id: 119085009)

9Surely His salvation is near to those who fear Him, that His glory may dwell in our land.


## Psalms 85:10 (id: 119085010)

10Loving devotion and faithfulness have joined together; righteousness and peace have kissed.


## Psalms 85:11 (id: 119085011)

11Faithfulness sprouts from the earth, and righteousness looks down from heaven.


## Psalms 85:12 (id: 119085012)

12The LORD will indeed provide what is good, and our land will yield its increase.


## Psalms 85:13 (id: 119085013)

13Righteousness will go before Him to prepare the way for His steps.


## Psalms 86:0 (id: 119086000)

0A prayer of David.


## Psalms 86:1 (id: 119086001)

1Incline Your ear, O LORD, and answer me, for I am poor and needy.


## Psalms 86:2 (id: 119086002)

2Preserve my soul, for I am godly. You are my God; save Your servant who trusts in You.


## Psalms 86:3 (id: 119086003)

3Be merciful to me, O Lord, for I call to You all day long.


## Psalms 86:4 (id: 119086004)

4Bring joy to Your servant, for to You, O Lord, I lift up my soul.


## Psalms 86:5 (id: 119086005)

5For You, O Lord, are kind and forgiving, rich in loving devotion to all who call on You.


## Psalms 86:6 (id: 119086006)

6Hear my prayer, O LORD, and attend to my plea for mercy.


## Psalms 86:7 (id: 119086007)

7In the day of my distress I call on You, because You answer me.


## Psalms 86:8 (id: 119086008)

8O Lord, there is none like You among the gods, nor any works like Yours.


## Psalms 86:9 (id: 119086009)

9All the nations You have made will come and bow before You, O Lord, and they will glorify Your name.


## Psalms 86:10 (id: 119086010)

10For You are great and perform wonders; You alone are God.


## Psalms 86:11 (id: 119086011)

11Teach me Your way, O LORD, that I may walk in Your truth. Give me an undivided heart, that I may fear Your name.


## Psalms 86:12 (id: 119086012)

12I will praise You, O Lord my God, with all my heart; I will glorify Your name forever.


## Psalms 86:13 (id: 119086013)

13For great is Your loving devotion to me; You have delivered me from the depths of Sheol.


## Psalms 86:14 (id: 119086014)

14The arrogant rise against me, O God; a band of ruthless men seeks my life; they have no regard for You.


## Psalms 86:15 (id: 119086015)

15But You, O Lord, are a compassionate and gracious God, slow to anger, abounding in loving devotion and faithfulness.


## Psalms 86:16 (id: 119086016)

16Turn to me and have mercy; grant Your strength to Your servant; save the son of Your maidservant.


## Psalms 86:17 (id: 119086017)

17Show me a sign of Your goodness, that my enemies may see and be ashamed; for You, O LORD, have helped me and comforted me.


## Psalms 87:0 (id: 119087000)

0A Psalm of the sons of Korah. A song.


## Psalms 87:1 (id: 119087001)

1He has founded His city on the holy mountains.


## Psalms 87:2 (id: 119087002)

2The LORD loves the gates of Zion more than all the dwellings of Jacob.


## Psalms 87:3 (id: 119087003)

3Glorious things are ascribed to you, O city of God. Selah


## Psalms 87:4 (id: 119087004)

4“I will mention Rahab and Babylon among those who know Me—along with Philistia, Tyre, and Cush—when I say, ‘This one was born in Zion.’”


## Psalms 87:5 (id: 119087005)

5And it will be said of Zion: “This one and that one were born in her, and the Most High Himself will establish her.”


## Psalms 87:6 (id: 119087006)

6The LORD will record in the register of the peoples: “This one was born in Zion.” Selah


## Psalms 87:7 (id: 119087007)

7Singers and pipers will proclaim, “All my springs of joy are in You.”


## Psalms 88:0 (id: 119088000)

0A song. A Psalm of the sons of Korah. For the choirmaster. According to Mahalath Leannoth. A Maskil of Heman the Ezrahite.


## Psalms 88:1 (id: 119088001)

1O LORD, the God of my salvation, day and night I cry out before You.


## Psalms 88:2 (id: 119088002)

2May my prayer come before You; incline Your ear to my cry.


## Psalms 88:3 (id: 119088003)

3For my soul is full of troubles, and my life draws near to Sheol.


## Psalms 88:4 (id: 119088004)

4I am counted among those descending to the Pit. I am like a man without strength.


## Psalms 88:5 (id: 119088005)

5I am forsaken among the dead, like the slain who lie in the grave, whom You remember no more, who are cut off from Your care.


## Psalms 88:6 (id: 119088006)

6You have laid me in the lowest Pit, in the darkest of the depths.


## Psalms 88:7 (id: 119088007)

7Your wrath weighs heavily upon me; all Your waves have submerged me. Selah


## Psalms 88:8 (id: 119088008)

8You have removed my friends from me; You have made me repulsive to them; I am confined and cannot escape.


## Psalms 88:9 (id: 119088009)

9My eyes grow dim with grief. I call to You daily, O LORD; I spread out my hands to You.


## Psalms 88:10 (id: 119088010)

10Do You work wonders for the dead? Do departed spirits rise up to praise You? Selah


## Psalms 88:11 (id: 119088011)

11Can Your loving devotion be proclaimed in the grave, Your faithfulness in Abaddon?


## Psalms 88:12 (id: 119088012)

12Will Your wonders be known in the darkness, or Your righteousness in the land of oblivion?


## Psalms 88:13 (id: 119088013)

13But to You, O LORD, I cry for help; in the morning my prayer comes before You.


## Psalms 88:14 (id: 119088014)

14Why, O LORD, do You reject me? Why do You hide Your face from me?


## Psalms 88:15 (id: 119088015)

15From my youth I was afflicted and near death. I have borne Your terrors; I am in despair.


## Psalms 88:16 (id: 119088016)

16Your wrath has swept over me; Your terrors have destroyed me.


## Psalms 88:17 (id: 119088017)

17All day long they engulf me like water; they enclose me on every side.


## Psalms 88:18 (id: 119088018)

18You have removed my beloved and my friend; darkness is my closest companion.


## Psalms 89:0 (id: 119089000)

0A Maskil of Ethan the Ezrahite.


## Psalms 89:1 (id: 119089001)

1I will sing of the loving devotion of the LORD forever; with my mouth I will proclaim Your faithfulness to all generations.


## Psalms 89:2 (id: 119089002)

2For I have said, “Loving devotion is built up forever; in the heavens You establish Your faithfulness.”


## Psalms 89:3 (id: 119089003)

3You said, “I have made a covenant with My chosen one, I have sworn to David My servant:


## Psalms 89:4 (id: 119089004)

4‘I will establish your offspring forever and build up your throne for all generations.’” Selah


## Psalms 89:5 (id: 119089005)

5The heavens praise Your wonders, O LORD—Your faithfulness as well—in the assembly of the holy ones.


## Psalms 89:6 (id: 119089006)

6For who in the skies can compare with the LORD? Who among the heavenly beings is like the LORD?


## Psalms 89:7 (id: 119089007)

7In the council of the holy ones, God is greatly feared, and awesome above all who surround Him.


## Psalms 89:8 (id: 119089008)

8O LORD God of Hosts, who is like You? O mighty LORD, Your faithfulness surrounds You.


## Psalms 89:9 (id: 119089009)

9You rule the raging sea; when its waves mount up, You still them.


## Psalms 89:10 (id: 119089010)

10You crushed Rahab like a carcass; You scattered Your enemies with Your mighty arm.


## Psalms 89:11 (id: 119089011)

11The heavens are Yours, and also the earth. The earth and its fullness You founded.


## Psalms 89:12 (id: 119089012)

12North and south You created; Tabor and Hermon shout for joy at Your name.


## Psalms 89:13 (id: 119089013)

13Mighty is Your arm; strong is Your hand. Your right hand is exalted.


## Psalms 89:14 (id: 119089014)

14Righteousness and justice are the foundation of Your throne; loving devotion and faithfulness go before You.


## Psalms 89:15 (id: 119089015)

15Blessed are those who know the joyful sound, who walk, O LORD, in the light of Your presence.


## Psalms 89:16 (id: 119089016)

16They rejoice in Your name all day long, and in Your righteousness they exult.


## Psalms 89:17 (id: 119089017)

17For You are the glory of their strength, and by Your favor our horn is exalted.


## Psalms 89:18 (id: 119089018)

18Surely our shield belongs to the LORD, and our king to the Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 89:19 (id: 119089019)

19You once spoke in a vision; to Your godly ones You said, “I have bestowed help on a warrior; I have exalted one chosen from the people.


## Psalms 89:20 (id: 119089020)

20I have found My servant David; with My sacred oil I have anointed him.


## Psalms 89:21 (id: 119089021)

21My hand will sustain him; surely My arm will strengthen him.


## Psalms 89:22 (id: 119089022)

22No enemy will exact tribute; no wicked man will oppress him.


## Psalms 89:23 (id: 119089023)

23I will crush his foes before him and strike down those who hate him.


## Psalms 89:24 (id: 119089024)

24My faithfulness and loving devotion will be with him, and through My name his horn will be exalted.


## Psalms 89:25 (id: 119089025)

25I will set his hand over the sea, and his right hand upon the rivers.


## Psalms 89:26 (id: 119089026)

26He will call to Me, ‘You are my Father, my God, the Rock of my salvation.’


## Psalms 89:27 (id: 119089027)

27I will indeed appoint him as My firstborn, the highest of the kings of the earth.


## Psalms 89:28 (id: 119089028)

28I will forever preserve My loving devotion for him, and My covenant with him will stand fast.


## Psalms 89:29 (id: 119089029)

29I will establish his line forever, his throne as long as the heavens endure.


## Psalms 89:30 (id: 119089030)

30If his sons forsake My law and do not walk in My judgments,


## Psalms 89:31 (id: 119089031)

31if they violate My statutes and fail to keep My commandments,


## Psalms 89:32 (id: 119089032)

32I will attend to their transgression with the rod, and to their iniquity with stripes.


## Psalms 89:33 (id: 119089033)

33But I will not withdraw My loving devotion from him, nor ever betray My faithfulness.


## Psalms 89:34 (id: 119089034)

34I will not violate My covenant or alter the utterance of My lips.


## Psalms 89:35 (id: 119089035)

35Once and for all I have sworn by My holiness—I will not lie to David—


## Psalms 89:36 (id: 119089036)

36his offspring shall endure forever, and his throne before Me like the sun,


## Psalms 89:37 (id: 119089037)

37like the moon, established forever, a faithful witness in the sky.” Selah


## Psalms 89:38 (id: 119089038)

38Now, however, You have spurned and rejected him; You are enraged by Your anointed one.


## Psalms 89:39 (id: 119089039)

39You have renounced the covenant with Your servant and sullied his crown in the dust.


## Psalms 89:40 (id: 119089040)

40You have broken down all his walls; You have reduced his strongholds to rubble.


## Psalms 89:41 (id: 119089041)

41All who pass by plunder him; he has become a reproach to his neighbors.


## Psalms 89:42 (id: 119089042)

42You have exalted the right hand of his foes; You have made all his enemies rejoice.


## Psalms 89:43 (id: 119089043)

43You have bent the edge of his sword and have not sustained him in battle.


## Psalms 89:44 (id: 119089044)

44You have ended his splendor and cast his throne to the ground.


## Psalms 89:45 (id: 119089045)

45You have cut short the days of his youth; You have covered him with shame. Selah


## Psalms 89:46 (id: 119089046)

46How long, O LORD? Will You hide Yourself forever? Will Your wrath keep burning like fire?


## Psalms 89:47 (id: 119089047)

47Remember the briefness of my lifespan! For what futility You have created all men!


## Psalms 89:48 (id: 119089048)

48What man can live and never see death? Can he deliver his soul from the power of Sheol? Selah


## Psalms 89:49 (id: 119089049)

49Where, O Lord, is Your loving devotion of old, which You faithfully swore to David?


## Psalms 89:50 (id: 119089050)

50Remember, O Lord, the reproach of Your servants, which I bear in my heart from so many people—


## Psalms 89:51 (id: 119089051)

51how Your enemies have taunted, O LORD, and have mocked every step of Your anointed one!


## Psalms 89:52 (id: 119089052)

52Blessed be the LORD forever! Amen and amen.


## Psalms 90:0 (id: 119090000)

0A prayer of Moses the man of God.


## Psalms 90:1 (id: 119090001)

1Lord, You have been our dwelling place through all generations.


## Psalms 90:2 (id: 119090002)

2Before the mountains were born or You brought forth the earth and the world, from everlasting to everlasting You are God.


## Psalms 90:3 (id: 119090003)

3You return man to dust, saying, “Return, O sons of mortals.”


## Psalms 90:4 (id: 119090004)

4For in Your sight a thousand years are but a day that passes, or a watch of the night.


## Psalms 90:5 (id: 119090005)

5You sweep them away in their sleep; they are like the new grass of the morning—


## Psalms 90:6 (id: 119090006)

6in the morning it springs up new, but by evening it fades and withers.


## Psalms 90:7 (id: 119090007)

7For we are consumed by Your anger and terrified by Your wrath.


## Psalms 90:8 (id: 119090008)

8You have set our iniquities before You, our secret sins in the light of Your presence.


## Psalms 90:9 (id: 119090009)

9For all our days decline in Your fury; we finish our years with a sigh.


## Psalms 90:10 (id: 119090010)

10The length of our days is seventy years—or eighty if we are strong—yet their pride is but labor and sorrow, for they quickly pass, and we fly away.


## Psalms 90:11 (id: 119090011)

11Who knows the power of Your anger? Your wrath matches the fear You are due.


## Psalms 90:12 (id: 119090012)

12So teach us to number our days, that we may present a heart of wisdom.


## Psalms 90:13 (id: 119090013)

13Return, O LORD! How long will it be? Have compassion on Your servants.


## Psalms 90:14 (id: 119090014)

14Satisfy us in the morning with Your loving devotion, that we may sing for joy and be glad all our days.


## Psalms 90:15 (id: 119090015)

15Make us glad for as many days as You have afflicted us, for as many years as we have seen evil.


## Psalms 90:16 (id: 119090016)

16May Your work be shown to Your servants, and Your splendor to their children.


## Psalms 90:17 (id: 119090017)

17May the favor of the Lord our God rest upon us; establish for us the work of our hands—yes, establish the work of our hands!


## Psalms 91:1 (id: 119091001)

1He who dwells in the shelter of the Most High will abide in the shadow of the Almighty.


## Psalms 91:2 (id: 119091002)

2I will say to the LORD, “You are my refuge and my fortress, my God, in whom I trust.”


## Psalms 91:3 (id: 119091003)

3Surely He will deliver you from the snare of the fowler, and from the deadly plague.


## Psalms 91:4 (id: 119091004)

4He will cover you with His feathers; under His wings you will find refuge; His faithfulness is a shield and rampart.


## Psalms 91:5 (id: 119091005)

5You will not fear the terror of the night, nor the arrow that flies by day,


## Psalms 91:6 (id: 119091006)

6nor the pestilence that stalks in the darkness, nor the calamity that destroys at noon.


## Psalms 91:7 (id: 119091007)

7Though a thousand may fall at your side, and ten thousand at your right hand, no harm will come near you.


## Psalms 91:8 (id: 119091008)

8You will only see it with your eyes and witness the punishment of the wicked.


## Psalms 91:9 (id: 119091009)

9Because you have made the LORD your dwelling—my refuge, the Most High—


## Psalms 91:10 (id: 119091010)

10no evil will befall you, no plague will approach your tent.


## Psalms 91:11 (id: 119091011)

11For He will command His angels concerning you to guard you in all your ways.


## Psalms 91:12 (id: 119091012)

12They will lift you up in their hands, so that you will not strike your foot against a stone.


## Psalms 91:13 (id: 119091013)

13You will tread on the lion and cobra; you will trample the young lion and serpent.


## Psalms 91:14 (id: 119091014)

14“Because he loves Me, I will deliver him; because he knows My name, I will protect him.


## Psalms 91:15 (id: 119091015)

15When he calls out to Me, I will answer him; I will be with him in trouble. I will deliver him and honor him.


## Psalms 91:16 (id: 119091016)

16With long life I will satisfy him and show him My salvation.”


## Psalms 92:0 (id: 119092000)

0A Psalm. A song for the Sabbath day.


## Psalms 92:1 (id: 119092001)

1It is good to praise the LORD, and to sing praises to Your name, O Most High,


## Psalms 92:2 (id: 119092002)

2to proclaim Your loving devotion in the morning and Your faithfulness at night


## Psalms 92:3 (id: 119092003)

3with the ten\-stringed harp and the melody of the lyre.


## Psalms 92:4 (id: 119092004)

4For You, O LORD, have made me glad by Your deeds; I sing for joy at the works of Your hands.


## Psalms 92:5 (id: 119092005)

5How great are Your works, O LORD, how deep are Your thoughts!


## Psalms 92:6 (id: 119092006)

6A senseless man does not know, and a fool does not understand,


## Psalms 92:7 (id: 119092007)

7that though the wicked sprout like grass, and all evildoers flourish, they will be forever destroyed.


## Psalms 92:8 (id: 119092008)

8But You, O LORD, are exalted forever!


## Psalms 92:9 (id: 119092009)

9For surely Your enemies, O LORD, surely Your enemies will perish; all evildoers will be scattered.


## Psalms 92:10 (id: 119092010)

10But You have exalted my horn like that of a wild ox; with fine oil I have been anointed.


## Psalms 92:11 (id: 119092011)

11My eyes see the downfall of my enemies; my ears hear the wailing of my wicked foes.


## Psalms 92:12 (id: 119092012)

12The righteous will flourish like a palm tree, and grow like a cedar in Lebanon.


## Psalms 92:13 (id: 119092013)

13Planted in the house of the LORD, they will flourish in the courts of our God.


## Psalms 92:14 (id: 119092014)

14In old age they will still bear fruit; healthy and green they will remain,


## Psalms 92:15 (id: 119092015)

15to proclaim, “The LORD is upright; He is my Rock, and in Him there is no unrighteousness.”


## Psalms 93:1 (id: 119093001)

1The LORD reigns! He is robed in majesty; the LORD has clothed and armed Himself with strength. The world indeed is firmly established; it cannot be moved.


## Psalms 93:2 (id: 119093002)

2Your throne was established long ago; You are from all eternity.


## Psalms 93:3 (id: 119093003)

3The floodwaters have risen, O LORD; the rivers have raised their voice; the seas lift up their pounding waves.


## Psalms 93:4 (id: 119093004)

4Above the roar of many waters—the mighty breakers of the sea—the LORD on high is majestic.


## Psalms 93:5 (id: 119093005)

5Your testimonies are fully confirmed; holiness adorns Your house, O LORD, for all the days to come.


## Psalms 94:1 (id: 119094001)

1O LORD, God of vengeance, O God of vengeance, shine forth.


## Psalms 94:2 (id: 119094002)

2Rise up, O Judge of the earth; render a reward to the proud.


## Psalms 94:3 (id: 119094003)

3How long will the wicked, O LORD, how long will the wicked exult?


## Psalms 94:4 (id: 119094004)

4They pour out arrogant words; all workers of iniquity boast.


## Psalms 94:5 (id: 119094005)

5They crush Your people, O LORD; they oppress Your heritage.


## Psalms 94:6 (id: 119094006)

6They kill the widow and the foreigner; they murder the fatherless.


## Psalms 94:7 (id: 119094007)

7They say, “The LORD does not see; the God of Jacob pays no heed.”


## Psalms 94:8 (id: 119094008)

8Take notice, O senseless among the people! O fools, when will you be wise?


## Psalms 94:9 (id: 119094009)

9He who affixed the ear, can He not hear? He who formed the eye, can He not see?


## Psalms 94:10 (id: 119094010)

10He who admonishes the nations, does He not discipline? He who teaches man, does He lack knowledge?


## Psalms 94:11 (id: 119094011)

11The LORD knows the thoughts of man, that they are futile.


## Psalms 94:12 (id: 119094012)

12Blessed is the man You discipline, O LORD, and teach from Your law,


## Psalms 94:13 (id: 119094013)

13to grant him relief from days of trouble, until a pit is dug for the wicked.


## Psalms 94:14 (id: 119094014)

14For the LORD will not forsake His people; He will never abandon His heritage.


## Psalms 94:15 (id: 119094015)

15Surely judgment will again be righteous, and all the upright in heart will follow it.


## Psalms 94:16 (id: 119094016)

16Who will rise up for me against the wicked? Who will stand for me against the workers of iniquity?


## Psalms 94:17 (id: 119094017)

17Unless the LORD had been my helper, I would soon have dwelt in the abode of silence.


## Psalms 94:18 (id: 119094018)

18If I say, “My foot is slipping,” Your loving devotion, O LORD, supports me.


## Psalms 94:19 (id: 119094019)

19When anxiety overwhelms me, Your consolation delights my soul.


## Psalms 94:20 (id: 119094020)

20Can a corrupt throne be Your ally—one devising mischief by decree?


## Psalms 94:21 (id: 119094021)

21They band together against the righteous and condemn the innocent to death.


## Psalms 94:22 (id: 119094022)

22But the LORD has been my stronghold, and my God is my rock of refuge.


## Psalms 94:23 (id: 119094023)

23He will bring upon them their own iniquity and destroy them for their wickedness. The LORD our God will destroy them.


## Psalms 95:1 (id: 119095001)

1Come, let us sing for joy to the LORD; let us shout to the Rock of our salvation!


## Psalms 95:2 (id: 119095002)

2Let us enter His presence with thanksgiving; let us make a joyful noise to Him in song.


## Psalms 95:3 (id: 119095003)

3For the LORD is a great God, a great King above all gods.


## Psalms 95:4 (id: 119095004)

4In His hand are the depths of the earth, and the mountain peaks belong to Him.


## Psalms 95:5 (id: 119095005)

5The sea is His, for He made it, and His hands formed the dry land.


## Psalms 95:6 (id: 119095006)

6O come, let us worship and bow down; let us kneel before the LORD our Maker.


## Psalms 95:7 (id: 119095007)

7For He is our God, and we are the people of His pasture, the sheep under His care. Today, if you hear His voice,


## Psalms 95:8 (id: 119095008)

8do not harden your hearts as you did at Meribah, in the day at Massah in the wilderness,


## Psalms 95:9 (id: 119095009)

9where your fathers tested and tried Me, though they had seen My work.


## Psalms 95:10 (id: 119095010)

10For forty years I was angry with that generation, and I said, “They are a people whose hearts go astray, and they have not known My ways.”


## Psalms 95:11 (id: 119095011)

11So I swore on oath in My anger, “They shall never enter My rest.”


## Psalms 96:1 (id: 119096001)

1Sing to the LORD a new song; sing to the LORD, all the earth.


## Psalms 96:2 (id: 119096002)

2Sing to the LORD, bless His name; proclaim His salvation day after day.


## Psalms 96:3 (id: 119096003)

3Declare His glory among the nations, His wonders among all peoples.


## Psalms 96:4 (id: 119096004)

4For great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised; He is to be feared above all gods.


## Psalms 96:5 (id: 119096005)

5For all the gods of the nations are idols, but it is the LORD who made the heavens.


## Psalms 96:6 (id: 119096006)

6Splendor and majesty are before Him; strength and beauty fill His sanctuary.


## Psalms 96:7 (id: 119096007)

7Ascribe to the LORD, O families of the nations, ascribe to the LORD glory and strength.


## Psalms 96:8 (id: 119096008)

8Ascribe to the LORD the glory due His name; bring an offering and enter His courts.


## Psalms 96:9 (id: 119096009)

9Worship the LORD in the splendor of His holiness; tremble before Him, all the earth.


## Psalms 96:10 (id: 119096010)

10Declare among the nations: “The LORD reigns!” The world is firmly established; it cannot be moved; He will judge the peoples with equity.


## Psalms 96:11 (id: 119096011)

11Let the heavens be glad and the earth rejoice; let the sea resound, and all that fills it.


## Psalms 96:12 (id: 119096012)

12Let the fields exult, and all that is in them. Then all the trees of the forest will sing for joy


## Psalms 96:13 (id: 119096013)

13before the LORD, for He is coming—He is coming to judge the earth. He will judge the world in righteousness and the peoples in His faithfulness.


## Psalms 97:1 (id: 119097001)

1The LORD reigns, let the earth rejoice; let the distant shores be glad.


## Psalms 97:2 (id: 119097002)

2Clouds and darkness surround Him; righteousness and justice are His throne’s foundation.


## Psalms 97:3 (id: 119097003)

3Fire goes before Him and consumes His foes on every side.


## Psalms 97:4 (id: 119097004)

4His lightning illuminates the world; the earth sees and trembles.


## Psalms 97:5 (id: 119097005)

5The mountains melt like wax at the presence of the LORD, before the Lord of all the earth.


## Psalms 97:6 (id: 119097006)

6The heavens proclaim His righteousness; all the peoples see His glory.


## Psalms 97:7 (id: 119097007)

7All worshipers of images are put to shame—those who boast in idols. Worship Him, all you gods!


## Psalms 97:8 (id: 119097008)

8Zion hears and rejoices, and the towns of Judah exult because of Your judgments, O LORD.


## Psalms 97:9 (id: 119097009)

9For You, O LORD, are Most High over all the earth; You are exalted far above all gods.


## Psalms 97:10 (id: 119097010)

10Hate evil, O you who love the LORD! He preserves the souls of His saints; He delivers them from the hand of the wicked.


## Psalms 97:11 (id: 119097011)

11Light shines on the righteous, gladness on the upright in heart.


## Psalms 97:12 (id: 119097012)

12Rejoice in the LORD, you righteous ones, and praise His holy name.


## Psalms 98:0 (id: 119098000)

0A Psalm.


## Psalms 98:1 (id: 119098001)

1Sing to the LORD a new song, for He has done wonders; His right hand and holy arm have gained Him the victory.


## Psalms 98:2 (id: 119098002)

2The LORD has proclaimed His salvation and revealed His righteousness to the nations.


## Psalms 98:3 (id: 119098003)

3He has remembered His love and faithfulness to the house of Israel; all the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God.


## Psalms 98:4 (id: 119098004)

4Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all the earth; break forth—let your cry ring out, and sing praises!


## Psalms 98:5 (id: 119098005)

5Sing praises to the LORD with the lyre, in melodious song with the harp.


## Psalms 98:6 (id: 119098006)

6With trumpets and the blast of the ram’s horn shout for joy before the LORD, the King.


## Psalms 98:7 (id: 119098007)

7Let the sea resound, and all that fills it, the world, and all who dwell in it.


## Psalms 98:8 (id: 119098008)

8Let the rivers clap their hands, let the mountains sing together for joy


## Psalms 98:9 (id: 119098009)

9before the LORD, for He comes to judge the earth. He will judge the world with righteousness and the peoples with equity.


## Psalms 99:1 (id: 119099001)

1The LORD reigns; let the nations tremble! He is enthroned above the cherubim; let the earth quake!


## Psalms 99:2 (id: 119099002)

2Great is the LORD in Zion; He is exalted above all the peoples.


## Psalms 99:3 (id: 119099003)

3Let them praise Your great and awesome name—He is holy!


## Psalms 99:4 (id: 119099004)

4The mighty King loves justice. You have established equity; You have exercised justice and righteousness in Jacob.


## Psalms 99:5 (id: 119099005)

5Exalt the LORD our God, and worship at His footstool; He is holy!


## Psalms 99:6 (id: 119099006)

6Moses and Aaron were among His priests; Samuel was among those who called on His name. They called to the LORD and He answered.


## Psalms 99:7 (id: 119099007)

7He spoke to them from the pillar of cloud; they kept His decrees and the statutes He gave them.


## Psalms 99:8 (id: 119099008)

8O LORD our God, You answered them. You were a forgiving God to them, yet an avenger of their misdeeds.


## Psalms 99:9 (id: 119099009)

9Exalt the LORD our God and worship at His holy mountain, for the LORD our God is holy.


## Psalms 100:0 (id: 119100000)

0A Psalm of thanksgiving.


## Psalms 100:1 (id: 119100001)

1Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all the earth.


## Psalms 100:2 (id: 119100002)

2Serve the LORD with gladness; come into His presence with joyful songs.


## Psalms 100:3 (id: 119100003)

3Know that the LORD is God. It is He who made us, and we are His; we are His people, and the sheep of His pasture.


## Psalms 100:4 (id: 119100004)

4Enter His gates with thanksgiving and His courts with praise; give thanks to Him and bless His name.


## Psalms 100:5 (id: 119100005)

5For the LORD is good, and His loving devotion endures forever; His faithfulness continues to all generations.


## Psalms 101:0 (id: 119101000)

0A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 101:1 (id: 119101001)

1I will sing of Your loving devotion and justice; to You, O LORD, I will sing praises.


## Psalms 101:2 (id: 119101002)

2I will ponder the way that is blameless—when will You come to me? I will walk in my house with integrity of heart.


## Psalms 101:3 (id: 119101003)

3I will set no worthless thing before my eyes. I hate the work of those who fall away; it shall not cling to me.


## Psalms 101:4 (id: 119101004)

4A perverse heart shall depart from me; I will know nothing of evil.


## Psalms 101:5 (id: 119101005)

5Whoever slanders his neighbor in secret, I will put to silence; the one with haughty eyes and a proud heart, I will not endure.


## Psalms 101:6 (id: 119101006)

6My eyes favor the faithful of the land, that they may dwell with me; he who walks in the way of integrity shall minister to me.


## Psalms 101:7 (id: 119101007)

7No one who practices deceit shall dwell in my house; no one who tells lies shall stand in my presence.


## Psalms 101:8 (id: 119101008)

8Every morning I will remove all the wicked of the land, that I may cut off every evildoer from the city of the LORD.


## Psalms 102:0 (id: 119102000)

0A prayer of one who is afflicted, when he grows faint and pours out his lament before the LORD.


## Psalms 102:1 (id: 119102001)

1Hear my prayer, O LORD; let my cry for help come before You.


## Psalms 102:2 (id: 119102002)

2Do not hide Your face from me in my day of distress. Incline Your ear to me; answer me quickly when I call.


## Psalms 102:3 (id: 119102003)

3For my days vanish like smoke, and my bones burn like glowing embers.


## Psalms 102:4 (id: 119102004)

4My heart is afflicted, and withered like grass; I even forget to eat my bread.


## Psalms 102:5 (id: 119102005)

5Through my loud groaning my skin hangs on my bones.


## Psalms 102:6 (id: 119102006)

6I am like a desert owl, like an owl among the ruins.


## Psalms 102:7 (id: 119102007)

7I lie awake; I am like a lone bird on a housetop.


## Psalms 102:8 (id: 119102008)

8All day long my enemies taunt me; they ridicule me and curse me.


## Psalms 102:9 (id: 119102009)

9For I have eaten ashes like bread and mixed my drink with tears


## Psalms 102:10 (id: 119102010)

10because of Your indignation and wrath, for You have picked me up and cast me aside.


## Psalms 102:11 (id: 119102011)

11My days are like lengthening shadows, and I wither away like grass.


## Psalms 102:12 (id: 119102012)

12But You, O LORD, sit enthroned forever; Your renown endures to all generations.


## Psalms 102:13 (id: 119102013)

13You will rise up and have compassion on Zion, for it is time to show her favor—the appointed time has come.


## Psalms 102:14 (id: 119102014)

14For Your servants delight in her stones and take pity on her dust.


## Psalms 102:15 (id: 119102015)

15So the nations will fear the name of the LORD, and all the kings of the earth will fear Your glory.


## Psalms 102:16 (id: 119102016)

16For the LORD will rebuild Zion; He has appeared in His glory.


## Psalms 102:17 (id: 119102017)

17He will turn toward the prayer of the destitute; He will not despise their prayer.


## Psalms 102:18 (id: 119102018)

18Let this be written for the generation to come, so that a people not yet created may praise the LORD.


## Psalms 102:19 (id: 119102019)

19For He looked down from the heights of His sanctuary; the LORD gazed out from heaven to earth


## Psalms 102:20 (id: 119102020)

20to hear a prisoner’s groaning, to release those condemned to death,


## Psalms 102:21 (id: 119102021)

21that they may proclaim the name of the LORD in Zion and praise Him in Jerusalem,


## Psalms 102:22 (id: 119102022)

22when peoples and kingdoms assemble to serve the LORD.


## Psalms 102:23 (id: 119102023)

23He has broken my strength on the way; He has cut short my days.


## Psalms 102:24 (id: 119102024)

24I say: “O my God, do not take me in the midst of my days! Your years go on through all generations.


## Psalms 102:25 (id: 119102025)

25In the beginning You laid the foundations of the earth, and the heavens are the work of Your hands.
