## Psalms 102:26 (id: 119102026)

26They will perish, but You remain; they will all wear out like a garment. Like clothing You will change them, and they will be passed on.


## Psalms 102:27 (id: 119102027)

27But You remain the same, and Your years will never end.


## Psalms 102:28 (id: 119102028)

28The children of Your servants will dwell securely, and their descendants will be established before You.”


## Psalms 103:0 (id: 119103000)

0Of David.


## Psalms 103:1 (id: 119103001)

1Bless the LORD, O my soul; all that is within me, bless His holy name.


## Psalms 103:2 (id: 119103002)

2Bless the LORD, O my soul, and do not forget all His kind deeds—


## Psalms 103:3 (id: 119103003)

3He who forgives all your iniquities and heals all your diseases,


## Psalms 103:4 (id: 119103004)

4who redeems your life from the Pit and crowns you with loving devotion and compassion,


## Psalms 103:5 (id: 119103005)

5who satisfies you with good things, so that your youth is renewed like the eagle’s.


## Psalms 103:6 (id: 119103006)

6The LORD executes righteousness and justice for all the oppressed.


## Psalms 103:7 (id: 119103007)

7He made known His ways to Moses, His deeds to the people of Israel.


## Psalms 103:8 (id: 119103008)

8The LORD is compassionate and gracious, slow to anger, abounding in loving devotion.


## Psalms 103:9 (id: 119103009)

9He will not always accuse us, nor harbor His anger forever.


## Psalms 103:10 (id: 119103010)

10He has not dealt with us according to our sins or repaid us according to our iniquities.


## Psalms 103:11 (id: 119103011)

11For as high as the heavens are above the earth, so great is His loving devotion for those who fear Him.


## Psalms 103:12 (id: 119103012)

12As far as the east is from the west, so far has He removed our transgressions from us.


## Psalms 103:13 (id: 119103013)

13As a father has compassion on his children, so the LORD has compassion on those who fear Him.


## Psalms 103:14 (id: 119103014)

14For He knows our frame; He is mindful that we are dust.


## Psalms 103:15 (id: 119103015)

15As for man, his days are like grass—he blooms like a flower of the field;


## Psalms 103:16 (id: 119103016)

16when the wind passes over, it vanishes, and its place remembers it no more.


## Psalms 103:17 (id: 119103017)

17But from everlasting to everlasting the loving devotion of the LORD extends to those who fear Him, and His righteousness to their children’s children—


## Psalms 103:18 (id: 119103018)

18to those who keep His covenant and remember to obey His precepts.


## Psalms 103:19 (id: 119103019)

19The LORD has established His throne in heaven, and His kingdom rules over all.


## Psalms 103:20 (id: 119103020)

20Bless the LORD, all His angels mighty in strength who carry out His word, who hearken to the voice of His command.


## Psalms 103:21 (id: 119103021)

21Bless the LORD, all His hosts, you servants who do His will.


## Psalms 103:22 (id: 119103022)

22Bless the LORD, all His works in all places of His dominion. Bless the LORD, O my soul!


## Psalms 104:1 (id: 119104001)

1Bless the LORD, O my soul! O LORD my God, You are very great; You are clothed with splendor and majesty.


## Psalms 104:2 (id: 119104002)

2He wraps Himself in light as with a garment; He stretches out the heavens like a tent,


## Psalms 104:3 (id: 119104003)

3laying the beams of His chambers in the waters above, making the clouds His chariot, walking on the wings of the wind.


## Psalms 104:4 (id: 119104004)

4He makes the winds His messengers, flames of fire His servants.


## Psalms 104:5 (id: 119104005)

5He set the earth on its foundations, never to be moved.


## Psalms 104:6 (id: 119104006)

6You covered it with the deep like a garment; the waters stood above the mountains.


## Psalms 104:7 (id: 119104007)

7At Your rebuke the waters fled; at the sound of Your thunder they hurried away—


## Psalms 104:8 (id: 119104008)

8the mountains rose and the valleys sank to the place You assigned for them—


## Psalms 104:9 (id: 119104009)

9You set a boundary they cannot cross, that they may never again cover the earth.


## Psalms 104:10 (id: 119104010)

10He sends forth springs in the valleys; they flow between the mountains.


## Psalms 104:11 (id: 119104011)

11They give drink to every beast of the field; the wild donkeys quench their thirst.


## Psalms 104:12 (id: 119104012)

12The birds of the air nest beside the springs; they sing among the branches.


## Psalms 104:13 (id: 119104013)

13He waters the mountains from His chambers; the earth is satisfied by the fruit of His works.


## Psalms 104:14 (id: 119104014)

14He makes the grass grow for the livestock and provides crops for man to cultivate, bringing forth food from the earth:


## Psalms 104:15 (id: 119104015)

15wine that gladdens the heart of man, oil that makes his face to shine, and bread that sustains his heart.


## Psalms 104:16 (id: 119104016)

16The trees of the LORD have their fill, the cedars of Lebanon that He planted,


## Psalms 104:17 (id: 119104017)

17where the birds build their nests; the stork makes her home in the cypresses.


## Psalms 104:18 (id: 119104018)

18The high mountains are for the wild goats, the cliffs a refuge for the rock badgers.


## Psalms 104:19 (id: 119104019)

19He made the moon to mark the seasons; the sun knows when to set.


## Psalms 104:20 (id: 119104020)

20You bring darkness, and it becomes night, when all the beasts of the forest prowl.


## Psalms 104:21 (id: 119104021)

21The young lions roar for their prey and seek their food from God.


## Psalms 104:22 (id: 119104022)

22The sun rises, and they withdraw; they lie down in their dens.


## Psalms 104:23 (id: 119104023)

23Man goes forth to his work and to his labor until evening.


## Psalms 104:24 (id: 119104024)

24How many are Your works, O LORD! In wisdom You have made them all; the earth is full of Your creatures.


## Psalms 104:25 (id: 119104025)

25Here is the sea, vast and wide, teeming with creatures beyond number, living things both great and small.


## Psalms 104:26 (id: 119104026)

26There the ships pass, and Leviathan, which You formed to frolic there.


## Psalms 104:27 (id: 119104027)

27All creatures look to You to give them their food in due season.


## Psalms 104:28 (id: 119104028)

28When You give it to them, they gather it up; when You open Your hand, they are satisfied with good things.


## Psalms 104:29 (id: 119104029)

29When You hide Your face, they are terrified; when You take away their breath, they die and return to dust.


## Psalms 104:30 (id: 119104030)

30When You send Your Spirit, they are created, and You renew the face of the earth.


## Psalms 104:31 (id: 119104031)

31May the glory of the LORD endure forever; may the LORD rejoice in His works.


## Psalms 104:32 (id: 119104032)

32He looks on the earth, and it trembles; He touches the mountains, and they smolder.


## Psalms 104:33 (id: 119104033)

33I will sing to the LORD all my life; I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.


## Psalms 104:34 (id: 119104034)

34May my meditation be pleasing to Him, for I rejoice in the LORD.


## Psalms 104:35 (id: 119104035)

35May sinners vanish from the earth and the wicked be no more. Bless the LORD, O my soul. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 105:1 (id: 119105001)

1Give thanks to the LORD, call upon His name; make known His deeds among the nations.


## Psalms 105:2 (id: 119105002)

2Sing to Him, sing praises to Him; tell of all His wonders.


## Psalms 105:3 (id: 119105003)

3Glory in His holy name; let the hearts of those who seek the LORD rejoice.


## Psalms 105:4 (id: 119105004)

4Seek out the LORD and His strength; seek His face always.


## Psalms 105:5 (id: 119105005)

5Remember the wonders He has done, His marvels, and the judgments He has pronounced,


## Psalms 105:6 (id: 119105006)

6O offspring of His servant Abraham, O sons of Jacob, His chosen ones.


## Psalms 105:7 (id: 119105007)

7He is the LORD our God; His judgments carry throughout the earth.


## Psalms 105:8 (id: 119105008)

8He remembers His covenant forever, the word He ordained for a thousand generations—


## Psalms 105:9 (id: 119105009)

9the covenant He made with Abraham, and the oath He swore to Isaac.


## Psalms 105:10 (id: 119105010)

10He confirmed it to Jacob as a decree, to Israel as an everlasting covenant:


## Psalms 105:11 (id: 119105011)

11“I will give you the land of Canaan as the portion of your inheritance.”


## Psalms 105:12 (id: 119105012)

12When they were few in number, few indeed, and strangers in the land,


## Psalms 105:13 (id: 119105013)

13they wandered from nation to nation, from one kingdom to another.


## Psalms 105:14 (id: 119105014)

14He let no man oppress them; He rebuked kings on their behalf:


## Psalms 105:15 (id: 119105015)

15“Do not touch My anointed ones! Do no harm to My prophets!”


## Psalms 105:16 (id: 119105016)

16He called down famine on the land and cut off all their supplies of food.


## Psalms 105:17 (id: 119105017)

17He sent a man before them—Joseph, sold as a slave.


## Psalms 105:18 (id: 119105018)

18They bruised his feet with shackles and placed his neck in irons,


## Psalms 105:19 (id: 119105019)

19until his prediction came true and the word of the LORD proved him right.


## Psalms 105:20 (id: 119105020)

20The king sent and released him; the ruler of peoples set him free.


## Psalms 105:21 (id: 119105021)

21He made him master of his household, ruler over all his substance,


## Psalms 105:22 (id: 119105022)

22to instruct his princes as he pleased and teach his elders wisdom.


## Psalms 105:23 (id: 119105023)

23Then Israel entered Egypt; Jacob dwelt in the land of Ham.


## Psalms 105:24 (id: 119105024)

24And the LORD made His people very fruitful, more numerous than their foes,


## Psalms 105:25 (id: 119105025)

25whose hearts He turned to hate His people, to conspire against His servants.


## Psalms 105:26 (id: 119105026)

26He sent Moses His servant, and Aaron, whom He had chosen.


## Psalms 105:27 (id: 119105027)

27They performed His miraculous signs among them, and wonders in the land of Ham.


## Psalms 105:28 (id: 119105028)

28He sent darkness, and it became dark—yet they defied His words.


## Psalms 105:29 (id: 119105029)

29He turned their waters to blood and caused their fish to die.


## Psalms 105:30 (id: 119105030)

30Their land teemed with frogs, even in their royal chambers.


## Psalms 105:31 (id: 119105031)

31He spoke, and insects swarmed—gnats throughout their country.


## Psalms 105:32 (id: 119105032)

32He gave them hail for rain, with lightning throughout their land.


## Psalms 105:33 (id: 119105033)

33He struck their vines and fig trees and shattered the trees of their country.


## Psalms 105:34 (id: 119105034)

34He spoke, and the locusts came—young locusts without number.


## Psalms 105:35 (id: 119105035)

35They devoured every plant in their land and consumed the produce of their soil.


## Psalms 105:36 (id: 119105036)

36Then He struck all the firstborn in their land, the firstfruits of all their vigor.


## Psalms 105:37 (id: 119105037)

37He brought Israel out with silver and gold, and none among His tribes stumbled.


## Psalms 105:38 (id: 119105038)

38Egypt was glad when they departed, for the dread of Israel had fallen on them.


## Psalms 105:39 (id: 119105039)

39He spread a cloud as a covering and a fire to light up the night.


## Psalms 105:40 (id: 119105040)

40They asked, and He brought quail and satisfied them with the bread of heaven.


## Psalms 105:41 (id: 119105041)

41He opened a rock, and water gushed out; it flowed like a river in the desert.


## Psalms 105:42 (id: 119105042)

42For He remembered His holy promise to Abraham His servant.


## Psalms 105:43 (id: 119105043)

43He brought forth His people with rejoicing, His chosen with shouts of joy.


## Psalms 105:44 (id: 119105044)

44He gave them the lands of the nations, that they might inherit the fruit of others’ labor,


## Psalms 105:45 (id: 119105045)

45that they might keep His statutes and obey His laws. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 106:1 (id: 119106001)

1Hallelujah! Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good; His loving devotion endures forever.


## Psalms 106:2 (id: 119106002)

2Who can describe the mighty acts of the LORD or fully proclaim His praise?


## Psalms 106:3 (id: 119106003)

3Blessed are those who uphold justice, who practice righteousness at all times.


## Psalms 106:4 (id: 119106004)

4Remember me, O LORD, in Your favor to Your people; visit me with Your salvation,


## Psalms 106:5 (id: 119106005)

5that I may see the prosperity of Your chosen ones, and rejoice in the gladness of Your nation, and give glory with Your inheritance.


## Psalms 106:6 (id: 119106006)

6We have sinned like our fathers; we have done wrong and acted wickedly.


## Psalms 106:7 (id: 119106007)

7Our fathers in Egypt did not grasp Your wonders or remember Your abundant kindness; but they rebelled by the sea, there at the Red Sea.


## Psalms 106:8 (id: 119106008)

8Yet He saved them for the sake of His name, to make His power known.


## Psalms 106:9 (id: 119106009)

9He rebuked the Red Sea, and it dried up; He led them through the depths as through a desert.


## Psalms 106:10 (id: 119106010)

10He saved them from the hand that hated them; He redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.


## Psalms 106:11 (id: 119106011)

11The waters covered their foes; not one of them remained.


## Psalms 106:12 (id: 119106012)

12Then they believed His promises and sang His praise.


## Psalms 106:13 (id: 119106013)

13Yet they soon forgot His works and failed to wait for His counsel.


## Psalms 106:14 (id: 119106014)

14They craved intensely in the wilderness and tested God in the desert.


## Psalms 106:15 (id: 119106015)

15So He granted their request, but sent a wasting disease upon them.


## Psalms 106:16 (id: 119106016)

16In the camp they envied Moses, as well as Aaron, the holy one of the LORD.


## Psalms 106:17 (id: 119106017)

17The earth opened up and swallowed Dathan; it covered the assembly of Abiram.


## Psalms 106:18 (id: 119106018)

18Then fire blazed through their company; flames consumed the wicked.


## Psalms 106:19 (id: 119106019)

19At Horeb they made a calf and worshiped a molten image.


## Psalms 106:20 (id: 119106020)

20They exchanged their Glory for the image of a grass\-eating ox.


## Psalms 106:21 (id: 119106021)

21They forgot God their Savior, who did great things in Egypt,


## Psalms 106:22 (id: 119106022)

22wondrous works in the land of Ham, and awesome deeds by the Red Sea.


## Psalms 106:23 (id: 119106023)

23So He said He would destroy them—had not Moses His chosen one stood before Him in the breach to divert His wrath from destroying them.


## Psalms 106:24 (id: 119106024)

24They despised the pleasant land; they did not believe His promise.


## Psalms 106:25 (id: 119106025)

25They grumbled in their tents and did not listen to the voice of the LORD.


## Psalms 106:26 (id: 119106026)

26So He raised His hand and swore to cast them down in the wilderness,


## Psalms 106:27 (id: 119106027)

27to disperse their offspring among the nations and scatter them throughout the lands.


## Psalms 106:28 (id: 119106028)

28They yoked themselves to Baal of Peor and ate sacrifices offered to lifeless gods.


## Psalms 106:29 (id: 119106029)

29So they provoked the LORD to anger with their deeds, and a plague broke out among them.


## Psalms 106:30 (id: 119106030)

30But Phinehas stood and intervened, and the plague was restrained.


## Psalms 106:31 (id: 119106031)

31It was credited to him as righteousness for endless generations to come.


## Psalms 106:32 (id: 119106032)

32At the waters of Meribah they angered the LORD, and trouble came to Moses because of them.


## Psalms 106:33 (id: 119106033)

33For they rebelled against His Spirit, and Moses spoke rashly with his lips.


## Psalms 106:34 (id: 119106034)

34They did not destroy the peoples as the LORD had commanded them,


## Psalms 106:35 (id: 119106035)

35but they mingled with the nations and adopted their customs.


## Psalms 106:36 (id: 119106036)

36They worshiped their idols, which became a snare to them.


## Psalms 106:37 (id: 119106037)

37They sacrificed their sons and their daughters to demons.


## Psalms 106:38 (id: 119106038)

38They shed innocent blood—the blood of their sons and daughters, whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan, and the land was polluted with blood.


## Psalms 106:39 (id: 119106039)

39They defiled themselves by their actions and prostituted themselves by their deeds.


## Psalms 106:40 (id: 119106040)

40So the anger of the LORD burned against His people, and He abhorred His own inheritance.


## Psalms 106:41 (id: 119106041)

41He delivered them into the hand of the nations, and those who hated them ruled over them.


## Psalms 106:42 (id: 119106042)

42Their enemies oppressed them and subdued them under their hand.


## Psalms 106:43 (id: 119106043)

43Many times He rescued them, but they were bent on rebellion and sank down in their iniquity.


## Psalms 106:44 (id: 119106044)

44Nevertheless He heard their cry; He took note of their distress.


## Psalms 106:45 (id: 119106045)

45And He remembered His covenant with them, and relented by the abundance of His loving devotion.


## Psalms 106:46 (id: 119106046)

46He made them objects of compassion to all who held them captive.


## Psalms 106:47 (id: 119106047)

47Save us, O LORD our God, and gather us from the nations, that we may give thanks to Your holy name, that we may glory in Your praise.


## Psalms 106:48 (id: 119106048)

48Blessed be the LORD, the God of Israel, from everlasting to everlasting. Let all the people say, “Amen!” Hallelujah!


## Psalms 107:1 (id: 119107001)

1Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good; His loving devotion endures forever.


## Psalms 107:2 (id: 119107002)

2Let the redeemed of the LORD say so, whom He has redeemed from the hand of the enemy


## Psalms 107:3 (id: 119107003)

3and gathered from the lands, from east and west, from north and south.


## Psalms 107:4 (id: 119107004)

4Some wandered in desert wastelands, finding no path to a city in which to dwell.


## Psalms 107:5 (id: 119107005)

5They were hungry and thirsty; their soul fainted within them.


## Psalms 107:6 (id: 119107006)

6Then they cried out to the LORD in their trouble, and He delivered them from their distress.


## Psalms 107:7 (id: 119107007)

7He led them on a straight path to reach a city where they could live.


## Psalms 107:8 (id: 119107008)

8Let them give thanks to the LORD for His loving devotion and His wonders to the sons of men.


## Psalms 107:9 (id: 119107009)

9For He satisfies the thirsty and fills the hungry with good things.


## Psalms 107:10 (id: 119107010)

10Some sat in darkness and in the shadow of death, prisoners in affliction and chains,


## Psalms 107:11 (id: 119107011)

11because they rebelled against the words of God and despised the counsel of the Most High.


## Psalms 107:12 (id: 119107012)

12He humbled their hearts with hard labor; they stumbled, and there was no one to help.


## Psalms 107:13 (id: 119107013)

13Then they cried out to the LORD in their trouble, and He saved them from their distress.


## Psalms 107:14 (id: 119107014)

14He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death and broke away their chains.


## Psalms 107:15 (id: 119107015)

15Let them give thanks to the LORD for His loving devotion and His wonders to the sons of men.


## Psalms 107:16 (id: 119107016)

16For He has broken down the gates of bronze and cut through the bars of iron.


## Psalms 107:17 (id: 119107017)

17Fools, in their rebellious ways, and through their iniquities, suffered affliction.


## Psalms 107:18 (id: 119107018)

18They loathed all food and drew near to the gates of death.


## Psalms 107:19 (id: 119107019)

19Then they cried out to the LORD in their trouble, and He saved them from their distress.


## Psalms 107:20 (id: 119107020)

20He sent forth His word and healed them; He rescued them from the Pit.


## Psalms 107:21 (id: 119107021)

21Let them give thanks to the LORD for His loving devotion and His wonders to the sons of men.


## Psalms 107:22 (id: 119107022)

22Let them offer sacrifices of thanksgiving and declare His works with rejoicing.


## Psalms 107:23 (id: 119107023)

23Others went out to sea in ships, conducting trade on the mighty waters.


## Psalms 107:24 (id: 119107024)

24They saw the works of the LORD, and His wonders in the deep.


## Psalms 107:25 (id: 119107025)

25For He spoke and raised a tempest that lifted the waves of the sea.


## Psalms 107:26 (id: 119107026)

26They mounted up to the heavens, then sunk to the depths; their courage melted in their anguish.


## Psalms 107:27 (id: 119107027)

27They reeled and staggered like drunkards, and all their skill was useless.


## Psalms 107:28 (id: 119107028)

28Then they cried out to the LORD in their trouble, and He brought them out of their distress.


## Psalms 107:29 (id: 119107029)

29He calmed the storm to a whisper, and the waves of the sea were hushed.


## Psalms 107:30 (id: 119107030)

30They rejoiced in the silence, and He guided them to the harbor they desired.


## Psalms 107:31 (id: 119107031)

31Let them give thanks to the LORD for His loving devotion and His wonders to the sons of men.


## Psalms 107:32 (id: 119107032)

32Let them exalt Him in the assembly of the people and praise Him in the council of the elders.


## Psalms 107:33 (id: 119107033)

33He turns rivers into deserts, springs of water into thirsty ground,


## Psalms 107:34 (id: 119107034)

34and fruitful land into fields of salt, because of the wickedness of its dwellers.


## Psalms 107:35 (id: 119107035)

35He turns a desert into pools of water and a dry land into flowing springs.


## Psalms 107:36 (id: 119107036)

36He causes the hungry to settle there, that they may establish a city in which to dwell.


## Psalms 107:37 (id: 119107037)

37They sow fields and plant vineyards that yield a fruitful harvest.


## Psalms 107:38 (id: 119107038)

38He blesses them, and they multiply greatly; He does not let their herds diminish.


## Psalms 107:39 (id: 119107039)

39When they are decreased and humbled by oppression, evil, and sorrow,


## Psalms 107:40 (id: 119107040)

40He pours out contempt on the nobles and makes them wander in a trackless wasteland.


## Psalms 107:41 (id: 119107041)

41But He lifts the needy from affliction and increases their families like flocks.


## Psalms 107:42 (id: 119107042)

42The upright see and rejoice, and all iniquity shuts its mouth.


## Psalms 107:43 (id: 119107043)

43Let him who is wise pay heed to these things and consider the loving devotion of the LORD.


## Psalms 108:0 (id: 119108000)

0A song. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 108:1 (id: 119108001)

1My heart is steadfast, O God; I will sing and make music with all my being.


## Psalms 108:2 (id: 119108002)

2Awake, O harp and lyre! I will awaken the dawn.


## Psalms 108:3 (id: 119108003)

3I will praise You, O LORD, among the nations; I will sing Your praises among the peoples.


## Psalms 108:4 (id: 119108004)

4For Your loving devotion extends beyond the heavens, and Your faithfulness reaches to the clouds.


## Psalms 108:5 (id: 119108005)

5Be exalted, O God, above the heavens; may Your glory cover all the earth.


## Psalms 108:6 (id: 119108006)

6Respond and save us with Your right hand, that Your beloved may be delivered.


## Psalms 108:7 (id: 119108007)

7God has spoken from His sanctuary: “I will triumph! I will parcel out Shechem and apportion the Valley of Succoth.


## Psalms 108:8 (id: 119108008)

8Gilead is Mine, and Manasseh is Mine; Ephraim is My helmet, Judah is My scepter.


## Psalms 108:9 (id: 119108009)

9Moab is My washbasin; upon Edom I toss My sandal; over Philistia I shout in triumph.”


## Psalms 108:10 (id: 119108010)

10Who will bring me to the fortified city? Who will lead me to Edom?


## Psalms 108:11 (id: 119108011)

11Have You not rejected us, O God? Will You no longer march out, O God, with our armies?


## Psalms 108:12 (id: 119108012)

12Give us aid against the enemy, for the help of man is worthless.


## Psalms 108:13 (id: 119108013)

13With God we will perform with valor, and He will trample our enemies.


## Psalms 109:0 (id: 119109000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 109:1 (id: 119109001)

1O God of my praise, be not silent.


## Psalms 109:2 (id: 119109002)

2For wicked and deceitful mouths open against me; they speak against me with lying tongues.


## Psalms 109:3 (id: 119109003)

3They surround me with hateful words and attack me without cause.


## Psalms 109:4 (id: 119109004)

4In return for my love they accuse me, but I am a man of prayer.


## Psalms 109:5 (id: 119109005)

5They repay me evil for good, and hatred for my love.


## Psalms 109:6 (id: 119109006)

6Set over him a wicked man; let an accuser stand at his right hand.


## Psalms 109:7 (id: 119109007)

7When he is tried, let him be found guilty, and may his prayer be regarded as sin.


## Psalms 109:8 (id: 119109008)

8May his days be few; may another take his position.


## Psalms 109:9 (id: 119109009)

9May his children be fatherless and his wife a widow.


## Psalms 109:10 (id: 119109010)

10May his children wander as beggars, seeking sustenance far from their ruined homes.


## Psalms 109:11 (id: 119109011)

11May the creditor seize all he owns, and strangers plunder the fruits of his labor.


## Psalms 109:12 (id: 119109012)

12May there be no one to extend kindness to him, and no one to favor his fatherless children.


## Psalms 109:13 (id: 119109013)

13May his descendants be cut off; may their name be blotted out from the next generation.


## Psalms 109:14 (id: 119109014)

14May the iniquity of his fathers be remembered before the LORD, and the sin of his mother never be blotted out.


## Psalms 109:15 (id: 119109015)

15May their sins always remain before the LORD, that He may cut off their memory from the earth.


## Psalms 109:16 (id: 119109016)

16For he never thought to show kindness, but pursued the poor and needy and brokenhearted, even to their death.


## Psalms 109:17 (id: 119109017)

17The cursing that he loved, may it fall on him; the blessing in which he refused to delight, may it be far from him.


## Psalms 109:18 (id: 119109018)

18The cursing that he wore like a coat, may it soak into his body like water, and into his bones like oil.


## Psalms 109:19 (id: 119109019)

19May it be like a robe wrapped about him, like a belt tied forever around him.


## Psalms 109:20 (id: 119109020)

20May this be the LORD’s reward to my accusers, to those who speak evil against me.


## Psalms 109:21 (id: 119109021)

21But You, O GOD, the Lord, deal kindly with me for the sake of Your name; deliver me by the goodness of Your loving devotion.


## Psalms 109:22 (id: 119109022)

22For I am poor and needy; my heart is wounded within me.


## Psalms 109:23 (id: 119109023)

23I am fading away like a lengthening shadow; I am shaken off like a locust.


## Psalms 109:24 (id: 119109024)

24My knees are weak from fasting, and my body grows lean and gaunt.


## Psalms 109:25 (id: 119109025)

25I am an object of scorn to my accusers; when they see me, they shake their heads.


## Psalms 109:26 (id: 119109026)

26Help me, O LORD my God; save me according to Your loving devotion.


## Psalms 109:27 (id: 119109027)

27Let them know that this is Your hand, that You, O LORD, have done it.


## Psalms 109:28 (id: 119109028)

28Though they curse, You will bless. When they rise up, they will be put to shame, but Your servant will rejoice.


## Psalms 109:29 (id: 119109029)

29May my accusers be clothed with disgrace; may they wear their shame like a robe.


## Psalms 109:30 (id: 119109030)

30With my mouth I will thank the LORD profusely; I will praise Him in the presence of many.


## Psalms 109:31 (id: 119109031)

31For He stands at the right hand of the needy one, to save him from the condemners of his soul.


## Psalms 110:0 (id: 119110000)

0A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 110:1 (id: 119110001)

1The LORD said to my Lord: “Sit at My right hand until I make Your enemies a footstool for Your feet.”


## Psalms 110:2 (id: 119110002)

2The LORD extends Your mighty scepter from Zion: “Rule in the midst of Your enemies.”


## Psalms 110:3 (id: 119110003)

3Your people shall be willing on Your day of battle. Arrayed in holy splendor, from the womb of the dawn, to You belongs the dew of Your youth.


## Psalms 110:4 (id: 119110004)

4The LORD has sworn and will not change His mind: “You are a priest forever in the order of Melchizedek.”


## Psalms 110:5 (id: 119110005)

5The Lord is at Your right hand; He will crush kings in the day of His wrath.


## Psalms 110:6 (id: 119110006)

6He will judge the nations, heaping up the dead; He will crush the leaders far and wide.


## Psalms 110:7 (id: 119110007)

7He will drink from the brook by the road; therefore He will lift up His head.


## Psalms 111:1 (id: 119111001)

1Hallelujah! I will give thanks to the LORD with all my heart in the council of the upright and in the assembly.


## Psalms 111:2 (id: 119111002)

2Great are the works of the LORD; they are pondered by all who delight in them.


## Psalms 111:3 (id: 119111003)

3Splendid and majestic is His work; His righteousness endures forever.


## Psalms 111:4 (id: 119111004)

4He has caused His wonders to be remembered; the LORD is gracious and compassionate.


## Psalms 111:5 (id: 119111005)

5He provides food for those who fear Him; He remembers His covenant forever.


## Psalms 111:6 (id: 119111006)

6He has shown His people the power of His works by giving them the inheritance of the nations.


## Psalms 111:7 (id: 119111007)

7The works of His hands are truth and justice; all His precepts are trustworthy.


## Psalms 111:8 (id: 119111008)

8They are upheld forever and ever, enacted in truth and uprightness.


## Psalms 111:9 (id: 119111009)

9He has sent redemption to His people; He has ordained His covenant forever; holy and awesome is His name.


## Psalms 111:10 (id: 119111010)

10The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom; all who follow His precepts gain rich understanding. His praise endures forever!


## Psalms 112:1 (id: 119112001)

1Hallelujah! Blessed is the man who fears the LORD, who greatly delights in His commandments.


## Psalms 112:2 (id: 119112002)

2His descendants will be mighty in the land; the generation of the upright will be blessed.


## Psalms 112:3 (id: 119112003)

3Wealth and riches are in his house, and his righteousness endures forever.


## Psalms 112:4 (id: 119112004)

4Light dawns in the darkness for the upright—for the gracious, compassionate, and righteous.


## Psalms 112:5 (id: 119112005)

5It is well with the man who is generous and lends freely, whose affairs are guided by justice.


## Psalms 112:6 (id: 119112006)

6Surely he will never be shaken; the righteous man will be remembered forever.


## Psalms 112:7 (id: 119112007)

7He does not fear bad news; his heart is steadfast, trusting in the LORD.


## Psalms 112:8 (id: 119112008)

8His heart is assured; he does not fear, until he looks in triumph on his foes.


## Psalms 112:9 (id: 119112009)

9He has scattered abroad his gifts to the poor; his righteousness endures forever; his horn will be lifted high in honor.


## Psalms 112:10 (id: 119112010)

10The wicked man will see and be grieved; he will gnash his teeth and waste away; the desires of the wicked will perish.


## Psalms 113:1 (id: 119113001)

1Hallelujah! Give praise, O servants of the LORD; praise the name of the LORD.


## Psalms 113:2 (id: 119113002)

2Blessed be the name of the LORD both now and forevermore.


## Psalms 113:3 (id: 119113003)

3From where the sun rises to where it sets, the name of the LORD is praised.


## Psalms 113:4 (id: 119113004)

4The LORD is exalted over all the nations, His glory above the heavens.


## Psalms 113:5 (id: 119113005)

5Who is like the LORD our God, the One enthroned on high?


## Psalms 113:6 (id: 119113006)

6He humbles Himself to behold the heavens and the earth.


## Psalms 113:7 (id: 119113007)

7He raises the poor from the dust and lifts the needy from the dump


## Psalms 113:8 (id: 119113008)

8to seat them with nobles, with the princes of His people.


## Psalms 113:9 (id: 119113009)

9He settles the barren woman in her home as a joyful mother to her children. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 114:1 (id: 119114001)

1When Israel departed from Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people of foreign tongue,


## Psalms 114:2 (id: 119114002)

2Judah became God’s sanctuary, Israel His dominion.


## Psalms 114:3 (id: 119114003)

3The sea observed and fled; the Jordan turned back;


## Psalms 114:4 (id: 119114004)

4the mountains skipped like rams, the hills like lambs.


## Psalms 114:5 (id: 119114005)

5Why was it, O sea, that you fled, O Jordan, that you turned back,


## Psalms 114:6 (id: 119114006)

6O mountains, that you skipped like rams, O hills, like lambs?


## Psalms 114:7 (id: 119114007)

7Tremble, O earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the presence of the God of Jacob,


## Psalms 114:8 (id: 119114008)

8who turned the rock into a pool, the flint into a fountain of water!


## Psalms 115:1 (id: 119115001)

1Not to us, O LORD, not to us, but to Your name be the glory, because of Your loving devotion, because of Your faithfulness.


## Psalms 115:2 (id: 119115002)

2Why should the nations say, “Where is their God?”


## Psalms 115:3 (id: 119115003)

3Our God is in heaven; He does as He pleases.


## Psalms 115:4 (id: 119115004)

4Their idols are silver and gold, made by the hands of men.


## Psalms 115:5 (id: 119115005)

5They have mouths, but cannot speak; they have eyes, but cannot see;


## Psalms 115:6 (id: 119115006)

6they have ears, but cannot hear; they have noses, but cannot smell;


## Psalms 115:7 (id: 119115007)

7they have hands, but cannot feel; they have feet, but cannot walk; they cannot even clear their throats.


## Psalms 115:8 (id: 119115008)

8Those who make them become like them, as do all who trust in them.


## Psalms 115:9 (id: 119115009)

9O Israel, trust in the LORD! He is their help and shield.


## Psalms 115:10 (id: 119115010)

10O house of Aaron, trust in the LORD! He is their help and shield.


## Psalms 115:11 (id: 119115011)

11You who fear the LORD, trust in the LORD! He is their help and shield.


## Psalms 115:12 (id: 119115012)

12The LORD is mindful of us; He will bless us. He will bless the house of Israel; He will bless the house of Aaron;


## Psalms 115:13 (id: 119115013)

13He will bless those who fear the LORD—small and great alike.


## Psalms 115:14 (id: 119115014)

14May the LORD give you increase, both you and your children.


## Psalms 115:15 (id: 119115015)

15May you be blessed by the LORD, the Maker of heaven and earth.


## Psalms 115:16 (id: 119115016)

16The highest heavens belong to the LORD, but the earth He has given to mankind.


## Psalms 115:17 (id: 119115017)

17It is not the dead who praise the LORD, nor any who descend into silence.


## Psalms 115:18 (id: 119115018)

18But it is we who will bless the LORD, both now and forevermore. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 116:1 (id: 119116001)

1I love the LORD, for He has heard my voice—my appeal for mercy.


## Psalms 116:2 (id: 119116002)

2Because He has inclined His ear to me, I will call on Him as long as I live.


## Psalms 116:3 (id: 119116003)

3The ropes of death entangled me; the anguish of Sheol overcame me; I was confronted by trouble and sorrow.


## Psalms 116:4 (id: 119116004)

4Then I called on the name of the LORD: “O LORD, deliver my soul!”


## Psalms 116:5 (id: 119116005)

5The LORD is gracious and righteous; our God is full of compassion.


## Psalms 116:6 (id: 119116006)

6The LORD preserves the simplehearted; I was helpless, and He saved me.


## Psalms 116:7 (id: 119116007)

7Return to your rest, O my soul, for the LORD has been good to you.


## Psalms 116:8 (id: 119116008)

8For You have delivered my soul from death, my eyes from tears, my feet from stumbling.


## Psalms 116:9 (id: 119116009)

9I will walk before the LORD in the land of the living.


## Psalms 116:10 (id: 119116010)

10I believed, therefore I said, “I am greatly afflicted.”


## Psalms 116:11 (id: 119116011)

11In my alarm I said, “All men are liars!”


## Psalms 116:12 (id: 119116012)

12How can I repay the LORD for all His goodness to me?


## Psalms 116:13 (id: 119116013)

13I will lift the cup of salvation and call on the name of the LORD.


## Psalms 116:14 (id: 119116014)

14I will fulfill my vows to the LORD in the presence of all His people.


## Psalms 116:15 (id: 119116015)

15Precious in the sight of the LORD is the death of His saints.


## Psalms 116:16 (id: 119116016)

16Truly, O LORD, I am Your servant; I am Your servant, the son of Your maidservant; You have broken my bonds.


## Psalms 116:17 (id: 119116017)

17I will offer to You a sacrifice of thanksgiving and call on the name of the LORD.


## Psalms 116:18 (id: 119116018)

18I will fulfill my vows to the LORD in the presence of all His people,


## Psalms 116:19 (id: 119116019)

19in the courts of the LORD’s house, in your midst, O Jerusalem. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 117:1 (id: 119117001)

1Praise the LORD, all you nations! Extol Him, all you peoples!


## Psalms 117:2 (id: 119117002)

2For great is His loving devotion toward us, and the faithfulness of the LORD endures forever. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 118:1 (id: 119118001)

1Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good; His loving devotion endures forever.


## Psalms 118:2 (id: 119118002)

2Let Israel say, “His loving devotion endures forever.”


## Psalms 118:3 (id: 119118003)

3Let the house of Aaron say, “His loving devotion endures forever.”


## Psalms 118:4 (id: 119118004)

4Let those who fear the LORD say, “His loving devotion endures forever.”


## Psalms 118:5 (id: 119118005)

5In my distress I called to the LORD, and He answered and set me free.


## Psalms 118:6 (id: 119118006)

6The LORD is on my side; I will not be afraid. What can man do to me?


## Psalms 118:7 (id: 119118007)

7The LORD is on my side; He is my helper. Therefore I will look in triumph on those who hate me.


## Psalms 118:8 (id: 119118008)

8It is better to take refuge in the LORD than to trust in man.


## Psalms 118:9 (id: 119118009)

9It is better to take refuge in the LORD than to trust in princes.


## Psalms 118:10 (id: 119118010)

10All the nations surrounded me, but in the name of the LORD I cut them off.


## Psalms 118:11 (id: 119118011)

11They surrounded me on every side, but in the name of the LORD I cut them off.


## Psalms 118:12 (id: 119118012)

12They swarmed around me like bees, but they were extinguished like burning thorns; in the name of the LORD I cut them off.


## Psalms 118:13 (id: 119118013)

13I was pushed so hard I was falling, but the LORD helped me.


## Psalms 118:14 (id: 119118014)

14The LORD is my strength and my song, and He has become my salvation.


## Psalms 118:15 (id: 119118015)

15Shouts of joy and salvation resound in the tents of the righteous: “The right hand of the LORD performs with valor!


## Psalms 118:16 (id: 119118016)

16The right hand of the LORD is exalted! The right hand of the LORD performs with valor!”


## Psalms 118:17 (id: 119118017)

17I will not die, but I will live and proclaim what the LORD has done.


## Psalms 118:18 (id: 119118018)

18The LORD disciplined me severely, but He has not given me over to death.


## Psalms 118:19 (id: 119118019)

19Open to me the gates of righteousness, that I may enter and give thanks to the LORD.


## Psalms 118:20 (id: 119118020)

20This is the gate of the LORD; the righteous shall enter through it.


## Psalms 118:21 (id: 119118021)

21I will give You thanks, for You have answered me, and You have become my salvation.


## Psalms 118:22 (id: 119118022)

22The stone the builders rejected has become the cornerstone.


## Psalms 118:23 (id: 119118023)

23This is from the LORD, and it is marvelous in our eyes.


## Psalms 118:24 (id: 119118024)

24This is the day that the LORD has made; we will rejoice and be glad in it.


## Psalms 118:25 (id: 119118025)

25O LORD, save us, we pray. We beseech You, O LORD, cause us to prosper!


## Psalms 118:26 (id: 119118026)

26Blessed is he who comes in the name of the LORD. From the house of the LORD we bless you.


## Psalms 118:27 (id: 119118027)

27The LORD is God; He has made His light to shine upon us. Bind the festal sacrifice with cords to the horns of the altar.


## Psalms 118:28 (id: 119118028)

28You are my God, and I will give You thanks. You are my God, and I will exalt You.


## Psalms 118:29 (id: 119118029)

29Give thanks to the LORD, for He is good; His loving devotion endures forever.


## Psalms 119:1 (id: 119119001)

1Blessed are those whose way is blameless, who walk in the Law of the LORD.


## Psalms 119:2 (id: 119119002)

2Blessed are those who keep His testimonies and seek Him with all their heart.


## Psalms 119:3 (id: 119119003)

3They do no iniquity; they walk in His ways.


## Psalms 119:4 (id: 119119004)

4You have ordained Your precepts, that we should keep them diligently.


## Psalms 119:5 (id: 119119005)

5Oh, that my ways were committed to keeping Your statutes!


## Psalms 119:6 (id: 119119006)

6Then I would not be ashamed when I consider all Your commandments.


## Psalms 119:7 (id: 119119007)

7I will praise You with an upright heart when I learn Your righteous judgments.


## Psalms 119:8 (id: 119119008)

8I will keep Your statutes; do not utterly forsake me.


## Psalms 119:9 (id: 119119009)

9How can a young man keep his way pure? By guarding it according to Your word.


## Psalms 119:10 (id: 119119010)

10With all my heart I have sought You; do not let me stray from Your commandments.


## Psalms 119:11 (id: 119119011)

11I have hidden Your word in my heart that I might not sin against You.


## Psalms 119:12 (id: 119119012)

12Blessed are You, O LORD; teach me Your statutes.


## Psalms 119:13 (id: 119119013)

13With my lips I proclaim all the judgments of Your mouth.


## Psalms 119:14 (id: 119119014)

14I rejoice in the way of Your testimonies as much as in all riches.


## Psalms 119:15 (id: 119119015)

15I will meditate on Your precepts and regard Your ways.


## Psalms 119:16 (id: 119119016)

16I will delight in Your statutes; I will not forget Your word.


## Psalms 119:17 (id: 119119017)

17Deal bountifully with Your servant, that I may live and keep Your word.


## Psalms 119:18 (id: 119119018)

18Open my eyes that I may see wondrous things from Your law.


## Psalms 119:19 (id: 119119019)

19I am a stranger on the earth; do not hide Your commandments from me.


## Psalms 119:20 (id: 119119020)

20My soul is consumed with longing for Your judgments at all times.


## Psalms 119:21 (id: 119119021)

21You rebuke the arrogant—the cursed who stray from Your commandments.


## Psalms 119:22 (id: 119119022)

22Remove my scorn and contempt, for I have kept Your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:23 (id: 119119023)

23Though rulers sit and slander me, Your servant meditates on Your statutes.


## Psalms 119:24 (id: 119119024)

24Your testimonies are indeed my delight; they are my counselors.


## Psalms 119:25 (id: 119119025)

25My soul cleaves to the dust; revive me according to Your word.


## Psalms 119:26 (id: 119119026)

26I recounted my ways, and You answered me; teach me Your statutes.


## Psalms 119:27 (id: 119119027)

27Make clear to me the way of Your precepts; then I will meditate on Your wonders.


## Psalms 119:28 (id: 119119028)

28My soul melts with sorrow; strengthen me according to Your word.


## Psalms 119:29 (id: 119119029)

29Remove me from the path of deceit and graciously grant me Your law.


## Psalms 119:30 (id: 119119030)

30I have chosen the way of truth; I have set Your ordinances before me.


## Psalms 119:31 (id: 119119031)

31I cling to Your testimonies, O LORD; let me not be put to shame.


## Psalms 119:32 (id: 119119032)

32I run in the path of Your commandments, for You will enlarge my heart.


## Psalms 119:33 (id: 119119033)

33Teach me, O LORD, the way of Your statutes, and I will keep them to the end.


## Psalms 119:34 (id: 119119034)

34Give me understanding that I may obey Your law, and follow it with all my heart.


## Psalms 119:35 (id: 119119035)

35Direct me in the path of Your commandments, for there I find delight.


## Psalms 119:36 (id: 119119036)

36Turn my heart to Your testimonies and not to covetous gain.


## Psalms 119:37 (id: 119119037)

37Turn my eyes away from worthless things; revive me with Your word.


## Psalms 119:38 (id: 119119038)

38Establish Your word to Your servant, to produce reverence for You.


## Psalms 119:39 (id: 119119039)

39Turn away the disgrace I dread, for Your judgments are good.


## Psalms 119:40 (id: 119119040)

40How I long for Your precepts! Revive me in Your righteousness.


## Psalms 119:41 (id: 119119041)

41May Your loving devotion come to me, O LORD, Your salvation, according to Your promise.


## Psalms 119:42 (id: 119119042)

42Then I can answer him who taunts, for I trust in Your word.


## Psalms 119:43 (id: 119119043)

43Never take Your word of truth from my mouth, for I hope in Your judgments.


## Psalms 119:44 (id: 119119044)

44I will always obey Your law, forever and ever.


## Psalms 119:45 (id: 119119045)

45And I will walk in freedom, for I have sought Your precepts.


## Psalms 119:46 (id: 119119046)

46I will speak of Your testimonies before kings, and I will not be ashamed.


## Psalms 119:47 (id: 119119047)

47I delight in Your commandments because I love them.


## Psalms 119:48 (id: 119119048)

48I lift up my hands to Your commandments, which I love, and I meditate on Your statutes.


## Psalms 119:49 (id: 119119049)

49Remember Your word to Your servant, upon which You have given me hope.


## Psalms 119:50 (id: 119119050)

50This is my comfort in affliction, that Your promise has given me life.


## Psalms 119:51 (id: 119119051)

51The arrogant utterly deride me, but I do not turn from Your law.


## Psalms 119:52 (id: 119119052)

52I remember Your judgments of old, O LORD, and in them I find comfort.


## Psalms 119:53 (id: 119119053)

53Rage has taken hold of me because of the wicked who reject Your law.


## Psalms 119:54 (id: 119119054)

54Your statutes are songs to me in the house of my pilgrimage.


## Psalms 119:55 (id: 119119055)

55In the night, O LORD, I remember Your name, that I may keep Your law.


## Psalms 119:56 (id: 119119056)

56This is my practice, for I obey Your precepts.


## Psalms 119:57 (id: 119119057)

57The LORD is my portion; I have promised to keep Your words.


## Psalms 119:58 (id: 119119058)

58I have sought Your face with all my heart; be gracious to me according to Your promise.


## Psalms 119:59 (id: 119119059)

59I considered my ways and turned my steps to Your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:60 (id: 119119060)

60I hurried without hesitating to keep Your commandments.


## Psalms 119:61 (id: 119119061)

61Though the ropes of the wicked bind me, I do not forget Your law.


## Psalms 119:62 (id: 119119062)

62At midnight I rise to give You thanks for Your righteous judgments.


## Psalms 119:63 (id: 119119063)

63I am a friend to all who fear You, and to those who keep Your precepts.


## Psalms 119:64 (id: 119119064)

64The earth is filled with Your loving devotion, O LORD; teach me Your statutes.


## Psalms 119:65 (id: 119119065)

65You are good to Your servant, O LORD, according to Your word.


## Psalms 119:66 (id: 119119066)

66Teach me good judgment and knowledge, for I believe in Your commandments.


## Psalms 119:67 (id: 119119067)

67Before I was afflicted, I went astray; but now I keep Your word.


## Psalms 119:68 (id: 119119068)

68You are good, and You do what is good; teach me Your statutes.


## Psalms 119:69 (id: 119119069)

69Though the arrogant have smeared me with lies, I keep Your precepts with all my heart.


## Psalms 119:70 (id: 119119070)

70Their hearts are callous and insensitive, but I delight in Your law.


## Psalms 119:71 (id: 119119071)

71It was good for me to be afflicted, that I might learn Your statutes.


## Psalms 119:72 (id: 119119072)

72The law from Your mouth is more precious to me than thousands of pieces of gold and silver.


## Psalms 119:73 (id: 119119073)

73Your hands have made me and fashioned me; give me understanding to learn Your commandments.


## Psalms 119:74 (id: 119119074)

74May those who fear You see me and rejoice, for I have hoped in Your word.


## Psalms 119:75 (id: 119119075)

75I know, O LORD, that Your judgments are righteous, and that in faithfulness You have afflicted me.


## Psalms 119:76 (id: 119119076)

76May Your loving devotion comfort me, I pray, according to Your promise to Your servant.


## Psalms 119:77 (id: 119119077)

77May Your compassion come to me, that I may live, for Your law is my delight.


## Psalms 119:78 (id: 119119078)

78May the arrogant be put to shame for subverting me with a lie; I will meditate on Your precepts.


## Psalms 119:79 (id: 119119079)

79May those who fear You turn to me, those who know Your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:80 (id: 119119080)

80May my heart be blameless in Your statutes, that I may not be put to shame.


## Psalms 119:81 (id: 119119081)

81My soul faints for Your salvation; I wait for Your word.


## Psalms 119:82 (id: 119119082)

82My eyes fail, looking for Your promise; I ask, “When will You comfort me?”


## Psalms 119:83 (id: 119119083)

83Though I am like a wineskin dried up by smoke, I do not forget Your statutes.


## Psalms 119:84 (id: 119119084)

84How many days must Your servant wait? When will You execute judgment on my persecutors?


## Psalms 119:85 (id: 119119085)

85The arrogant have dug pits for me in violation of Your law.


## Psalms 119:86 (id: 119119086)

86All Your commandments are faithful; I am persecuted without cause—help me!


## Psalms 119:87 (id: 119119087)

87They almost wiped me from the earth, but I have not forsaken Your precepts.


## Psalms 119:88 (id: 119119088)

88Revive me according to Your loving devotion, that I may obey the testimony of Your mouth.


## Psalms 119:89 (id: 119119089)

89Your word, O LORD, is everlasting; it is firmly fixed in the heavens.


## Psalms 119:90 (id: 119119090)

90Your faithfulness continues through all generations; You established the earth, and it endures.


## Psalms 119:91 (id: 119119091)

91Your ordinances stand to this day, for all things are servants to You.


## Psalms 119:92 (id: 119119092)

92If Your law had not been my delight, then I would have perished in my affliction.


## Psalms 119:93 (id: 119119093)

93I will never forget Your precepts, for by them You have revived me.


## Psalms 119:94 (id: 119119094)

94I am Yours; save me, for I have sought Your precepts.


## Psalms 119:95 (id: 119119095)

95The wicked wait to destroy me, but I will ponder Your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:96 (id: 119119096)

96I have seen a limit to all perfection, but Your commandment is without limit.


## Psalms 119:97 (id: 119119097)

97Oh, how I love Your law! All day long it is my meditation.


## Psalms 119:98 (id: 119119098)

98Your commandments make me wiser than my enemies, for they are always with me.


## Psalms 119:99 (id: 119119099)

99I have more insight than all my teachers, for Your testimonies are my meditation.


## Psalms 119:100 (id: 119119100)

100I discern more than the elders, for I obey Your precepts.


## Psalms 119:101 (id: 119119101)

101I have kept my feet from every evil path, that I may keep Your word.


## Psalms 119:102 (id: 119119102)

102I have not departed from Your ordinances, for You Yourself have taught me.


## Psalms 119:103 (id: 119119103)

103How sweet are Your words to my taste—sweeter than honey in my mouth!


## Psalms 119:104 (id: 119119104)

104I gain understanding from Your precepts; therefore I hate every false way.


## Psalms 119:105 (id: 119119105)

105Your word is a lamp to my feet and a light to my path.


## Psalms 119:106 (id: 119119106)

106I have sworn and confirmed that I will keep Your righteous judgments.


## Psalms 119:107 (id: 119119107)

107I am severely afflicted, O LORD; revive me through Your word.

109I constantly take my life in my hands, yet I do not forget Your law.

120My flesh trembles in awe of You; I stand in fear of Your judgments.

126It is time for the LORD to act, for they have broken Your law.


## Psalms 119:127 (id: 119119127)

127Therefore I love Your commandments more than gold, even the purest gold.

129Wonderful are Your testimonies; therefore I obey them.

130The unfolding of Your words gives light; it informs the simple.

134Redeem me from the oppression of man, that I may keep Your precepts.

135Make Your face shine upon Your servant, and teach me Your statutes.

136My eyes shed streams of tears because Your law is not obeyed.

137Righteous are You, O LORD, and upright are Your judgments.


## Psalms 119:138 (id: 119119138)

138The testimonies You have laid down are righteous and altogether faithful.

139My zeal has consumed me because my foes forget Your words.

140Your promise is completely pure; therefore Your servant loves it.

145I call with all my heart; answer me, O LORD! I will obey Your statutes.

146I call to You; save me, that I may keep Your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:147 (id: 119119147)

147I rise before dawn and cry for help; in Your word I have put my hope.

148My eyes anticipate the watches of night, that I may meditate on Your word.


## Psalms 119:149 (id: 119119149)

149Hear my voice, O LORD, according to Your loving devotion; give me life according to Your justice.


## Psalms 119:150 (id: 119119150)

150Those who follow after wickedness draw near; they are far from Your law.


## Psalms 119:151 (id: 119119151)

151You are near, O LORD, and all Your commandments are true.


## Psalms 119:152 (id: 119119152)

152Long ago I learned from Your testimonies that You have established them forever.


## Psalms 119:153 (id: 119119153)

## Psalms 119:155 (id: 119119155)

155Salvation is far from the wicked because they do not seek Your statutes.

156Great are Your mercies, O LORD; revive me according to Your ordinances.


## Psalms 119:157 (id: 119119157)

157Though my persecutors and foes are many, I have not turned from Your testimonies.


## Psalms 119:158 (id: 119119158)

158I look on the faithless with loathing because they do not keep Your word.


## Psalms 119:159 (id: 119119159)

159Consider how I love Your precepts, O LORD; give me life according to Your loving devotion.


## Psalms 119:160 (id: 119119160)

160The entirety of Your word is truth, and all Your righteous judgments endure forever.

161Rulers persecute me without cause, but my heart fears only Your word.

162I rejoice in Your promise like one who finds great spoil.

163I hate and abhor falsehood, but Your law I love.

164Seven times a day I praise You for Your righteous judgments.

165Abundant peace belongs to those who love Your law; nothing can make them stumble.

## Psalms 119:167 (id: 119119167)

167I obey Your testimonies and love them greatly.

172My tongue sings of Your word, for all Your commandments are righteous.

## Psalms 119:174 (id: 119119174)

174I long for Your salvation, O LORD, and Your law is my delight.

175Let me live to praise You; may Your judgments sustain me.

176I have strayed like a lost sheep; seek Your servant, for I have not forgotten Your commandments.


## Psalms 120:0 (id: 119120000)

0A song of ascents.


## Psalms 120:1 (id: 119120001)

1In my distress I cried to the LORD, and He answered me.


## Psalms 120:2 (id: 119120002)

2Deliver my soul, O LORD, from lying lips and a deceitful tongue.


## Psalms 120:3 (id: 119120003)

3What will He do to you, and what will be added to you, O deceitful tongue?


## Psalms 120:4 (id: 119120004)

4Sharp arrows will come from the warrior, with burning coals of the broom tree!


## Psalms 120:5 (id: 119120005)

5Woe to me that I dwell in Meshech, that I live among the tents of Kedar!


## Psalms 120:6 (id: 119120006)

6Too long have I dwelt among those who hate peace.


## Psalms 120:7 (id: 119120007)

7I am in favor of peace; but when I speak, they want war.


## Psalms 121:0 (id: 119121000)

0A song of ascents.


## Psalms 121:1 (id: 119121001)

1I lift up my eyes to the hills. From where does my help come?


## Psalms 121:2 (id: 119121002)

2My help comes from the LORD, the Maker of heaven and earth.


## Psalms 121:3 (id: 119121003)

3He will not allow your foot to slip; your Protector will not slumber.


## Psalms 121:4 (id: 119121004)

4Behold, the Protector of Israel will neither slumber nor sleep.


## Psalms 121:5 (id: 119121005)

5The LORD is your keeper; the LORD is the shade on your right hand.


## Psalms 121:6 (id: 119121006)

6The sun will not strike you by day, nor the moon by night.


## Psalms 121:7 (id: 119121007)

7The LORD will guard you from all evil; He will preserve your soul.


## Psalms 121:8 (id: 119121008)

8The LORD will watch over your coming and going, both now and forevermore.


## Psalms 122:0 (id: 119122000)

0A song of ascents. Of David.


## Psalms 122:1 (id: 119122001)

1I was glad when they said to me, “Let us go to the house of the LORD.”


## Psalms 122:2 (id: 119122002)

2Our feet are standing in your gates, O Jerusalem.


## Psalms 122:3 (id: 119122003)

3Jerusalem is built up as a city united together,


## Psalms 122:4 (id: 119122004)

4where the tribes go up, the tribes of the LORD, as a testimony for Israel, to give thanks to the name of the LORD.


## Psalms 122:5 (id: 119122005)

5For there the thrones of judgment stand, the thrones of the house of David.


## Psalms 122:6 (id: 119122006)

6Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: “May those who love you prosper.


## Psalms 122:7 (id: 119122007)

7May there be peace within your walls, and prosperity inside your fortresses.”


## Psalms 122:8 (id: 119122008)

8For the sake of my brothers and friends, I will say, “Peace be within you.”


## Psalms 122:9 (id: 119122009)

9For the sake of the house of the LORD our God, I will seek your prosperity.


## Psalms 123:0 (id: 119123000)

0A song of ascents.


## Psalms 123:1 (id: 119123001)

1I lift up my eyes to You, the One enthroned in heaven.


## Psalms 123:2 (id: 119123002)

2As the eyes of servants look to the hand of their master, as the eyes of a maidservant look to the hand of her mistress, so our eyes are on the LORD our God until He shows us mercy.


## Psalms 123:3 (id: 119123003)

3Have mercy on us, O LORD, have mercy, for we have endured much contempt.


## Psalms 123:4 (id: 119123004)

4We have endured much scorn from the arrogant, much contempt from the proud.


## Psalms 124:0 (id: 119124000)

0A song of ascents. Of David.


## Psalms 124:1 (id: 119124001)

1If the LORD had not been on our side—let Israel now declare—


## Psalms 124:2 (id: 119124002)

2if the LORD had not been on our side when men attacked us,


## Psalms 124:3 (id: 119124003)

3when their anger flared against us, then they would have swallowed us alive,


## Psalms 124:4 (id: 119124004)

4then the floods would have engulfed us, then the torrent would have overwhelmed us,


## Psalms 124:5 (id: 119124005)

5then the raging waters would have swept us away.


## Psalms 124:6 (id: 119124006)

6Blessed be the LORD, who has not given us as prey to their teeth.


## Psalms 124:7 (id: 119124007)

7We have escaped like a bird from the snare of the fowler; the net is torn, and we have slipped away.


## Psalms 124:8 (id: 119124008)

8Our help is in the name of the LORD, the Maker of heaven and earth.


## Psalms 125:0 (id: 119125000)

0A song of ascents.


## Psalms 125:1 (id: 119125001)

1Those who trust in the LORD are like Mount Zion. It cannot be moved; it abides forever.


## Psalms 125:2 (id: 119125002)

2As the mountains surround Jerusalem, so the LORD surrounds His people, both now and forevermore.


## Psalms 125:3 (id: 119125003)

3For the scepter of the wicked will not rest upon the land allotted to the righteous, so that the righteous will not put forth their hands to injustice.


## Psalms 125:4 (id: 119125004)

4Do good, O LORD, to those who are good, and to the upright in heart.


## Psalms 125:5 (id: 119125005)

5But those who turn to crooked ways the LORD will banish with the evildoers. Peace be upon Israel.


## Psalms 126:0 (id: 119126000)

0A song of ascents.


## Psalms 126:1 (id: 119126001)

1When the LORD restored the captives of Zion, we were like dreamers.


## Psalms 126:2 (id: 119126002)

2Then our mouths were filled with laughter, our tongues with shouts of joy. Then it was said among the nations, “The LORD has done great things for them.”


## Psalms 126:3 (id: 119126003)

3The LORD has done great things for us; we are filled with joy.


## Psalms 126:4 (id: 119126004)

4Restore our captives, O LORD, like streams in the Negev.


## Psalms 126:5 (id: 119126005)

5Those who sow in tears will reap with shouts of joy.


## Psalms 126:6 (id: 119126006)

6He who goes out weeping, bearing a trail of seed, will surely return with shouts of joy, carrying sheaves of grain.


## Psalms 127:0 (id: 119127000)

0A song of ascents. Of Solomon.


## Psalms 127:1 (id: 119127001)

1Unless the LORD builds the house, its builders labor in vain; unless the LORD protects the city, its watchmen stand guard in vain.


## Psalms 127:2 (id: 119127002)

2In vain you rise early and stay up late, toiling for bread to eat—for He gives sleep to His beloved.


## Psalms 127:3 (id: 119127003)

3Children are indeed a heritage from the LORD, and the fruit of the womb is His reward.


## Psalms 127:4 (id: 119127004)

4Like arrows in the hand of a warrior, so are children born in one’s youth.


## Psalms 127:5 (id: 119127005)

5Blessed is the man whose quiver is full of them. He will not be put to shame when he confronts the enemies at the gate.


## Psalms 128:0 (id: 119128000)

0A song of ascents.


## Psalms 128:1 (id: 119128001)

1Blessed are all who fear the LORD, who walk in His ways!


## Psalms 128:2 (id: 119128002)

2For when you eat the fruit of your labor, blessings and prosperity will be yours.


## Psalms 128:3 (id: 119128003)

3Your wife will be like a fruitful vine flourishing within your house, your sons like olive shoots sitting around your table.


## Psalms 128:4 (id: 119128004)

4In this way indeed shall blessing come to the man who fears the LORD.


## Psalms 128:5 (id: 119128005)

5May the LORD bless you from Zion, that you may see the prosperity of Jerusalem all the days of your life,


## Psalms 128:6 (id: 119128006)

6that you may see your children’s children. Peace be upon Israel!


## Psalms 129:0 (id: 119129000)

0A song of ascents.


## Psalms 129:1 (id: 119129001)

1Many a time they have persecuted me from my youth—let Israel now declare—


## Psalms 129:2 (id: 119129002)

2many a time they have persecuted me from my youth, but they have not prevailed against me.


## Psalms 129:3 (id: 119129003)

3The plowmen plowed over my back; they made their furrows long.


## Psalms 129:4 (id: 119129004)

4The LORD is righteous; He has cut me from the cords of the wicked.


## Psalms 129:5 (id: 119129005)

5May all who hate Zion be turned back in shame.


## Psalms 129:6 (id: 119129006)

6May they be like grass on the rooftops, which withers before it can grow,


## Psalms 129:7 (id: 119129007)

7unable to fill the hands of the reaper, or the arms of the binder of sheaves.


## Psalms 129:8 (id: 119129008)

8May none who pass by say to them, “The blessing of the LORD be on you; we bless you in the name of the LORD.”

## Psalms 132:12 (id: 119132012)

## Psalms 132:14 (id: 119132014)

## Psalms 132:15 (id: 119132015)

## Psalms 132:16 (id: 119132016)

## Psalms 132:17 (id: 119132017)

## Psalms 132:18 (id: 119132018)

## Psalms 135:7 (id: 119135007)

## Psalms 135:8 (id: 119135008)

## Psalms 135:9 (id: 119135009)

## Psalms 135:11 (id: 119135011)

## Psalms 135:13 (id: 119135013)

## Psalms 135:14 (id: 119135014)

## Psalms 135:17 (id: 119135017)

15but swept Pharaoh and his army into the Red Sea. His loving devotion endures forever.
