## Psalms 139:0 (id: 119139000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 139:1 (id: 119139001)

1O LORD, You have searched me and known me.


## Psalms 139:2 (id: 119139002)

2You know when I sit and when I rise; You understand my thoughts from afar.


## Psalms 139:3 (id: 119139003)

3You search out my path and my lying down; You are aware of all my ways.


## Psalms 139:4 (id: 119139004)

4Even before a word is on my tongue, You know all about it, O LORD.


## Psalms 139:5 (id: 119139005)

5You hem me in behind and before; You have laid Your hand upon me.


## Psalms 139:6 (id: 119139006)

6Such knowledge is too wonderful for me, too lofty for me to attain.


## Psalms 139:7 (id: 119139007)

7Where can I go to escape Your Spirit? Where can I flee from Your presence?


## Psalms 139:8 (id: 119139008)

8If I ascend to the heavens, You are there; if I make my bed in Sheol, You are there.


## Psalms 139:9 (id: 119139009)

9If I rise on the wings of the dawn, if I settle by the farthest sea,


## Psalms 139:10 (id: 119139010)

10even there Your hand will guide me; Your right hand will hold me fast.


## Psalms 139:11 (id: 119139011)

11If I say, “Surely the darkness will hide me, and the light become night around me”—


## Psalms 139:12 (id: 119139012)

12even the darkness is not dark to You, but the night shines like the day, for darkness is as light to You.


## Psalms 139:13 (id: 119139013)

13For You formed my inmost being; You knit me together in my mother’s womb.


## Psalms 139:14 (id: 119139014)

14I praise You, for I am fearfully and wonderfully made. Marvelous are Your works, and I know this very well.


## Psalms 139:15 (id: 119139015)

15My frame was not hidden from You when I was made in secret, when I was woven together in the depths of the earth.


## Psalms 139:16 (id: 119139016)

16Your eyes saw my unformed body; all my days were written in Your book and ordained for me before one of them came to be.


## Psalms 139:17 (id: 119139017)

17How precious to me are Your thoughts, O God, how vast is their sum!


## Psalms 139:18 (id: 119139018)

18If I were to count them, they would outnumber the grains of sand; and when I awake, I am still with You.


## Psalms 139:19 (id: 119139019)

19O God, that You would slay the wicked—away from me, you bloodthirsty men—


## Psalms 139:20 (id: 119139020)

20who speak of You deceitfully; Your enemies take Your name in vain.


## Psalms 139:21 (id: 119139021)

21Do I not hate those who hate You, O LORD, and detest those who rise against You?


## Psalms 139:22 (id: 119139022)

22I hate them with perfect hatred; I count them as my enemies.


## Psalms 139:23 (id: 119139023)

23Search me, O God, and know my heart; test me and know my concerns.


## Psalms 139:24 (id: 119139024)

24See if there is any offensive way in me; lead me in the way everlasting.


## Psalms 140:0 (id: 119140000)

0For the choirmaster. A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 140:1 (id: 119140001)

1Rescue me, O LORD, from evil men. Protect me from men of violence,


## Psalms 140:2 (id: 119140002)

2who devise evil in their hearts and stir up war all day long.


## Psalms 140:3 (id: 119140003)

3They sharpen their tongues like snakes; the venom of vipers is on their lips. Selah


## Psalms 140:4 (id: 119140004)

4Guard me, O LORD, from the hands of the wicked. Keep me safe from men of violence who scheme to make me stumble.


## Psalms 140:5 (id: 119140005)

5The proud hide a snare for me; the cords of their net are spread along the path, and lures are set out for me. Selah


## Psalms 140:6 (id: 119140006)

6I say to the LORD, “You are my God.” Hear, O LORD, my cry for help.


## Psalms 140:7 (id: 119140007)

7O GOD the Lord, the strength of my salvation, You shield my head in the day of battle.


## Psalms 140:8 (id: 119140008)

8Grant not, O LORD, the desires of the wicked; do not promote their evil plans, lest they be exalted. Selah


## Psalms 140:9 (id: 119140009)

9May the heads of those who surround me be covered in the trouble their lips have caused.


## Psalms 140:10 (id: 119140010)

10May burning coals fall on them; may they be thrown into the fire, into the miry pits, never to rise again.


## Psalms 140:11 (id: 119140011)

11May no slanderer be established in the land; may calamity hunt down the man of violence.


## Psalms 140:12 (id: 119140012)

12I know that the LORD upholds justice for the poor and defends the cause of the needy.


## Psalms 140:13 (id: 119140013)

13Surely the righteous will praise Your name; the upright will dwell in Your presence.


## Psalms 141:0 (id: 119141000)

0A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 141:1 (id: 119141001)

1I call upon You, O LORD; come quickly to me. Hear my voice when I call to You.


## Psalms 141:2 (id: 119141002)

2May my prayer be set before You like incense; my uplifted hands, like the evening offering.


## Psalms 141:3 (id: 119141003)

3Set a guard, O LORD, over my mouth; keep watch at the door of my lips.


## Psalms 141:4 (id: 119141004)

4Do not let my heart be drawn to any evil thing or take part in works of wickedness with men who do iniquity; let me not feast on their delicacies.


## Psalms 141:5 (id: 119141005)

5Let the righteous man strike me; let his rebuke be an act of loving devotion. It is oil for my head; let me not refuse it. For my prayer is ever against the deeds of the wicked.


## Psalms 141:6 (id: 119141006)

6When their rulers are thrown down from the cliffs, the people will listen to my words, for they are pleasant.


## Psalms 141:7 (id: 119141007)

7As when one plows and breaks up the soil, so our bones have been scattered at the mouth of Sheol.


## Psalms 141:8 (id: 119141008)

8But my eyes are fixed on You, O GOD the Lord. In You I seek refuge; do not leave my soul defenseless.


## Psalms 141:9 (id: 119141009)

9Keep me from the snares they have laid for me, and from the lures of evildoers.


## Psalms 141:10 (id: 119141010)

10Let the wicked fall into their own nets, while I pass by in safety.


## Psalms 142:0 (id: 119142000)

0A Maskil of David, when he was in the cave. A prayer.


## Psalms 142:1 (id: 119142001)

1I cry aloud to the LORD; I lift my voice to the LORD for mercy.


## Psalms 142:2 (id: 119142002)

2I pour out my complaint before Him; I reveal my trouble to Him.


## Psalms 142:3 (id: 119142003)

3Although my spirit grows faint within me, You know my way. Along the path I travel they have hidden a snare for me.


## Psalms 142:4 (id: 119142004)

4Look to my right and see; no one attends to me. There is no refuge for me; no one cares for my soul.


## Psalms 142:5 (id: 119142005)

5I cry to You, O LORD: “You are my refuge, my portion in the land of the living.”


## Psalms 142:6 (id: 119142006)

6Listen to my cry, for I am brought quite low. Rescue me from my pursuers, for they are too strong for me.


## Psalms 142:7 (id: 119142007)

7Free my soul from prison, that I may praise Your name. The righteous will gather around me because of Your goodness to me.


## Psalms 143:0 (id: 119143000)

0A Psalm of David.


## Psalms 143:1 (id: 119143001)

1O LORD, hear my prayer. In Your faithfulness, give ear to my plea; in Your righteousness, answer me.


## Psalms 143:2 (id: 119143002)

2Do not bring Your servant into judgment, for no one alive is righteous before You.


## Psalms 143:3 (id: 119143003)

3For the enemy has pursued my soul, crushing my life to the ground, making me dwell in darkness like those long since dead.


## Psalms 143:4 (id: 119143004)

4My spirit grows faint within me; my heart is dismayed inside me.


## Psalms 143:5 (id: 119143005)

5I remember the days of old; I meditate on all Your works; I consider the work of Your hands.


## Psalms 143:6 (id: 119143006)

6I stretch out my hands to You; my soul thirsts for You like a parched land. Selah


## Psalms 143:7 (id: 119143007)

7Answer me quickly, O LORD; my spirit fails. Do not hide Your face from me, or I will be like those who descend to the Pit.


## Psalms 143:8 (id: 119143008)

8Let me hear Your loving devotion in the morning, for I have put my trust in You. Teach me the way I should walk, for to You I lift up my soul.


## Psalms 143:9 (id: 119143009)

9Deliver me from my enemies, O LORD; I flee to You for refuge.


## Psalms 143:10 (id: 119143010)

10Teach me to do Your will, for You are my God. May Your good Spirit lead me on level ground.


## Psalms 143:11 (id: 119143011)

11For the sake of Your name, O LORD, revive me. In Your righteousness, bring my soul out of trouble.


## Psalms 143:12 (id: 119143012)

12And in Your loving devotion, cut off my enemies. Destroy all who afflict me, for I am Your servant.


## Psalms 144:0 (id: 119144000)

0Of David.


## Psalms 144:1 (id: 119144001)

1Blessed be the LORD, my Rock, who trains my hands for war, my fingers for battle.


## Psalms 144:2 (id: 119144002)

2He is my steadfast love and my fortress, my stronghold and my deliverer. He is my shield, in whom I take refuge, who subdues peoples under me.


## Psalms 144:3 (id: 119144003)

3O LORD, what is man, that You regard him, the son of man that You think of him?


## Psalms 144:4 (id: 119144004)

4Man is like a breath; his days are like a passing shadow.


## Psalms 144:5 (id: 119144005)

5Part Your heavens, O LORD, and come down; touch the mountains, that they may smoke.


## Psalms 144:6 (id: 119144006)

6Flash forth Your lightning and scatter them; shoot Your arrows and rout them.


## Psalms 144:7 (id: 119144007)

7Reach down from on high; set me free and rescue me from the deep waters, from the grasp of foreigners,


## Psalms 144:8 (id: 119144008)

8whose mouths speak falsehood, whose right hands are deceitful.


## Psalms 144:9 (id: 119144009)

9I will sing to You a new song, O God; on a harp of ten strings I will make music to You—


## Psalms 144:10 (id: 119144010)

10to Him who gives victory to kings, who frees His servant David from the deadly sword.


## Psalms 144:11 (id: 119144011)

11Set me free and rescue me from the grasp of foreigners, whose mouths speak falsehood, whose right hands are deceitful.


## Psalms 144:12 (id: 119144012)

12Then our sons will be like plants nurtured in their youth, our daughters like corner pillars carved to adorn a palace.


## Psalms 144:13 (id: 119144013)

13Our storehouses will be full, supplying all manner of produce; our flocks will bring forth thousands, tens of thousands in our fields.


## Psalms 144:14 (id: 119144014)

14Our oxen will bear great loads. There will be no breach in the walls, no going into captivity, and no cry of lament in our streets.


## Psalms 144:15 (id: 119144015)

15Blessed are the people of whom this is so; blessed are the people whose God is the LORD.


## Psalms 145:0 (id: 119145000)

0A Psalm of praise. Of David.


## Psalms 145:1 (id: 119145001)

1I will exalt You, my God and King; I will bless Your name forever and ever.


## Psalms 145:2 (id: 119145002)

2Every day I will bless You, and I will praise Your name forever and ever.


## Psalms 145:3 (id: 119145003)

3Great is the LORD and greatly to be praised; His greatness is unsearchable.


## Psalms 145:4 (id: 119145004)

4One generation will commend Your works to the next, and will proclaim Your mighty acts—


## Psalms 145:5 (id: 119145005)

5the glorious splendor of Your majesty. And I will meditate on Your wondrous works.


## Psalms 145:6 (id: 119145006)

6They will proclaim the power of Your awesome deeds, and I will declare Your greatness.


## Psalms 145:7 (id: 119145007)

7They will extol the fame of Your abundant goodness and sing joyfully of Your righteousness.


## Psalms 145:8 (id: 119145008)

8The LORD is gracious and compassionate, slow to anger and abounding in loving devotion.


## Psalms 145:9 (id: 119145009)

9The LORD is good to all; His compassion rests on all He has made.


## Psalms 145:10 (id: 119145010)

10All You have made will give You thanks, O LORD, and Your saints will bless You.


## Psalms 145:11 (id: 119145011)

11They will tell of the glory of Your kingdom and speak of Your might,


## Psalms 145:12 (id: 119145012)

12to make known to men Your mighty acts and the glorious splendor of Your kingdom.


## Psalms 145:13 (id: 119145013)

13Your kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and Your dominion endures through all generations. The LORD is faithful in all His words and kind in all His actions.


## Psalms 145:14 (id: 119145014)

14The LORD upholds all who fall and lifts up all who are bowed down.


## Psalms 145:15 (id: 119145015)

15The eyes of all look to You, and You give them their food in season.


## Psalms 145:16 (id: 119145016)

16You open Your hand and satisfy the desire of every living thing.


## Psalms 145:17 (id: 119145017)

17The LORD is righteous in all His ways and kind in all His deeds.


## Psalms 145:18 (id: 119145018)

18The LORD is near to all who call on Him, to all who call out to Him in truth.


## Psalms 145:19 (id: 119145019)

19He fulfills the desires of those who fear Him; He hears their cry and saves them.


## Psalms 145:20 (id: 119145020)

20The LORD preserves all who love Him, but all the wicked He will destroy.


## Psalms 145:21 (id: 119145021)

21My mouth will declare the praise of the LORD; let every creature bless His holy name forever and ever.


## Psalms 146:1 (id: 119146001)

1Hallelujah! Praise the LORD, O my soul.


## Psalms 146:2 (id: 119146002)

2I will praise the LORD all my life; I will sing praises to my God while I have my being.


## Psalms 146:3 (id: 119146003)

3Put not your trust in princes, in mortal man, who cannot save.


## Psalms 146:4 (id: 119146004)

4When his spirit departs, he returns to the ground; on that very day his plans perish.


## Psalms 146:5 (id: 119146005)

5Blessed is he whose help is the God of Jacob, whose hope is in the LORD his God,


## Psalms 146:6 (id: 119146006)

6the Maker of heaven and earth, the sea, and everything in them. He remains faithful forever.


## Psalms 146:7 (id: 119146007)

7He executes justice for the oppressed and gives food to the hungry. The LORD sets the prisoners free,


## Psalms 146:8 (id: 119146008)

8the LORD opens the eyes of the blind, the LORD lifts those who are weighed down, the LORD loves the righteous.


## Psalms 146:9 (id: 119146009)

9The LORD protects foreigners; He sustains the fatherless and the widow, but the ways of the wicked He frustrates.


## Psalms 146:10 (id: 119146010)

10The LORD reigns forever, your God, O Zion, for all generations. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 147:1 (id: 119147001)

1Hallelujah! How good it is to sing praises to our God, how pleasant and lovely to praise Him!


## Psalms 147:2 (id: 119147002)

2The LORD builds up Jerusalem; He gathers the exiles of Israel.


## Psalms 147:3 (id: 119147003)

3He heals the brokenhearted and binds up their wounds.


## Psalms 147:4 (id: 119147004)

4He determines the number of the stars; He calls them each by name.


## Psalms 147:5 (id: 119147005)

5Great is our Lord, and mighty in power; His understanding has no limit.


## Psalms 147:6 (id: 119147006)

6The LORD sustains the humble, but casts the wicked to the ground.


## Psalms 147:7 (id: 119147007)

7Sing to the LORD with thanksgiving; make music on the harp to our God,


## Psalms 147:8 (id: 119147008)

8who covers the sky with clouds, who prepares rain for the earth, who makes grass to grow on the hills.


## Psalms 147:9 (id: 119147009)

9He provides food for the animals, and for the young ravens when they call.


## Psalms 147:10 (id: 119147010)

10He does not delight in the strength of the horse; He takes no pleasure in the legs of a man.


## Psalms 147:11 (id: 119147011)

11The LORD is pleased with those who fear Him, who hope in His loving devotion.


## Psalms 147:12 (id: 119147012)

12Exalt the LORD, O Jerusalem; praise your God, O Zion!


## Psalms 147:13 (id: 119147013)

13For He strengthens the bars of your gates and blesses the children within you.


## Psalms 147:14 (id: 119147014)

14He makes peace at your borders; He fills you with the finest wheat.


## Psalms 147:15 (id: 119147015)

15He sends forth His command to the earth; His word runs swiftly.


## Psalms 147:16 (id: 119147016)

16He spreads the snow like wool; He scatters the frost like ashes;


## Psalms 147:17 (id: 119147017)

17He casts forth His hail like pebbles. Who can withstand His icy blast?


## Psalms 147:18 (id: 119147018)

18He sends forth His word and melts them; He unleashes His winds, and the waters flow.


## Psalms 147:19 (id: 119147019)

19He declares His word to Jacob, His statutes and judgments to Israel.


## Psalms 147:20 (id: 119147020)

20He has done this for no other nation; they do not know His judgments. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 148:1 (id: 119148001)

1Hallelujah! Praise the LORD from the heavens; praise Him in the highest places.


## Psalms 148:2 (id: 119148002)

2Praise Him, all His angels; praise Him, all His heavenly hosts.


## Psalms 148:3 (id: 119148003)

3Praise Him, O sun and moon; praise Him, all you shining stars.


## Psalms 148:4 (id: 119148004)

4Praise Him, O highest heavens, and you waters above the skies.


## Psalms 148:5 (id: 119148005)

5Let them praise the name of the LORD, for He gave the command and they were created.


## Psalms 148:6 (id: 119148006)

6He established them forever and ever; He issued a decree that will never pass away.


## Psalms 148:7 (id: 119148007)

7Praise the LORD from the earth, all great sea creatures and ocean depths,


## Psalms 148:8 (id: 119148008)

8lightning and hail, snow and clouds, powerful wind fulfilling His word,


## Psalms 148:9 (id: 119148009)

9mountains and all hills, fruit trees and all cedars,


## Psalms 148:10 (id: 119148010)

10wild animals and all cattle, crawling creatures and flying birds,


## Psalms 148:11 (id: 119148011)

11kings of the earth and all peoples, princes and all rulers of the earth,


## Psalms 148:12 (id: 119148012)

12young men and maidens, old and young together.


## Psalms 148:13 (id: 119148013)

13Let them praise the name of the LORD, for His name alone is exalted; His splendor is above the earth and the heavens.


## Psalms 148:14 (id: 119148014)

14He has raised up a horn for His people, the praise of all His saints, of Israel, a people near to Him. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 149:1 (id: 119149001)

1Hallelujah! Sing to the LORD a new song—His praise in the assembly of the godly.


## Psalms 149:2 (id: 119149002)

2Let Israel rejoice in their Maker; let the children of Zion rejoice in their King.


## Psalms 149:3 (id: 119149003)

3Let them praise His name with dancing, and make music to Him with tambourine and harp.


## Psalms 149:4 (id: 119149004)

4For the LORD takes pleasure in His people; He adorns the afflicted with salvation.


## Psalms 149:5 (id: 119149005)

5Let the saints exult in glory; let them shout for joy upon their beds.


## Psalms 149:6 (id: 119149006)

6May the high praises of God be in their mouths, and a double\-edged sword in their hands,


## Psalms 149:7 (id: 119149007)

7to inflict vengeance on the nations and punishment on the peoples,


## Psalms 149:8 (id: 119149008)

8to bind their kings with chains and their nobles with shackles of iron,


## Psalms 149:9 (id: 119149009)

9to execute the judgment written against them. This honor is for all His saints. Hallelujah!


## Psalms 150:1 (id: 119150001)

1Hallelujah! Praise God in His sanctuary. Praise Him in His mighty heavens.


## Psalms 150:2 (id: 119150002)

2Praise Him for His mighty acts; praise Him for His excellent greatness.


## Psalms 150:3 (id: 119150003)

3Praise Him with the sound of the horn; praise Him with the harp and lyre.


## Psalms 150:4 (id: 119150004)

4Praise Him with tambourine and dancing; praise Him with strings and flute.


## Psalms 150:5 (id: 119150005)

5Praise Him with clashing cymbals; praise Him with resounding cymbals.


## Psalms 150:6 (id: 119150006)

6Let everything that has breath praise the LORD! Hallelujah!
